<!-- weld.swarm -- Page
     A polished multi-agent app built on the Weld suite: decompose a goal, dispatch
     parallel worker agents (each a weld.crew ReAct loop), watch them reason live, and
     synthesize one answer. Works fully offline with a scripted reasoner; lights up with
     real AI, web.fetch, the cross-tab bus, and cross-device storage when the Weld
     Companion is installed. Imports weld.skybridge, weld.sync, weld.crew, weld.swarm,
     weld.fetch. -->

            <div class="row">

            </div>
            <div class="row">
              <label class="fld">parallel <span class="val" id="conc-v">2</span></label>

            </div>

            <button class="btn" id="import" title="Load settings + inputs (and view results) from a .json snapshot">import</button>

        <div class="hd">aggregate <span class="tag" id="agg-tag"></span></div>

          <div class="syn" id="agg-syn"></div>
          <div id="agg-body"></div>
          <div style="display:flex; gap:8px; margin-top:12px; flex-wrap:wrap;">
            <button class="btn" id="agg-copy" style="flex:0 0 auto; max-width:140px;">copy</button>
            <button class="btn" id="agg-export" style="flex:0 0 auto; max-width:160px;">export .md</button>
            <button class="btn" id="agg-export-json" style="flex:0 0 auto; max-width:150px;">export .json</button>

  <div class="modal-card">

<script>
  // ===== Inlined Weld plugins (self-contained: no DSL import of weld generators, so no
  //       stale-import or fetch failures). Each block is a plugin's $output body wrapped
  //       in an IIFE; it stashes window.weld.<name> as a side effect. Only the built-in
  //       ai-text and text-to-image plugins remain DSL imports (always available).
  //       Regenerated from the weld-*-dsl.txt sources; re-inline when those change. =====
  window.aiTextPlugin = (function(){ var r=(typeof root!=='undefined'&&root)?root:(window.root||null); return r&&r.aiTextPlugin; })();
  window.t2iSource    = (function(){ var r=(typeof root!=='undefined'&&root)?root:(window.root||null); return r&&r.textToImagePlugin; })();
  // ---- weld-persist ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.persist) return window.weld.persist;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.persist: Collection-based CRUD over IndexedDB.
  // One database, one object store, logical collections via a compound
  // key of (collection + id). No schema versioning needed when collections
  // are added (they're just key prefixes). No Dexie dependency.
  //
  // Usage:
  //   var db = weld.persist.open('my-app');
  //   var chars = db.collection('characters');
  //   await chars.put({ id: 'c1', name: 'Alice' });
  //   var alice = await chars.get('c1');
  //   var all = await chars.getAll();
  //   await chars.delete('c1');
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var STORE_NAME = 'records';
  var DB_VERSION = 1;

  // Cache of opened databases: dbName -> Promise<IDBDatabase>
  var dbCache = {};

  function openDatabase(dbName) {
    if (dbCache[dbName]) return dbCache[dbName];
    dbCache[dbName] = new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      var request = indexedDB.open(dbName, DB_VERSION);
      request.onupgradeneeded = function(e) {
        var db = e.target.result;
        if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(STORE_NAME)) {
          var store = db.createObjectStore(STORE_NAME, { keyPath: ['_col', '_id'] });
          store.createIndex('by_col', '_col', { unique: false });
        }
      };
      request.onsuccess = function(e) { resolve(e.target.result); };
      request.onerror = function(e) {
        delete dbCache[dbName];
        reject(new Error('weld.persist: failed to open "' + dbName + '": ' + (e.target.error || 'unknown')));
      };
    });
    return dbCache[dbName];
  }

  function uid() {
    return Date.now().toString(36) + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Collection handle
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function makeCollection(dbName, colName) {
    function getStore(mode) {
      return openDatabase(dbName).then(function(db) {
        var tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, mode);
        return tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME);
      });
    }

    function wrapRequest(req) {
      return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
        req.onsuccess = function() { resolve(req.result); };
        req.onerror = function() { reject(req.error); };
      });
    }

    // Put: upsert a record. If record has no .id, one is generated.
    function put(record) {
      if (!record || typeof record !== 'object') {
        return Promise.reject(new Error('persist.put: record must be an object'));
      }
      var rec = Object.assign({}, record);
      if (rec.id == null) rec.id = uid();
      rec._col = colName;
      rec._id = String(rec.id);
      return getStore('readwrite').then(function(store) {
        return wrapRequest(store.put(rec));
      }).then(function() {
        return rec.id;
      });
    }

    // Put many records in a single transaction
    function putMany(records) {
      if (!Array.isArray(records)) return Promise.reject(new Error('persist.putMany: expected array'));
      return openDatabase(dbName).then(function(db) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
          var tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readwrite');
          var store = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME);
          var ids = [];
          for (var i = 0; i < records.length; i++) {
            var rec = Object.assign({}, records[i]);
            if (rec.id == null) rec.id = uid();
            rec._col = colName;
            rec._id = String(rec.id);
            ids.push(rec.id);
            store.put(rec);
          }
          tx.oncomplete = function() { resolve(ids); };
          tx.onerror = function() { reject(tx.error); };
        });
      });
    }

    // Get a single record by id
    function get(id) {
      return getStore('readonly').then(function(store) {
        return wrapRequest(store.get([colName, String(id)]));
      }).then(function(rec) {
        if (!rec) return null;
        var out = Object.assign({}, rec);
        delete out._col;
        delete out._id;
        return out;
      });
    }

    // Get all records in this collection
    function getAll() {
      return getStore('readonly').then(function(store) {
        var index = store.index('by_col');
        return wrapRequest(index.getAll(colName));
      }).then(function(recs) {
        return (recs || []).map(function(rec) {
          var out = Object.assign({}, rec);
          delete out._col;
          delete out._id;
          return out;
        });
      });
    }

    // Query: get all records matching a filter function
    function query(filterFn) {
      return getAll().then(function(all) {
        if (typeof filterFn !== 'function') return all;
        return all.filter(filterFn);
      });
    }

    // Delete a single record by id
    function del(id) {
      return getStore('readwrite').then(function(store) {
        return wrapRequest(store.delete([colName, String(id)]));
      }).then(function() { return true; });
    }

    // Delete many records by id array
    function delMany(ids) {
      if (!Array.isArray(ids)) return Promise.reject(new Error('persist.delMany: expected array'));
      return openDatabase(dbName).then(function(db) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
          var tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readwrite');
          var store = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME);
          for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
            store.delete([colName, String(ids[i])]);
          }
          tx.oncomplete = function() { resolve(ids.length); };
          tx.onerror = function() { reject(tx.error); };
        });
      });
    }

    // Clear all records in this collection
    function clear() {
      return getAll().then(function(all) {
        var ids = all.map(function(r) { return r.id; });
        return delMany(ids);
      });
    }

    // Count records in this collection
    function count() {
      return getStore('readonly').then(function(store) {
        var index = store.index('by_col');
        return wrapRequest(index.count(colName));
      });
    }

    // Update: merge a patch into an existing record
    function update(id, patch) {
      return get(id).then(function(existing) {
        if (!existing) return Promise.reject(new Error('persist.update: record not found: ' + id));
        var merged = Object.assign({}, existing, patch, { id: id });
        return put(merged);
      });
    }

    return {
      put: put,
      putMany: putMany,
      get: get,
      getAll: getAll,
      query: query,
      delete: del,
      deleteMany: delMany,
      clear: clear,
      count: count,
      update: update
    };
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Database handle
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function openDb(dbName) {
    dbName = dbName || 'weld-persist';

    function collection(name) {
      if (!name) throw new Error('persist: collection name required');
      return makeCollection(dbName, String(name));
    }

    // List all collection names that have data
    function collections() {
      return openDatabase(dbName).then(function(db) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
          var tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readonly');
          var store = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME);
          var index = store.index('by_col');
          var req = index.openKeyCursor();
          var names = {};
          req.onsuccess = function(e) {
            var cursor = e.target.result;
            if (cursor) {
              names[cursor.key] = true;
              cursor.continue();
            } else {
              resolve(Object.keys(names));
            }
          };
          req.onerror = function() { reject(req.error); };
        });
      });
    }

    // Export the entire database as a JSON-safe object (for weld.backup)
    function exportAll() {
      return openDatabase(dbName).then(function(db) {
        return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
          var tx = db.transaction(STORE_NAME, 'readonly');
          var store = tx.objectStore(STORE_NAME);
          var req = store.getAll();
          req.onsuccess = function() {
            var records = req.result || [];
            var byCol = {};
            for (var i = 0; i < records.length; i++) {
              var r = records[i];
              var col = r._col;
              if (!byCol[col]) byCol[col] = [];
              var out = Object.assign({}, r);
              delete out._col;
              delete out._id;
              byCol[col].push(out);
            }
            resolve({ dbName: dbName, collections: byCol, exportedAt: Date.now() });
          };
          req.onerror = function() { reject(req.error); };
        });
      });
    }

    // Import data from an exported object
    function importAll(data) {
      if (!data || !data.collections) {
        return Promise.reject(new Error('persist.importAll: invalid data'));
      }
      var colNames = Object.keys(data.collections);
      var chain = Promise.resolve();
      for (var i = 0; i < colNames.length; i++) {
        (function(colName) {
          var records = data.collections[colName];
          chain = chain.then(function() {
            return collection(colName).putMany(records);
          });
        })(colNames[i]);
      }
      return chain;
    }

    // Delete the entire database
    function destroy() {
      delete dbCache[dbName];
      return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
        var req = indexedDB.deleteDatabase(dbName);
        req.onsuccess = function() { resolve(true); };
        req.onerror = function() { reject(req.error); };
      });
    }

    return {
      collection: collection,
      collections: collections,
      exportAll: exportAll,
      importAll: importAll,
      destroy: destroy,
      name: dbName
    };
  }

  window.weld.persist = {
    open: openDb,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.persist;
  })();
  // ---- weld-skybridge ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.skybridge) return window.weld.skybridge;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.skybridge: the sandbox half of the Weld Companion bridge.
  //
  // Two execution contexts, complementary powers. A PLUGIN (here, in the
  // generator sandbox) is universal but confined. The COMPANION (a
  // userscript, top frame) is privileged but optional. skybridge joins
  // them, without ever letting a plugin require the companion.
  //
  //   var sb = weld.skybridge;
  //   sb.onConnect(function (info) {                 // fires if/when linked
  //     console.log('linked, protocol', info.protocol);
  //   });
  //   if (sb.has('ai')) {                            // honest capability check
  //     var r = await sb.request('ai', { prompt: 'Name a tavern.' });
  //     if (r.ok) use(r.value);                      // result is data, not throw
  //   }
  //   await sb.storage.set('slot1', state);          // works with OR without
  //   var s = await sb.storage.get('slot1');         // the companion present
  //
  // PROTOCOL VERSIONING. The two halves ship independently and land in
  // browsers at different times, so the handshake negotiates a protocol
  // version: each side advertises a min..max range; they settle on the
  // highest both support. No overlap -> stay disconnected (never half-speak a
  // protocol). weld.skybridge.protocol holds the agreed integer (0 = not
  // connected). This is separate from `version` (this plugin's own semver).
  //
  // TRUST. Everything inbound is untrusted. Every message, both ways, is
  // checked: right origin (*.perchance.org), right envelope shape, and a
  // per-request nonce the reply must echo (no spoof, no replay). The
  // companion (not this plugin) owns the consent prompt, per capability,
  // remembered per generator. A denied request comes back as
  // { ok:false, reason:'denied' }: data to branch on, not an exception.
  //
  // SECRETS NEVER CROSS. `ai` sends a prompt up; the companion runs the
  // keyed call itself and sends only the completion down. The API key is
  // never placed on the bridge in either direction.
  //
  // GRACEFUL FALLBACK. With no companion: connected=false, has('ai')=false,
  // but storage still works; it routes to weld.persist if present, else an
  // in-memory map. has('storage') always reports the truth so a plugin CAN
  // distinguish "saved everywhere" from "saved just here" if it cares; most
  // won't need to.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  // ---- protocol the sandbox end speaks (advertise a range) ----
  var PROTO_MIN = 1;
  var PROTO_MAX = 1;
  var MSG = 'weld.skybridge';          // envelope tag, both directions
  var HELLO_TIMEOUT = 4000;            // ms to wait for the anchor to answer
  var REQUEST_TIMEOUT = 30000;         // ms before a pending request gives up
  var BUILD = 'sb-plugin/2026-06-04.4';  // bump on every change; printed at load so a stale deploy is obvious
  var LOADED_AT = Date.now();
  // Early, dependency-free deployment beacon: even if a later line throws, this
  // proves WHICH build actually loaded (read it from the example or console).
  try { window.__weldSkybridge = { build: BUILD, version: '1.2.0', at: Date.now() }; } catch (e) {}
  // verbose console logging toggle: add ?sbdebug to the URL, or set
  // window.WELD_SKYBRIDGE_DEBUG = true before load, or call .debug(true) at runtime.
  var DEBUG = false;
  try {
    if (typeof window.WELD_SKYBRIDGE_DEBUG !== 'undefined') DEBUG = !!window.WELD_SKYBRIDGE_DEBUG;
    else if (typeof location !== 'undefined') DEBUG = ((' ' + location.search + ' ' + location.hash).indexOf('sbdebug') !== -1);
  } catch (e) {}

  // ---- diagnostics: a small ring buffer of handshake events, readable live ----
  var TRACE = new Array();             // ring of { t, dir, type, origin, note } records
  function rec(dir, type, origin, note) {
    try {
      TRACE.push({ t: Date.now(), dir: dir, type: type || '', origin: origin || '', note: note || '' });
      if (TRACE.length > 60) TRACE.shift();
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  // ---- connection state ----
  var connected = false;
  var proto = 0;                       // negotiated protocol (0 = none)
  var caps = {};                       // capability name -> true (advertised)
  var anchorVersion = null;            // the companion's reported semver
  var onConnectFns = new Array();
  var pending = {};                    // nonce -> { resolve, timer }
  var busSubs = {};                    // bus channel -> [fn, ...] (cross-tab pub/sub via companion)
  var helloTimer = null;

  function isTopFrame() { try { return window.top === window.self; } catch (e) { return false; } }
  function originOk(o) {
    if (typeof o !== 'string' || o === 'null') return false;
    if (o === location.origin) return true;
    // Parse without a regex: bracket character-classes like the ones a host
    // pattern would need are themselves list-reference traps in Perchance, so
    // we match "https://(...).perchance.org" with plain string ops instead.
    var host = o;
    var p = host.indexOf('://');
    if (p !== -1) host = host.slice(p + 3);
    var slash = host.indexOf('/'); if (slash !== -1) host = host.slice(0, slash);
    var colon = host.indexOf(':'); if (colon !== -1) host = host.slice(0, colon);
    host = host.toLowerCase();
    return host === 'perchance.org' || (host.length > 13 && host.slice(-14) === '.perchance.org');
  }
  function nonce() {
    return 'sb_' + Date.now().toString(36) + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
  }
  function sbLog() {
    try {
      if (!window.console) return;
      var a = Array.of('\[skybridge\]');                 // escaped so the engine doesn't read it as a list ref
      console.log.apply(console, a.concat(Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments)));
    } catch (e) {}
  }
  function sbDebug() { if (DEBUG) sbLog.apply(null, arguments); }   // verbose; silent unless debug is on
  // the counterpart frame(s): the companion runs in the top frame, but post to
  // the direct parent too in case of nesting. De-dup identical window refs.
  function peers() {
    var out = new Array();
    try { if (window.top && window.top !== window.self) out.push(window.top); } catch (e) {}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent !== window.self && out.indexOf(window.parent) === -1) out.push(window.parent); } catch (e) {}
    if (!out.length) out.push(window);   // not framed: talk to ourselves (e.g. companion-less self-test)
    return out;
  }
  function postUp(obj) {
    var ps = peers();
    for (var i = 0; i < ps.length; i++) { try { Reflect.get(ps, i).postMessage(obj, '*'); } catch (e) { /* cross-origin-guarded; harmless */ } }
  }

  function fireConnect() {
    var info = { protocol: proto, version: anchorVersion, capabilities: Object.keys(caps) };
    for (var i = 0; i < onConnectFns.length; i++) {
      try { Reflect.get(onConnectFns, i)(info); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
    }
  }
  function onConnect(fn) {
    if (typeof fn !== 'function') return function () {};
    onConnectFns.push(fn);
    if (connected) { try { fn({ protocol: proto, version: anchorVersion, capabilities: Object.keys(caps) }); } catch (e) {} }
    return function () { var ix = onConnectFns.indexOf(fn); if (ix !== -1) onConnectFns.splice(ix, 1); };
  }

  // ---- inbound message handling (treat everything as untrusted) ----
  function onMessage(ev) {
    var d = ev && ev.data;
    var isSb = d && typeof d === 'object' && d.channel === MSG;
    // Trace ALL skybridge-tagged traffic before any filter, so a message that
    // gets dropped (bad origin, no common protocol) is still visible.
    if (isSb) rec('rx', d.type, ev.origin, '');
    if (!ev || !originOk(ev.origin)) {
      if (isSb) { rec('drop', d.type, ev.origin, 'origin-rejected'); sbDebug('dropped ' + d.type + ' from disallowed origin ' + ev.origin); }
      return;
    }
    if (!isSb) return;

    if (d.type === 'here') {
      // handshake reply: negotiate the highest protocol both ends share
      var lo = Math.max(PROTO_MIN, (d.protoMin | 0) || 0);
      var hi = Math.min(PROTO_MAX, (d.protoMax | 0) || 0);
      if (hi < lo) { rec('drop', 'here', ev.origin, 'no-common-protocol'); sbDebug('here from ' + ev.origin + ' but no common protocol (' + d.protoMin + '..' + d.protoMax + ' vs ' + PROTO_MIN + '..' + PROTO_MAX + ')'); return; }
      if (connected) return;           // already linked; ignore duplicates
      proto = hi;
      anchorVersion = (typeof d.version === 'string') ? d.version : null;
      caps = {};
      if (d.capabilities && typeof d.capabilities === 'object' && d.capabilities.length != null) {
        for (var i = 0; i < d.capabilities.length; i++) {
          var c = Reflect.get(d.capabilities, i);
          if (typeof c === 'string') Reflect.set(caps, c, true);
        }
      }
      connected = true;
      if (helloTimer) { clearTimeout(helloTimer); helloTimer = null; }
      rec('ok', 'connected', ev.origin, 'proto ' + proto);
      sbLog('connected to companion (protocol ' + proto + ', caps: ' + Object.keys(caps).join(',') + ')');
      fireConnect();
      return;
    }

    if (d.type === 'reply') {
      var p = Reflect.get(pending, String(d.nonce));
      if (!p) return;                  // unknown / replayed / spoofed nonce -> drop
      Reflect.deleteProperty(pending, String(d.nonce));
      if (p.timer) clearTimeout(p.timer);
      var result = (d.result && typeof d.result === 'object')
        ? d.result
        : { ok: false, reason: 'malformed' };
      p.resolve(result);
      return;
    }

    if (d.type === 'bus') {
      // unsolicited push from the companion: a message on a channel we subscribed to
      var subs = Reflect.get(busSubs, String(d.busChannel));
      if (subs) { for (var bi = 0; bi < subs.length; bi++) { try { subs[bi](d.message); } catch (e) {} } }
      return;
    }
  }

  // ---- send a capability request up; resolve with a result object ----
  function request(capability, payload) {
    return new Promise(function (resolve) {
      if (!connected) { resolve({ ok: false, reason: 'disconnected' }); return; }
      if (!Reflect.get(caps, String(capability))) { resolve({ ok: false, reason: 'unsupported' }); return; }
      var id = nonce();
      var timer = setTimeout(function () {
        if (Reflect.get(pending, id)) {
          Reflect.deleteProperty(pending, id);
          resolve({ ok: false, reason: 'timeout' });
        }
      }, REQUEST_TIMEOUT);
      Reflect.set(pending, id, { resolve: resolve, timer: timer });
      postUp({
        channel: MSG, type: 'request', proto: proto, nonce: id,
        cap: String(capability),
        payload: (payload && typeof payload === 'object') ? payload : {}
      });
    });
  }

  function has(capability) { return !!Reflect.get(caps, String(capability)); }

  // ---- storage: companion, else weld.kv (cross-device), else weld.persist, else memory ----
  // Uniform async (Promise) API, since the companion path is a round-trip. A single
  // pickBackend() chooses the active tier; get/set/list dispatch on it and backend()
  // returns it, so what backend() reports can never drift from where data actually goes.
  var mem = {};                        // session-only fallback map
  var persistColl = null;              // lazily-opened weld.persist collection
  function persistCollection() {
    if (persistColl) return persistColl;
    try {
      if (window.weld && window.weld.persist && typeof window.weld.persist.open === 'function') {
        var db = window.weld.persist.open('weld-skybridge');
        persistColl = db.collection('kv');
        return persistColl;
      }
    } catch (e) { /* not available */ }
    return null;
  }
  var kvColl = null;                   // lazily-opened weld.kv folder (server-side, cross-device)
  function kvHandle() {
    if (kvColl) return kvColl;
    try {
      var kv = window.weld && window.weld.kv;
      // only when the *server* kv-plugin is actually present (available()), not just kv's mirror
      if (kv && typeof kv.folder === 'function' && typeof kv.available === 'function' && kv.available()) {
        kvColl = kv.folder('weld-skybridge');
        return kvColl;
      }
    } catch (e) { /* not available */ }
    return null;
  }
  // the single source of truth for which tier is live, in priority order
  function pickBackend() {
    if (connected && has('storage')) return 'companion';
    if (kvHandle()) return 'kv';
    if (persistCollection()) return 'persist';
    return 'memory';
  }
  function storageGet(key) {
    var k = String(key);
    switch (pickBackend()) {
      case 'companion':
        return request('storage', { op: 'get', key: k }).then(function (r) { return r.ok ? r.value : null; });
      case 'kv':
        return Promise.resolve(kvHandle().get(k, null)).then(function (v) { return v == null ? null : v; }, function () { return null; });
      case 'persist':
        return Promise.resolve(persistCollection().get(k)).then(function (rec) { return (rec != null && rec.value !== undefined) ? rec.value : null; }, function () { return null; });
      default:
        return Promise.resolve(Reflect.has(mem, k) ? Reflect.get(mem, k) : null);
    }
  }
  function storageSet(key, value) {
    var k = String(key);
    switch (pickBackend()) {
      case 'companion':
        return request('storage', { op: 'set', key: k, value: value }).then(function (r) { return !!r.ok; });
      case 'kv':
        return Promise.resolve(kvHandle().set(k, value)).then(function () { return true; }, function () { return false; });
      case 'persist':
        return Promise.resolve(persistCollection().put({ id: k, value: value })).then(function () { return true; }, function () { return false; });
      default:
        Reflect.set(mem, k, value);
        return Promise.resolve(true);
    }
  }
  function storageList(prefix) {
    var pre = prefix != null ? String(prefix) : '';
    function filterKeys(ks) {
      var out = new Array();
      if (ks && ks.length != null) {
        for (var i = 0; i < ks.length; i++) {
          var key = Reflect.get(ks, i);
          if (typeof key === 'string' && key.indexOf(pre) === 0) out.push(key);
        }
      }
      return out;
    }
    switch (pickBackend()) {
      case 'companion':
        return request('storage', { op: 'list', prefix: pre }).then(function (r) { return r.ok ? r.value : new Array(); });
      case 'kv':
        return Promise.resolve(kvHandle().keys()).then(filterKeys, function () { return new Array(); });
      case 'persist': {
        var coll = persistCollection();
        if (coll && typeof coll.query === 'function') {
          return Promise.resolve(coll.query()).then(function (rows) {
            var ks = new Array();
            if (rows && rows.length != null) { for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) { ks.push(Reflect.get(Reflect.get(rows, i) || {}, 'id')); } }
            return filterKeys(ks);
          }, function () { return new Array(); });
        }
        return Promise.resolve(new Array());
      }
      default: {
        var keys = Object.keys(mem), res = new Array();
        for (var j = 0; j < keys.length; j++) { var kk = Reflect.get(keys, j); if (kk.indexOf(pre) === 0) res.push(kk); }
        return Promise.resolve(res);
      }
    }
  }
  // where is storage actually going right now? (for honesty / debugging); same picker get/set use
  function storageBackend() { return pickBackend(); }

  // ---- ai: prompt up, completion down; key never crosses ----
  // ---- bus: cross-tab / cross-generator pub/sub, relayed by the companion ----
  // publish resolves a result object; subscribe registers a local handler and
  // tells the companion to relay matching messages down. Works only with a
  // companion that advertises 'bus'; callers (e.g. weld.swarm) gate on has('bus').
  function busPublish(channel, message) {
    return request('bus', { op: 'publish', channel: String(channel), message: message });
  }
  function busSubscribe(channel, fn) {
    if (typeof fn !== 'function') return function () {};
    var ch = String(channel);
    var arr = Reflect.get(busSubs, ch);
    if (!arr) { arr = new Array(); Reflect.set(busSubs, ch, arr); request('bus', { op: 'subscribe', channel: ch }); }
    arr.push(fn);
    return function () {
      var a = Reflect.get(busSubs, ch); if (!a) return;
      var ix = a.indexOf(fn); if (ix !== -1) a.splice(ix, 1);
      if (!a.length) { Reflect.deleteProperty(busSubs, ch); request('bus', { op: 'unsubscribe', channel: ch }); }
    };
  }

  function ai(prompt, options) {
    var payload = { prompt: String(prompt != null ? prompt : '') };
    if (options && typeof options === 'object') {
      if (options.system != null) payload.system = String(options.system);
      if (options.maxTokens != null) payload.maxTokens = options.maxTokens | 0;
      if (options.temperature != null) payload.temperature = +options.temperature;
    }
    return request('ai', payload);     // resolves { ok, value } or { ok:false, reason }
  }

  // ---- start the handshake ----
  function connect() {
    if (connected) return;
    var ps = peers();
    rec('tx', 'hello', '', ps.length + ' peer(s)');
    sbDebug('sending hello to ' + ps.length + ' peer frame(s); framed=' + (window.top !== window.self));
    postUp({ channel: MSG, type: 'hello', protoMin: PROTO_MIN, protoMax: PROTO_MAX });
    if (!helloTimer) {
      helloTimer = setTimeout(function () { helloTimer = null; if (!connected) { rec('to', 'timeout', '', 'no answer'); sbDebug('no companion answered (fallback mode)'); } }, HELLO_TIMEOUT);
    }
  }

  try { window.addEventListener('message', onMessage, false); } catch (e) { /* no window.addEventListener?? */ }
  // kick the handshake now and once more after load, in case the anchor mounts late
  connect();
  try { window.addEventListener('load', connect, { once: true }); } catch (e) {}
  // The companion anchor mounts at the top frame's document-idle, usually after
  // we load, so our first hellos may arrive before it is listening. Retry a few
  // times; connect() no-ops once linked. (The companion also announces itself
  // downward, so whichever side comes up first, the link forms.)
  Array.of(150, 500, 1500, 3000).forEach(function (t) { setTimeout(connect, t); });

  window.weld.skybridge = {
    // connection
    get connected() { return connected; },
    get protocol() { return proto; },          // negotiated protocol int (0 = none)
    get anchorVersion() { return anchorVersion; },
    has: has,
    onConnect: onConnect,
    reconnect: connect,
    // privileged calls (each resolves a result object, never throws)
    request: request,
    ai: ai,
    // storage: graceful fallback, honest backend
    storage: { get: storageGet, set: storageSet, list: storageList, backend: storageBackend },
    // bus: cross-tab / cross-generator pub/sub (only live when the companion advertises 'bus')
    bus: { publish: busPublish, subscribe: busSubscribe },
    // protocol range this sandbox end speaks
    protocolRange: { min: PROTO_MIN, max: PROTO_MAX },
    version: '1.2.0',
    build: BUILD,
    // verbose-logging toggle. on()/off; returns the new state.
    debug: function (on) {
      DEBUG = (on !== false);
      sbLog('debug ' + (DEBUG ? 'ON' : 'OFF') + ' \u2014 build ' + BUILD + ', connected=' + connected + ', protocol=' + proto);
      return DEBUG;
    },
    // a live snapshot for troubleshooting (state + recent handshake events)
    diagnostics: function () {
      return {
        build: BUILD, version: '1.2.0', debug: DEBUG, loadedAt: LOADED_AT,
        connected: connected, protocol: proto, anchorVersion: anchorVersion,
        framed: (function () { try { return window.top !== window.self; } catch (e) { return null; } })(),
        origin: location.origin,
        peers: peers().length,
        capabilities: Object.keys(caps),
        storageBackend: storageBackend(),
        trace: TRACE.slice()
      };
    }
  };

  rec('init', 'load', location.origin, BUILD);
  sbLog('plugin ' + BUILD + ' loaded; framed=' + (function () { try { return window.top !== window.self; } catch (e) { return '?'; } })() + ' origin=' + location.origin + (DEBUG ? ' (debug ON)' : ''));
  return window.weld.skybridge;
  })();
  // ---- weld-sync ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.sync) return window.weld.sync;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Cross-tab sync: BroadcastChannel + namespaced localStorage.
  // Same-origin tabs of the same generator see each other's updates instantly.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function uid() {
    return Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10) + '_' + Date.now();
  }

  function createSync(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var namespace = String(opts.namespace || (window.generatorName || 'anon')).replace(/[^a-z0-9-]/gi, '_');
    var STORAGE_PREFIX = 'weld-sync_' + namespace + ':';
    var CHANNEL_NAME = 'weld-sync_' + namespace + '_channel';
    var PEER_ID = uid();

    var bc = null;
    try { bc = new BroadcastChannel(CHANNEL_NAME); } catch (e) { /* fallback below */ }

    var channels = {};
    var changeListeners = [];
    var keyListeners = {};
    var peers = new Set();
    var lastPeerHeartbeat = {};

    function emit(target, args) {
      for (var i = 0; i < target.length; i++) {
        try { target[i].apply(null, args); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }

    function handleMessage(msg) {
      if (!msg || typeof msg !== 'object') return;
      if (msg.peer === PEER_ID) return;

      if (msg.type === 'set') {
        emit(changeListeners, [msg.key, msg.value, 'remote']);
        if (keyListeners[msg.key]) emit(keyListeners[msg.key], [msg.value, 'remote']);
      } else if (msg.type === 'delete') {
        emit(changeListeners, [msg.key, undefined, 'remote']);
        if (keyListeners[msg.key]) emit(keyListeners[msg.key], [undefined, 'remote']);
      } else if (msg.type === 'broadcast') {
        if (channels[msg.channel]) emit(channels[msg.channel], [msg.data, msg.peer]);
      } else if (msg.type === 'heartbeat') {
        peers.add(msg.peer);
        lastPeerHeartbeat[msg.peer] = Date.now();
      } else if (msg.type === 'goodbye') {
        peers.delete(msg.peer);
        delete lastPeerHeartbeat[msg.peer];
      }
    }

    if (bc) bc.onmessage = function(e) { handleMessage(e.data); };

    // Storage event fallback
    window.addEventListener('storage', function(e) {
      if (!e.key || e.key.indexOf(STORAGE_PREFIX) !== 0) return;
      var key = e.key.slice(STORAGE_PREFIX.length);
      var value;
      try { value = e.newValue === null ? undefined : JSON.parse(e.newValue); }
      catch (err) { value = e.newValue; }
      emit(changeListeners, [key, value, 'remote']);
      if (keyListeners[key]) emit(keyListeners[key], [value, 'remote']);
    });

    function publish(msg) {
      if (bc) {
        try { bc.postMessage(Object.assign({ peer: PEER_ID }, msg)); }
        catch (e) { /* channel might be closed */ }
      }
    }

    function heartbeat() { publish({ type: 'heartbeat' }); }
    function pruneStale() {
      var now = Date.now();
      var arr = Array.from(peers);
      for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
        var id = arr[i];
        if (now - (lastPeerHeartbeat[id] || 0) > 8000) {
          peers.delete(id);
          delete lastPeerHeartbeat[id];
        }
      }
    }
    var heartbeatTimer = setInterval(function() { heartbeat(); pruneStale(); }, 3000);
    heartbeat();

    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function() { publish({ type: 'goodbye' }); });

    // ---------- API ----------
    var api = {};

    api.set = function(key, value) {
      try {
        localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_PREFIX + key, JSON.stringify(value));
        publish({ type: 'set', key: key, value: value });
        emit(changeListeners, [key, value, 'local']);
        if (keyListeners[key]) emit(keyListeners[key], [value, 'local']);
        return true;
      } catch (e) { return false; }
    };

    api.get = function(key, defaultValue) {
      try {
        var raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_PREFIX + key);
        if (raw === null) return defaultValue;
        return JSON.parse(raw);
      } catch (e) { return defaultValue; }
    };

    api.has = function(key) {
      return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_PREFIX + key) !== null;
    };

    api.delete = function(key) {
      try {
        localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_PREFIX + key);
        publish({ type: 'delete', key: key });
        emit(changeListeners, [key, undefined, 'local']);
        if (keyListeners[key]) emit(keyListeners[key], [undefined, 'local']);
        return true;
      } catch (e) { return false; }
    };

    api.keys = function() {
      var out = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++) {
        var k = localStorage.key(i);
        if (k && k.indexOf(STORAGE_PREFIX) === 0) out.push(k.slice(STORAGE_PREFIX.length));
      }
      return out;
    };

    api.clear = function() {
      var ks = api.keys();
      for (var i = 0; i < ks.length; i++) api.delete(ks[i]);
      return ks.length;
    };

    // Ephemeral pub/sub
    api.broadcast = function(channel, data) {
      publish({ type: 'broadcast', channel: channel, data: data });
      return true;
    };

    api.subscribe = function(channel, callback) {
      if (!channels[channel]) channels[channel] = [];
      channels[channel].push(callback);
      return function() {
        var arr = channels[channel];
        if (!arr) return;
        var idx = arr.indexOf(callback);
        if (idx >= 0) arr.splice(idx, 1);
      };
    };

    api.onChange = function(callback) {
      changeListeners.push(callback);
      return function() {
        var idx = changeListeners.indexOf(callback);
        if (idx >= 0) changeListeners.splice(idx, 1);
      };
    };

    api.onKeyChange = function(key, callback) {
      if (!keyListeners[key]) keyListeners[key] = [];
      keyListeners[key].push(callback);
      return function() {
        var arr = keyListeners[key];
        if (!arr) return;
        var idx = arr.indexOf(callback);
        if (idx >= 0) arr.splice(idx, 1);
      };
    };

    api.peers = function() { return peers.size; };
    api.peerIds = function() { return Array.from(peers); };
    api.myId = function() { return PEER_ID; };

    // Reactive state primitive
    api.state = function(key, defaultValue) {
      if (!api.has(key) && defaultValue !== undefined) {
        api.set(key, defaultValue);
      }
      var subs = [];
      var unsub = api.onKeyChange(key, function(value, source) {
        for (var i = 0; i < subs.length; i++) {
          try { subs[i](value, source); } catch (e) {}
        }
      });
      return {
        get: function() { return api.get(key, defaultValue); },
        set: function(v) { return api.set(key, v); },
        onChange: function(fn) {
          subs.push(fn);
          return function() { var i = subs.indexOf(fn); if (i >= 0) subs.splice(i, 1); };
        },
        destroy: unsub
      };
    };

    api.info = function() {
      return {
        namespace: namespace,
        storagePrefix: STORAGE_PREFIX,
        broadcastChannel: CHANNEL_NAME,
        broadcastSupported: bc !== null,
        peerId: PEER_ID,
        peerCount: peers.size,
        storedKeys: api.keys().length
      };
    };

    api.destroy = function() {
      clearInterval(heartbeatTimer);
      publish({ type: 'goodbye' });
      if (bc) try { bc.close(); } catch (e) {}
    };

    return api;
  }

  window.weld.sync = {
    create: createSync,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.sync;
  })();
  // ---- weld-fetch ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.fetch) return window.weld.fetch;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.fetch: reach the outside world from inside the sandbox.
  //
  // A generator runs in a sandboxed iframe, so a plain fetch() to a third
  // party is usually blocked by CORS. Perchance provides superFetch, which
  // routes requests through fetch-plugin.perchance.org. weld.fetch wraps it
  // with the helpers people actually want and encodes the proxy's quirks:
  //
  //   - request headers are STRIPPED by the proxy (don't rely on them)
  //   - internal/SSRF targets are blocked
  //   - redirects are followed; there is no small body cap
  //   - identical URLs may be cached by the proxy
  //
  //   await weld.fetch.json('https://api.example.com/data')   // GET + parse
  //   await weld.fetch.post(url, { body: payload, json: true })
  //   await weld.fetch.get(url, { timeoutMs: 8000, retries: 2 })
  //
  // For hosts that already send permissive CORS (raw.githubusercontent,
  // jsdelivr, ...), set { direct: true } (or call when superFetch is
  // absent) to use the browser's own fetch and skip the proxy hop.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var deps = { superFetch: null };
  function getSF() {
    return deps.superFetch
      || (window.weld && window.weld.__superFetch)
      || (typeof window !== 'undefined' && typeof window.superFetch === 'function' ? window.superFetch : null)
      || (typeof superFetch === 'function' ? superFetch : null);
  }
  function attach(d) { if (d && d.superFetch) deps.superFetch = d.superFetch; }

  // Hosts known to serve permissive CORS, safe to hit directly, skipping
  // the proxy. Extendable via opts.direct or addDirectHost().
  var DIRECT_HOSTS = ['raw.githubusercontent.com', 'cdn.jsdelivr.net', 'api.github.com'];
  function isDirectHost(url) {
    try { var h = new URL(url).hostname; return DIRECT_HOSTS.indexOf(h) !== -1; }
    catch (e) { return false; }
  }
  function addDirectHost(h) { if (h && DIRECT_HOSTS.indexOf(h) === -1) DIRECT_HOSTS.push(String(h)); }

  function withTimeout(promise, ms, label) {
    if (!ms) return promise;
    return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
      var done = false;
      var t = setTimeout(function () { if (!done) { done = true; reject(new Error('weld.fetch: timeout after ' + ms + 'ms' + (label ? ' (' + label + ')' : ''))); } }, ms);
      Promise.resolve(promise).then(
        function (v) { if (!done) { done = true; clearTimeout(t); resolve(v); } },
        function (e) { if (!done) { done = true; clearTimeout(t); reject(e); } });
    });
  }

  // Core request. opts: { method, headers, body, json, direct, timeoutMs,
  // retries, retryDelayMs }. Resolves a normalized response, NOT a raw
  // Response, so callers don't have to remember .text()/.json() or the
  // proxy's boxed quirks.
  function request(url, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    url = String(url || '');
    if (!url) return Promise.reject(new Error('weld.fetch: empty URL'));
    var method = (opts.method || 'GET').toUpperCase();

    // Tier 0: the Weld Companion's GM_xmlhttpRequest, a true cross-origin bypass
    // with real header control (no proxy stripping), gated by the user's per-host
    // consent. Available only when the userscript is installed and advertises
    // 'fetch'. On denial or transport failure, fall through to the proxy/direct
    // tiers so callers still get the best available path. Skipped when the caller
    // forces { direct: true }.
    var sb = window.weld && window.weld.skybridge;
    if (opts.direct !== true && sb && sb.connected && typeof sb.has === 'function' && sb.has('fetch') && typeof sb.request === 'function') {
      var cbody = (opts.body != null) ? ((opts.json && typeof opts.body !== 'string') ? JSON.stringify(opts.body) : opts.body) : undefined;
      var cheaders = opts.headers || (opts.json ? { 'content-type': 'application/json' } : undefined);
      return sb.request('fetch', { url: url, method: method, headers: cheaders, body: cbody })
        .then(function (r) {
          if (r && typeof r.status === 'number' && r.status > 0) return normalizeCompanion(r, url);
          return viaProxyOrDirect(url, opts, method);   // denied / network error -> fall through
        }, function () { return viaProxyOrDirect(url, opts, method); });
    }
    return viaProxyOrDirect(url, opts, method);
  }

  // Tiers 1+2: superFetch proxy (default) then direct browser fetch.
  function viaProxyOrDirect(url, opts, method) {
    var direct = opts.direct === true || (opts.direct !== false && isDirectHost(url));
    var sf = getSF();
    if (!sf && !direct) {
      // No proxy available and not a known-direct host: try direct anyway,
      // but warn via the error if CORS then blocks it.
      direct = true;
    }
    var fetcher = direct ? (typeof fetch === 'function' ? fetch : null) : sf;
    if (!fetcher) return Promise.reject(new Error('weld.fetch: no fetch available (superFetch missing and no global fetch)'));

    var init = { method: method };
    if (opts.headers) init.headers = opts.headers; // note: proxy strips these
    if (opts.body != null) {
      init.body = (opts.json && typeof opts.body !== 'string') ? JSON.stringify(opts.body) : opts.body;
      if (opts.json && !direct) { init.headers = Object.assign({ 'content-type': 'application/json' }, init.headers || {}); }
    }

    var timeoutMs = opts.timeoutMs != null ? opts.timeoutMs : 15000;
    var retries = opts.retries || 0;
    var retryDelay = opts.retryDelayMs || 600;

    function attempt(n) {
      return withTimeout(Promise.resolve(fetcher(url, init)), timeoutMs, method + ' ' + url)
        .then(function (res) { return normalize(res, url, direct); })
        .catch(function (err) {
          if (n < retries) {
            return new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, retryDelay * (n + 1)); }).then(function () { return attempt(n + 1); });
          }
          // If we're under Perchance's ?$csp restricted mode, an outbound
          // failure is most likely the platform blocking it, not a bug.
          if (cspActive() && err && err.message && err.message.indexOf('$csp') === -1) {
            err.message += ' (note: page is in Perchance ?$csp restricted mode, which can block outbound requests)';
          }
          throw err;
        });
    }
    return attempt(0);
  }

  // Normalize the companion's fetch result (plain {status,headers,body}) into the
  // same shape as a proxy/direct response, so callers can't tell the tiers apart.
  function normalizeCompanion(r, url) {
    var status = (typeof r.status === 'number') ? r.status : 0;
    var bodyText = (typeof r.body === 'string') ? r.body : '';
    function text() { return Promise.resolve(bodyText); }
    function json() { return text().then(function (t) { try { return JSON.parse(t); } catch (e) { throw new Error('weld.fetch: response is not JSON (' + t.slice(0, 60) + ')'); } }); }
    return { ok: !!r.ok, status: status, url: r.url || url, via: 'companion', headers: r.headers || null, text: text, json: json, truncated: !!r.truncated, raw: r };
  }

  // Normalize a fetch Response (or superFetch result) into a plain object.
  function normalize(res, url, direct) {
    if (res == null) return { ok: false, status: 0, url: url, via: direct ? 'direct' : 'proxy', text: function () { return Promise.resolve(''); } };
    var status = (typeof res.status === 'number') ? res.status : 200;
    var ok = (typeof res.ok === 'boolean') ? res.ok : (status >= 200 && status < 300);
    var headers = res.headers || null;
    var bodyText = null;
    function text() {
      if (bodyText != null) return Promise.resolve(bodyText);
      if (typeof res.text === 'function') return Promise.resolve(res.text()).then(function (t) { bodyText = String(t); return bodyText; });
      bodyText = String(res); return Promise.resolve(bodyText);
    }
    function json() { return text().then(function (t) { try { return JSON.parse(t); } catch (e) { throw new Error('weld.fetch: response is not JSON (' + t.slice(0, 60) + ')'); } }); }
    return { ok: ok, status: status, url: url, via: direct ? 'direct' : 'proxy', headers: headers, text: text, json: json, raw: res };
  }

  // Convenience verbs.
  function get(url, opts) { return request(url, Object.assign({}, opts, { method: 'GET' })); }
  function post(url, opts) { return request(url, Object.assign({}, opts, { method: 'POST' })); }
  function del(url, opts) { return request(url, Object.assign({}, opts, { method: 'DELETE' })); }

  // GET (or any method) and parse JSON in one step -> the parsed value.
  function json(url, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    return request(url, opts).then(function (res) {
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('weld.fetch: ' + res.status + ' from ' + url);
      return res.json();
    });
  }
  // GET and return text in one step.
  function text(url, opts) { return request(url, opts || {}).then(function (res) { return res.text(); }); }

  function available() { return !!getSF(); }

  // Perchance's ?$csp URL mode (perchance.org/custom-content-security-policy)
  // restricts a page's ability to reach external servers. Under it, the
  // superFetch proxy and direct fetches to outside hosts may be blocked at
  // the platform level. weld.fetch can't lift that restriction, but it can
  // tell you it's in effect so a failed request reads as "CSP blocked this"
  // rather than a mysterious network error.
  function cspActive() {
    try {
      var q = (typeof location !== 'undefined' && location.search) ? location.search : '';
      var h = (typeof location !== 'undefined' && location.href) ? location.href : '';
      return /[?&]\$csp(\b|=|&|$)/.test(q) || /[?&]\$csp(\b|=|&|$)/.test(h);
    } catch (e) { return false; }
  }

  window.weld.fetch = {
    request: request,
    get: get,
    post: post,
    del: del,
    json: json,
    text: text,
    attach: attach,
    available: available,
    cspActive: cspActive,
    addDirectHost: addDirectHost,
    directHosts: function () { return DIRECT_HOSTS.slice(); },
    version: '1.2.0'
  };

  return window.weld.fetch;
  })();
  // ---- weld-stream ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.stream) {
    window.weld.stream.attach({ aiTextPlugin: aiTextPlugin });
    return window.weld.stream;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.stream: the generation half of an AI chat app.
  //
  // weld.prompt assembles the instruction string; weld.stream sends it
  // to ai-text-plugin and manages the call lifecycle. It exists because
  // the raw plugin has three sharp edges that every consumer re-hits:
  //
  //   1. The resolved value is a BOXED String, not a primitive, so
  //      `result === "x"` is always false. We hand back a plain string.
  //   2. stopReason is "natural" | "artificial" | "error" | "user" --
  //      NOT the "stop_sequence"/"max_tokens" the official docs claim.
  //      We translate to plain booleans: truncated / aborted / error.
  //   3. The broker accepts exactly one generation at a time. Overlapping
  //      calls don't error; they just contend. We serialize them in an
  //      internal FIFO queue so callers can fire-and-forget.
  //
  // The plugin must be imported in the lists editor (see the import
  // directive at the top of this generator) and handed to us via
  // weld.stream.attach({ aiTextPlugin: aiTextPlugin }); the DSL form
  // below does this automatically. If you skip it we also try
  // window.root.aiTextPlugin as a fallback.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var deps = { aiTextPlugin: null };

  function attach(d) {
    if (d && typeof d.aiTextPlugin === 'function') deps.aiTextPlugin = d.aiTextPlugin;
  }

  function grabPlugin() {
    if (typeof deps.aiTextPlugin === 'function') return deps.aiTextPlugin;
    try {
      if (window.root && typeof window.root.aiTextPlugin === 'function') return window.root.aiTextPlugin;
    } catch (e) { /* proxy miss */ }
    return null;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Constants. A literal double-open-bracket sequence would be read as a
  // Perchance template by the source scanner, so we assemble it from char
  // codes instead.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var LBR = String.fromCharCode(91);            // "["
  var DOUBLE = LBR + LBR;                        // a double open bracket
  var DEFAULT_CHAT_STOPS = ['\n\n' + DOUBLE, '\n' + DOUBLE]; // the two standard chat stop sequences
  var MAX_STOP_SEQUENCES = 20;                   // hard backend limit (21+ => stopReason "error")

  var idSeq = 0;
  function nextId() {
    idSeq += 1;
    return 'weldStream' + Date.now() + '_' + idSeq;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Normalize the boxed-String result into a plain, predictable object.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function normalize(result) {
    var out = {
      text: '',
      stopReason: 'natural',
      truncated: false,   // "artificial": hit a stop sequence or the output ceiling
      aborted: false,     // "user": stop() was called
      error: null
    };
    if (result == null) {
      out.stopReason = 'error';
      out.error = 'no result returned from ai-text-plugin';
      return out;
    }
    var reason = result.stopReason || 'natural';
    out.stopReason = reason;
    // generatedText is the full output; String(result) also works on the box.
    out.text = (result.generatedText != null) ? String(result.generatedText) : String(result);
    if (reason === 'artificial') out.truncated = true;
    if (reason === 'user') out.aborted = true;
    if (reason === 'error') {
      out.error = 'ai-text-plugin reported a generation error';
      out.text = '';
    }
    return out;
  }

  function clampStops(stops) {
    if (stops == null) return null;
    if (!Array.isArray(stops)) stops = [ stops];
    stops = stops.filter(function (s) { return s != null && String(s).length > 0; });
    if (stops.length === 0) return null;
    if (stops.length > MAX_STOP_SEQUENCES) stops = stops.slice(0, MAX_STOP_SEQUENCES);
    return stops;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Serial queue. activeEntry is the in-flight generation; the broker
  // handles exactly one at a time, so everything else waits behind it.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var queue = [];
  var activeEntry = null;
  var pumping = false;

  function buildCallOpts(entry) {
    var o = entry.opts;
    var callOpts = { instruction: String(o.instruction) };

    if (o.startWith != null) {
      callOpts.startWith = String(o.startWith);
      // Default to hiding the echoed prefix unless the caller opts out.
      callOpts.hideStartWith = (o.hideStartWith !== false);
    }

    var stops = (o.stopSequences != null)
      ? o.stopSequences
      : (o.chat ? DEFAULT_CHAT_STOPS : null);
    stops = clampStops(stops);
    if (stops) callOpts.stopSequences = stops;

    // Stream only when a chunk/token handler is supplied. A bare await
    // path still resolves with the complete text either way.
    if (typeof o.onChunk === 'function' || typeof o.onToken === 'function') {
      callOpts.onChunk = function (c) {
        if (!c) return;
        if (c.isFromStartWith) return;           // skip the echoed startWith
        var delta = c.textChunk || '';
        entry.liveText += delta;
        if (typeof o.onChunk === 'function') {
          try { o.onChunk(delta, entry.liveText); } catch (e) { /* consumer error */ }
        }
        if (typeof o.onToken === 'function') {
          try { o.onToken(delta); } catch (e) { /* consumer error */ }
        }
      };
    }
    return callOpts;
  }

  function settle(entry, norm) {
    if (entry._settled) return;
    entry._settled = true;
    var o = entry.opts;
    if (norm.error && typeof o.onError === 'function') {
      try { o.onError(norm.error, norm); } catch (e) { /* consumer error */ }
    }
    if (typeof o.onDone === 'function') {
      try { o.onDone(norm); } catch (e) { /* consumer error */ }
    }
    entry._resolve(norm);
  }

  function pump() {
    if (pumping || activeEntry) return;
    // Drop any entries cancelled while queued (already settled by stop()).
    while (queue.length && queue[0]._settled) queue.shift();
    if (queue.length === 0) return;

    pumping = true;
    var entry = queue.shift();
    activeEntry = entry;
    entry.started = true;

    var plugin = grabPlugin();
    if (!plugin) {
      activeEntry = null;
      pumping = false;
      settle(entry, {
        text: '', stopReason: 'error', truncated: false, aborted: false,
        error: 'weld.stream: ai-text-plugin is not attached. Add '
          + 'aiTextPlugin = ' + '{' + 'import:ai-text-plugin' + '}'
          + ' to your lists and call weld.stream.attach({ aiTextPlugin }).'
      });
      pump();
      return;
    }

    var instr = entry.opts.instruction;
    if (instr == null || String(instr).trim() === '') {
      activeEntry = null;
      pumping = false;
      settle(entry, {
        text: '', stopReason: 'error', truncated: false, aborted: false,
        error: 'weld.stream: instruction is empty.'
      });
      pump();
      return;
    }

    var done = function (norm) {
      activeEntry = null;
      entry.inner = null;
      pumping = false;
      settle(entry, norm);
      pump();
    };

    try {
      var inner = plugin(buildCallOpts(entry));   // synchronous extended-Promise handle
      entry.inner = inner;
      // If stop() arrived between dequeue and here, honor it now.
      if (entry._stopRequested && inner && typeof inner.stop === 'function') {
        try { inner.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
      }
      Promise.resolve(inner).then(function (raw) {
        done(normalize(raw));
      }, function (err) {
        done({
          text: '', stopReason: 'error', truncated: false, aborted: false,
          error: String((err && err.message) || err)
        });
      });
    } catch (err) {
      done({
        text: '', stopReason: 'error', truncated: false, aborted: false,
        error: String((err && err.message) || err)
      });
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Public: run(opts) -> handle. The handle is thenable and abortable.
  //
  // opts:
  //   instruction    (string, required)
  //   startWith      (string)  text the model continues from
  //   hideStartWith  (bool)    default true when startWith is set
  //   stopSequences  (string[]) clamped to 20; falls back to chat stops if chat:true
  //   chat           (bool)    use the double-bracketed Name wire-format stops
  //   onChunk(delta, fullText) stream callback (enables streaming)
  //   onToken(delta)           lighter stream callback
  //   onDone(result)           fires once on completion (any outcome)
  //   onError(message, result) fires once on error
  //
  // resolves to: { text, stopReason, truncated, aborted, error }
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function run(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var entry = {
      id: nextId(),
      opts: opts,
      liveText: '',
      started: false,
      inner: null,
      _settled: false,
      _stopRequested: false,
      _resolve: null
    };
    entry.promise = new Promise(function (resolve) { entry._resolve = resolve; });

    function stop() {
      entry._stopRequested = true;
      if (entry._settled) return;
      if (activeEntry === entry && entry.inner && typeof entry.inner.stop === 'function') {
        // In flight: abort the broker call. It resolves with stopReason "user".
        try { entry.inner.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
      } else if (!entry.started) {
        // Still queued: settle immediately as aborted; pump() will skip it.
        settle(entry, {
          text: entry.liveText, stopReason: 'user',
          truncated: false, aborted: true, error: null
        });
      }
    }

    var handle = {
      id: entry.id,
      stop: stop,
      promise: entry.promise,
      then: function (a, b) { return entry.promise.then(a, b); },
      catch: function (b) { return entry.promise.catch(b); },
      finally: function (f) { return entry.promise.finally(f); }
    };
    Object.defineProperty(handle, 'liveText', { get: function () { return entry.liveText; } });
    Object.defineProperty(handle, 'started', { get: function () { return entry.started; } });
    Object.defineProperty(handle, 'queued', { get: function () { return !entry.started && !entry._settled; } });

    queue.push(entry);
    pump();
    return handle;
  }

  // Abort the active generation and discard everything queued behind it.
  function stopAll() {
    var pending = queue.slice();
    if (activeEntry && activeEntry.inner && typeof activeEntry.inner.stop === 'function') {
      try { activeEntry.inner.stop(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
    }
    pending.forEach(function (entry) {
      if (entry._settled || entry === activeEntry) return;
      settle(entry, {
        text: entry.liveText, stopReason: 'user',
        truncated: false, aborted: true, error: null
      });
    });
  }

  function isBusy() { return !!activeEntry; }
  function pending() {
    return queue.filter(function (e) { return !e._settled && !e.started; }).length;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Token helpers, surfaced from the plugin's meta object.
  //   meta()        -> { countTokens, idealMaxContextTokens } | null
  //   count(text)   -> approximate token count (bigram estimate) | null
  //   budget(slack) -> idealMaxContextTokens - slack (default 800)
  //   preload()     -> warm the broker (harmless; no measurable speedup)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function meta() {
    var plugin = grabPlugin();
    if (!plugin) return null;
    try { return plugin({ getMetaObject: true }) || null; } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  function count(text) {
    var m = meta();
    if (!m || typeof m.countTokens !== 'function') return null;
    try { return m.countTokens(String(text || '')); } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  function budget(slack) {
    var m = meta();
    if (!m || typeof m.idealMaxContextTokens !== 'number') return null;
    var s = (slack == null) ? 800 : slack;
    return m.idealMaxContextTokens - s;
  }

  function preload() {
    var plugin = grabPlugin();
    if (!plugin) return;
    try { plugin({ preload: true }); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
  }

  window.weld.stream = {
    attach: attach,
    run: run,
    normalize: normalize,
    stopAll: stopAll,
    isBusy: isBusy,
    pending: pending,
    meta: meta,
    count: count,
    budget: budget,
    preload: preload,
    DEFAULT_CHAT_STOPS: DEFAULT_CHAT_STOPS,
    version: '1.1.0'
  };

  window.weld.stream.attach({ aiTextPlugin: aiTextPlugin });

  return window.weld.stream;
  })();
  // ---- weld-image ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.image) { window.weld.image.setT2i(t2iSource); return window.weld.image; }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.image: Promise-based wrapper around Perchance's text-to-image-plugin.
  // Adds batching, style presets, retry, resolution helpers.
  //
  // The actual t2i function comes from Perchance's text-to-image-plugin,
  // which must be imported in the DSL panel under any alias, e.g.:
  //   t2iSource = the import of text-to-image-plugin
  // The DSL form passes that function into weld.image.setT2i(...).
  // Standalone JS callers must call weld.image.setT2i(fn) themselves.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var t2iFn = null;

  // Resolution presets
  var RESOLUTIONS = {
    square:      '512x512',
    portrait:    '512x768',
    landscape:   '768x512',
    largeSquare: '768x768'
  };

  // Positive-only style presets (Perchance backend ignores negatives)
  var STYLES = {
    photo:      ', photorealistic, sharp focus, detailed, 8k, professional photography',
    cinematic:  ', cinematic shot, dramatic lighting, depth of field, film grain, atmospheric',
    anime:      ', anime style, cel shaded, vibrant, detailed line art',
    painting:   ', oil painting, classical art, brush strokes, painterly, masterpiece',
    digital:    ', digital art, concept art, trending on artstation, highly detailed',
    watercolor: ', watercolor painting, soft edges, paper texture, flowing colors',
    sketch:     ', pencil sketch, hand drawn, graphite, shading, detailed lines',
    lowpoly:    ', low poly 3d render, geometric, isometric, minimalist',
    pixelart:   ', pixel art, 16-bit style, retro game graphics, pixelated',
    cyberpunk:  ', cyberpunk, neon lights, futuristic, blade runner aesthetic, rain'
  };

  function setT2i(fn) {
    t2iFn = fn;
  }

  function getT2i() {
    if (!t2iFn) {
      throw new Error('weld.image: no text-to-image function set. Call weld.image.setT2i(fn) where fn is the imported text-to-image-plugin.');
    }
    return t2iFn;
  }

  function styleNames() { return Object.keys(STYLES); }
  function resolutionNames() { return Object.keys(RESOLUTIONS); }

  function withStyle(prompt, styleName) {
    var suffix = STYLES[styleName] || '';
    return String(prompt) + suffix;
  }

  function withResolution(opts, resName) {
    var res = RESOLUTIONS[resName];
    if (!res) return Object.assign({}, opts);
    var parts = res.split('x');
    return Object.assign({}, opts, { width: parseInt(parts[0], 10), height: parseInt(parts[1], 10) });
  }

  // --- truth-layer helpers (text-to-image-plugin's sharp edges) ---
  // Only four resolutions are accepted by the backend; anything else is
  // rejected. Validate up front with a clear error instead of a silent fail.
  var VALID_WH = { '512x512': 1, '512x768': 1, '768x512': 1, '768x768': 1 };
  function resolutionOf(opts) {
    if (!opts) return null;
    if (opts.resolution && VALID_WH[opts.resolution]) return opts.resolution;
    if (opts.width && opts.height) return opts.width + 'x' + opts.height;
    return null;
  }
  function validateResolution(opts) {
    var wh = resolutionOf(opts);
    if (wh && !VALID_WH[wh]) {
      throw new Error('weld.image: unsupported resolution "' + wh + '". Use one of 512x512, 512x768, 768x512, 768x768 (or a preset: ' + resolutionNames().join('/') + ').');
    }
  }
  function promptText(opts) { return String((opts && (opts.prompt != null ? opts.prompt : opts.text)) || '').trim(); }

  // The awaited t2i result is a BOXED String carrying canvas/dataUrl/inputs.
  // Comparing it with === fails and reading it as text needs coercion.
  // normalizeResult turns it into a plain, predictable object.
  function normalizeResult(data) {
    if (data == null) return { dataUrl: null, canvas: null, inputs: null, text: '' };
    var text = '';
    try { text = String(data); } catch (e) { text = ''; }
    return {
      dataUrl: (data.dataUrl != null) ? String(data.dataUrl) : (/^data:/.test(text) ? text : null),
      canvas: data.canvas || null,
      inputs: data.inputs || null,
      seed: (data.inputs && data.inputs.seed != null) ? data.inputs.seed : (data.seed != null ? data.seed : null),
      text: text,
      raw: data
    };
  }

  // Synchronous embed: returns the iframe HTML for direct insertion
  function embed(opts) {
    return String(getT2i()(opts));
  }

  // Async single generation: resolves with the result data
  function generate(opts) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      // Guard the two silent failure modes up front.
      try {
        validateResolution(opts);
      } catch (e) { reject(e); return; }
      if (!promptText(opts)) {
        reject(new Error('weld.image: empty prompt. text-to-image hangs forever on an empty prompt, so it is rejected here.'));
        return;
      }
      var settled = false;
      var fn = getT2i();
      var enriched = Object.assign({}, opts, {
        onFinish: function(data) {
          if (settled) return;
          settled = true;
          resolve(normalizeResult(data));
        }
      });
      var html;
      try {
        html = String(fn(enriched));
      } catch (e) {
        reject(e);
        return;
      }

      try {
        if (opts && opts.into) {
          var target = typeof opts.into === 'string' ? document.querySelector(opts.into) : opts.into;
          if (target) target.innerHTML = html;
        }
      } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }

      var ms = (opts && opts.timeoutMs) || 120000;
      setTimeout(function() {
        if (!settled) {
          settled = true;
          reject(new Error('weld.image: generation timeout after ' + ms + 'ms'));
        }
      }, ms);
    });
  }

  // Generate N images sequentially with the same prompt (variation via seed)
  function batch(opts, count, onProgress) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      var results = [];
      var i = 0;
      function step() {
        if (i >= count) { resolve(results); return; }
        var cellOpts = Object.assign({}, opts);
        if (cellOpts.seed === undefined || cellOpts.seed === -1) {
          cellOpts.seed = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
        } else if (i > 0) {
          cellOpts.seed = opts.seed + i;
        }
        generate(cellOpts).then(function(data) {
          results.push(data);
          if (onProgress) onProgress(i + 1, count, data);
          i++;
          step();
        }).catch(function(e) {
          results.push({ error: e.message });
          if (onProgress) onProgress(i + 1, count, { error: e.message });
          i++;
          step();
        });
      }
      step();
    });
  }

  // Variations: same opts but different prompts
  function variations(prompts, sharedOpts, onProgress) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      var results = [];
      var i = 0;
      function step() {
        if (i >= prompts.length) { resolve(results); return; }
        var cellOpts = Object.assign({}, sharedOpts, { prompt: prompts[i] });
        generate(cellOpts).then(function(data) {
          results.push(data);
          if (onProgress) onProgress(i + 1, prompts.length, data);
          i++;
          step();
        }).catch(function(e) {
          results.push({ error: e.message, prompt: prompts[i] });
          if (onProgress) onProgress(i + 1, prompts.length, { error: e.message });
          i++;
          step();
        });
      }
      step();
    });
  }

  // Auto-retry on failure with exponential backoff
  function generateWithRetry(opts, maxRetries) {
    maxRetries = maxRetries || 3;
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      var attempt = 0;
      var lastError = null;
      function tryOnce() {
        generate(opts).then(resolve).catch(function(e) {
          lastError = e;
          attempt++;
          if (attempt >= maxRetries) { reject(lastError); return; }
          var backoff = 1000 * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1);
          setTimeout(tryOnce, backoff);
        });
      }
      tryOnce();
    });
  }

  // regenerate(opts): reproduce or vary an image deterministically. With an
  // explicit opts.seed, the same prompt+seed reproduces the same image (the
  // "regenerate at full quality from a saved thumbnail" pattern). Pass
  // opts.vary:true to roll a fresh seed for an alternate take.
  function regenerate(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var next = Object.assign({}, opts);
    if (opts.vary || next.seed == null || next.seed === -1) {
      next.seed = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000000);
    }
    return generate(next).then(function (r) { r.seed = (next.seed != null ? next.seed : r.seed); return r; });
  }

  window.weld.image = {
    setT2i: setT2i,
    withStyle: withStyle,
    withResolution: withResolution,
    styleNames: styleNames,
    resolutionNames: resolutionNames,
    styles: STYLES,
    resolutions: RESOLUTIONS,
    validResolution: function (wh) { return !!VALID_WH[wh]; },
    normalizeResult: normalizeResult,
    embed: embed,
    generate: generate,
    regenerate: regenerate,
    batch: batch,
    variations: variations,
    generateWithRetry: generateWithRetry,
    version: '1.1.0'
  };

  window.weld.image.setT2i(t2iSource);

  return window.weld.image;
  })();
  // ---- weld-crew ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.crew) return window.weld.crew;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.crew: a ReAct agent that lives in the generator and thinks
  // with the user's own model, keeping durable state in the bridge.
  //
  //   var sb = weld.skybridge;            // trigger root.weldSkybridge() first
  //   var a  = weld.crew.create({ workspace: 'quest' });
  //   a.registerTool({ name:'roll', description:'roll dice like 2d6',
  //                    args:{ dice:'string' }, run: function (x){ return roll(x.dice); } });
  //   var out = await a.run('Plan a tavern brawl, roll for initiative.',
  //                         { onStep: function (s){ render(s); } });
  //   // out.answer, out.runId (resume later with a.resume(out.runId))
  //
  // State lives at  agent:<workspace>:<ns>  in skybridge storage:
  //   :mem      long-term memory (array of { id, text, tags, t })
  //   :scratch  the current scratchpad (array of thought strings)
  //   :run:<id> a run record (goal, steps, status, result)
  //   :runs     index of run ids (most-recent-first)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var BUILD = 'crew/2026-06-04.2';

  // ---- storage: lean on skybridge (companion -> persist -> memory), else our own fallback ----
  function makeStore() {
    var sb = window.weld && window.weld.skybridge;
    if (sb && sb.storage && typeof sb.storage.get === 'function') return sb.storage;
    // no bridge at all: tiny in-memory store with the same async shape
    var mem = {};
    return {
      get: function (k) { return Promise.resolve(k in mem ? mem[k] : null); },
      set: function (k, v) { mem[k] = v; return Promise.resolve(true); },
      list: function (prefix) {
        var out = [];
        for (var k in mem) if (mem.hasOwnProperty(k) && k.indexOf(prefix || '') === 0) out.push(k);
        return Promise.resolve(out);
      },
      backend: function () { return 'memory'; }
    };
  }

  function uid(prefix) {
    return (prefix || '') + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
  }

  // ---- robust extraction of a single JSON object from a model reply ----
  // Models wrap JSON in prose or ```json fences. Find the first balanced {...}.
  function extractJSON(text) {
    if (typeof text !== 'string') return null;
    var s = text.replace(/```json/gi, '```').replace(/```/g, '');
    var start = s.indexOf('{');
    while (start !== -1) {
      var depth = 0, inStr = false, esc = false;
      for (var i = start; i < s.length; i++) {
        var c = s.charAt(i);
        if (inStr) {
          if (esc) esc = false;
          else if (c === '\\') esc = true;
          else if (c === '"') inStr = false;
        } else if (c === '"') inStr = true;
        else if (c === '{') depth++;
        else if (c === '}') {
          depth--;
          if (depth === 0) {
            var chunk = s.slice(start, i + 1);
            try { return JSON.parse(chunk); } catch (e) { break; }  // not valid; try next {
          }
        }
      }
      start = s.indexOf('{', start + 1);
    }
    return null;
  }

  // ---- the agent factory ----
  function createCrew(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var workspace = opts.workspace || 'default';
    var maxSteps = opts.maxSteps || 8;
    var extraSystem = opts.system || '';
    var aiOpts = opts.model || {};
    var store = makeStore();
    var tools = {};            // name -> tool spec
    var stopped = false;

    function key(ns, k) { return 'crew:' + workspace + ':' + ns + (k ? (':' + k) : ''); }

    // --- memory ---
    var memory = {
      list: async function () { return (await store.get(key('mem'))) || []; },
      write: async function (text, tags) {
        var all = await memory.list();
        var item = { id: uid('m_'), text: String(text || ''), tags: tags || [], t: Date.now() };
        all.push(item);
        await store.set(key('mem'), all);
        return item.id;
      },
      search: async function (query, tags) {
        var all = await memory.list();
        var q = String(query || '').toLowerCase();
        return all.filter(function (m) {
          var hitQ = !q || (m.text && m.text.toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1);
          var hitT = !tags || !tags.length || (m.tags && tags.some(function (t) { return m.tags.indexOf(t) !== -1; }));
          return hitQ && hitT;
        });
      },
      clear: async function () { await store.set(key('mem'), []); return true; }
    };

    // --- scratchpad (the agent's durable "thoughts") ---
    var scratchpad = {
      read: async function () { return (await store.get(key('scratch'))) || []; },
      write: async function (note) {
        var sp = await scratchpad.read();
        sp.push({ t: Date.now(), note: String(note || '') });
        await store.set(key('scratch'), sp);
        return sp.length;
      },
      clear: async function () { await store.set(key('scratch'), []); return true; }
    };

    // --- run records (resumable) ---
    async function loadRun(id) { return await store.get(key('run', id)); }
    async function saveRun(rec) {
      await store.set(key('run', rec.id), rec);
      var idx = (await store.get(key('runs'))) || [];
      if (idx.indexOf(rec.id) === -1) { idx.unshift(rec.id); await store.set(key('runs'), idx.slice(0, 50)); }
    }
    async function listRuns() {
      var idx = (await store.get(key('runs'))) || [];
      var out = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < idx.length; i++) { var r = await loadRun(idx[i]); if (r) out.push(r); }
      return out;
    }

    // --- tools ---
    function registerTool(spec) {
      if (!spec || !spec.name || typeof spec.run !== 'function') throw new Error('tool needs { name, run }');
      tools[spec.name] = { name: spec.name, description: spec.description || '', args: spec.args || {}, run: spec.run };
      return this;
    }
    function toolList() { return Object.keys(tools).map(function (n) { return tools[n]; }); }

    // built-in tools (need no companion capability beyond storage)
    registerTool({ name: 'think', description: 'Record a private thought/plan. Use to reason before acting.', args: { note: 'string' },
      run: async function (a) { await scratchpad.write(a.note); return 'noted'; } });
    registerTool({ name: 'memory.write', description: 'Save a durable fact to long-term memory.', args: { text: 'string', tags: 'string[] (optional)' },
      run: async function (a) { return { id: await memory.write(a.text, a.tags) }; } });
    registerTool({ name: 'memory.search', description: 'Search long-term memory by text and/or tags.', args: { query: 'string (optional)', tags: 'string[] (optional)' },
      run: async function (a) { return await memory.search(a.query, a.tags); } });
    registerTool({ name: 'memory.list', description: 'List everything in long-term memory.', args: {},
