      run: async function () { return await memory.list(); } });
    registerTool({ name: 'time.now', description: 'Current date and time (ISO).', args: {},
      run: async function () { return new Date().toISOString(); } });
    // web.fetch: companion 'fetch' capability if present, else weld.fetch (superFetch
    // proxy, CORS-free) when the host imported it, else reports unavailable.
    registerTool({ name: 'web.fetch', description: 'Fetch a URL. Uses the companion web-access capability if present, else weld.fetch (superFetch) if the host imported weld-fetch-plugin.', args: { url: 'string', method: 'string (optional)' },
      run: async function (a) {
        var sb = window.weld && window.weld.skybridge;
        if (sb && sb.connected && typeof sb.has === 'function' && sb.has('fetch') && typeof sb.request === 'function') {
          return await sb.request('fetch', { url: a.url, method: a.method || 'GET' });
        }
        var wf = window.weld && window.weld.fetch;
        if (wf && typeof wf.request === 'function') {
          try {
            var res = await wf.request(a.url, { method: a.method || 'GET' });
            var body = '';
            try { body = await res.text(); } catch (e) {}
            if (typeof body === 'string' && body.length > 8000) body = body.slice(0, 8000) + '\u2026[truncated]';
            return { ok: !!res.ok, status: res.status, url: res.url, via: res.via, body: body };
          } catch (e) {
            return { ok: false, reason: 'weld.fetch error: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : String(e)) };
          }
        }
        return { ok: false, reason: 'web access unavailable (no companion fetch capability, and weld.fetch not imported)' };
      } });

    if (opts.tools && opts.tools.length) opts.tools.forEach(registerTool);

    // --- reasoner: own model via the bridge, or a caller-supplied function ---
    async function reason(prompt, system) {
      if (typeof opts.reason === 'function') return await opts.reason(prompt, system);
      var sb = window.weld && window.weld.skybridge;
      if (sb && sb.connected && typeof sb.has === 'function' && sb.has('ai') && typeof sb.ai === 'function') {
        var aiArgs = { system: system };
        for (var k in aiOpts) if (aiOpts.hasOwnProperty(k)) aiArgs[k] = aiOpts[k];
        var r = await sb.ai(prompt, aiArgs);
        if (r && r.ok) return r.value;
        throw new Error('model call failed: ' + (r && r.reason ? r.reason : 'unknown'));
      }
      throw new Error('no model available -- configure your own model in Weld Companion, or pass opts.reason');
    }

    function toolDocs() {
      return toolList().map(function (t) {
        var argKeys = Object.keys(t.args || {});
        var argStr = argKeys.length ? argKeys.map(function (k) { return k + ': ' + t.args[k]; }).join(', ') : 'none';
        return '- ' + t.name + ' -- ' + t.description + '  (args: ' + argStr + ')';
      }).join('\n');
    }

    function systemPrompt(memText, scratchText) {
      return [
        'You are weld.crew, a tool-using assistant running inside a Perchance generator.',
        extraSystem,
        '',
        'Work in small steps. On EACH step reply with ONE JSON object and nothing else:',
        '  to use a tool:   { "thought": "...", "tool": "<name>", "args": { ... } }',
        '  to finish:       { "thought": "...", "final": "<your answer to the goal>" }',
        '',
        'Available tools:',
        toolDocs(),
        '',
        'Long-term memory (durable across runs):',
        (memText || '(empty)'),
        '',
        'Scratchpad (your notes this run):',
        (scratchText || '(empty)')
      ].join('\n');
    }

    function stop() { stopped = true; }

    // --- the ReAct loop ---
    async function run(goal, runOpts) {
      runOpts = runOpts || {};
      stopped = false;
      var onStep = typeof runOpts.onStep === 'function' ? runOpts.onStep : function () {};
      var cap = runOpts.maxSteps || maxSteps;

      var rec;
      if (runOpts.runId) {
        rec = await loadRun(runOpts.runId);
        if (!rec) return { ok: false, reason: 'run-not-found', runId: runOpts.runId };
        rec.status = 'running';
      } else {
        rec = { id: uid('r_'), goal: String(goal || ''), status: 'running', steps: [], result: null, t: Date.now() };
        await scratchpad.clear();
      }
      await saveRun(rec);
      onStep({ type: 'start', runId: rec.id, goal: rec.goal });

      while (rec.steps.length < cap) {
        if (stopped) { rec.status = 'stopped'; await saveRun(rec); return { ok: false, reason: 'stopped', runId: rec.id, steps: rec.steps }; }

        var mem = await memory.list();
        var memText = mem.slice(-12).map(function (m) { return '- ' + m.text + (m.tags && m.tags.length ? '  [' + m.tags.join(',') + ']' : ''); }).join('\n');
        var sp = await scratchpad.read();
        var scratchText = sp.slice(-12).map(function (x) { return '- ' + x.note; }).join('\n');

        var transcript = 'GOAL: ' + rec.goal + '\n\n' + rec.steps.map(function (s, i) {
          var line = '[step ' + (i + 1) + '] thought: ' + (s.thought || '');
          if (s.tool) line += '\naction: ' + s.tool + ' ' + JSON.stringify(s.args || {}) + '\nobservation: ' + JSON.stringify(s.observation);
          return line;
        }).join('\n\n');
        transcript += '\n\nReply with the next JSON step.';

        var sysText = systemPrompt(memText, scratchText);
        onStep({ type: 'prompt', system: sysText, transcript: transcript, step: rec.steps.length + 1 });
        var reply;
        try { reply = await reason(transcript, sysText); }
        catch (e) { rec.status = 'error'; rec.result = String(e && e.message || e); await saveRun(rec); onStep({ type: 'error', error: rec.result }); return { ok: false, reason: 'reason-failed', error: rec.result, runId: rec.id }; }

        onStep({ type: 'raw', reply: String(reply) });
        var parsed = extractJSON(reply);
        if (!parsed) {
          // model answered in prose; treat as the final answer
          rec.status = 'done'; rec.result = String(reply).trim(); await saveRun(rec);
          onStep({ type: 'final', answer: rec.result });
          return { ok: true, answer: rec.result, runId: rec.id, steps: rec.steps };
        }

        var step = { thought: parsed.thought || '', tool: null, args: null, observation: null, t: Date.now() };
        if (parsed.thought) { await scratchpad.write(parsed.thought); onStep({ type: 'thought', thought: parsed.thought }); }

        if (typeof parsed.final !== 'undefined') {
          rec.steps.push(step); rec.status = 'done'; rec.result = String(parsed.final); await saveRun(rec);
          onStep({ type: 'final', answer: rec.result });
          return { ok: true, answer: rec.result, runId: rec.id, steps: rec.steps };
        }

        var name = parsed.tool;
        var tool = name && tools[name];
        if (!tool) {
          step.tool = name; step.observation = { error: 'unknown tool: ' + name + '. Pick from: ' + Object.keys(tools).join(', ') };
        } else {
          step.tool = name; step.args = parsed.args || {};
          onStep({ type: 'action', tool: name, args: step.args });
          try { step.observation = await tool.run(step.args || {}); }
          catch (e) { step.observation = { error: String(e && e.message || e) }; }
        }
        onStep({ type: 'observation', tool: step.tool, observation: step.observation });
        rec.steps.push(step);
        await saveRun(rec);   // persist every step -> durable + resumable
      }

      rec.status = 'maxsteps'; await saveRun(rec);
      onStep({ type: 'maxsteps', steps: rec.steps.length });
      return { ok: false, reason: 'maxsteps', runId: rec.id, steps: rec.steps };
    }

    return {
      workspace: workspace,
      run: run,
      resume: async function (runId, runOpts) {
        var rec = await loadRun(runId);
        if (!rec) return { ok: false, reason: 'run-not-found' };
        var o = runOpts || {}; o.runId = runId;
        return await run(rec.goal, o);
      },
      stop: stop,
      registerTool: registerTool,
      tools: toolList,
      memory: memory,
      scratchpad: scratchpad,
      runs: listRuns,
      getRun: loadRun,
      backend: function () { return store.backend ? store.backend() : 'unknown'; }
    };
  }

  window.weld.crew = {
    create: createCrew,
    extractJSON: extractJSON,   // exported for tests / reuse
    version: '1.0.1',
    build: BUILD
  };

  return window.weld.crew;
  })();
  // ---- weld-swarm ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.swarm) return window.weld.swarm;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.swarm: the generator-side half of orchestration. The heavy routing
  // logic is shared with the companion's orchestrator core; here every peer
  // runs it locally over a broadcast transport, so the tab that calls
  // dispatch() acts as the orchestrator for that exchange.
  //
  //   // worker tab (a generator that imports weld.crew):
  //   var a = weld.crew.create({ workspace: 'crew' });
  //   weld.swarm.create({ role: 'worker' }).serve(function (task) { return a.run(task.goal); });
  //
  //   // user/driver tab (the chat):
  //   var crew = weld.swarm.create({ role: 'user' });
  //   var results = await crew.dispatchMany(subtasks, { concurrency: 3 });
  //
  // message: { id, from, to, type, payload, corr?, t }   to = peerId | role | '*'
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var BUILD = 'swarm/2026-06-05.1';

  function uid(p) { return (p || 'm_') + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7); }

  // ---- transport: { send(msg), onMessage(fn) }, auto-selected or injected ----
  function pickTransport(opts) {
    if (opts && opts.transport) return opts.transport;
    var channel = (opts && opts.channel) || 'weld.swarm';
    var sb = window.weld && window.weld.skybridge;
    // 1) companion bus (cross-generator, cross-tab); present once the companion exposes it
    if (sb && sb.connected && typeof sb.has === 'function' && sb.has('bus') && sb.bus && typeof sb.bus.publish === 'function' && typeof sb.bus.subscribe === 'function') {
      return { kind: 'bus', send: function (m) { sb.bus.publish(channel, m); }, onMessage: function (fn) { return sb.bus.subscribe(channel, fn); } };
    }
    // 2) weld.sync (same-origin tabs of one generator)
    if (window.weld && window.weld.sync && typeof window.weld.sync.create === 'function') {
      var s = window.weld.sync.create({ namespace: channel });
      return { kind: 'sync', send: function (m) { s.broadcast('m', m); }, onMessage: function (fn) { s.subscribe('m', fn); }, _sync: s };
    }
    // 3) in-memory (single tab / tests / standalone)
    var subs = [];
    return { kind: 'memory', send: function (m) { setTimeout(function () { subs.forEach(function (fn) { try { fn(m); } catch (e) {} }); }, 0); }, onMessage: function (fn) { subs.push(fn); } };
  }

  function createSwarm(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var role = opts.role || 'worker';
    var now = opts.now || Date.now;
    var TTL = opts.peerTTL || 8000;
    var selfId = opts.id || uid(role + '_');
    var transport = pickTransport(opts);

    var peers = {};            // peerId -> { peerId, role, caps, lastSeen }
    var handlers = {};         // type -> [ fn]
    var pending = {};          // corr -> { resolve, reject, timer }

    function emit(type, msg) { (handlers[type] || []).forEach(function (f) { try { f(msg); } catch (e) {} }); }
    function on(type, fn) { (handlers[type] = handlers[type] || []).push(fn); return function () { handlers[type] = handlers[type].filter(function (f) { return f !== fn; }); }; }
    function touch(id, r, caps) { peers[id] = { peerId: id, role: r || (peers[id] && peers[id].role), caps: caps || (peers[id] && peers[id].caps) || [], lastSeen: now() }; }
    function livePeers(r) { var t = now(); return Object.keys(peers).map(function (k) { return peers[k]; }).filter(function (p) { return (t - p.lastSeen) < TTL && (!r || p.role === r); }); }

    function handleIncoming(msg) {
      if (!msg || !msg.type || msg.from === selfId) return;
      if (msg.type === 'register') { touch(msg.from, msg.role, msg.payload && msg.payload.caps); emit('peer', peers[msg.from]); if (!msg._reply) raw('register', { caps: opts.caps || [] }, '*', { _reply: true }); return; }
      if (msg.type === 'heartbeat') { touch(msg.from, msg.role); return; }
      if (msg.type === 'bye') { delete peers[msg.from]; emit('peerleave', { peerId: msg.from }); return; }
      if (peers[msg.from]) peers[msg.from].lastSeen = now();
      if (msg.type === 'result' && msg.corr && pending[msg.corr]) { var p = pending[msg.corr]; clearTimeout(p.timer); delete pending[msg.corr]; p.resolve(msg.payload); return; }
      // deliver to this peer's handlers only if addressed to it, its role, or broadcast
      if (msg.to === selfId || msg.to === role || msg.to === '*' || msg.to == null) { emit(msg.type, msg); emit('message', msg); }
    }
    transport.onMessage(handleIncoming);

    function raw(type, payload, to, extra) {
      var msg = { id: uid(), from: selfId, to: to == null ? '*' : to, role: role, type: type, payload: payload, t: now() };
      if (extra) for (var k in extra) if (extra.hasOwnProperty(k)) msg[k] = extra[k];
      transport.send(msg);
      return msg.id;
    }
    function send(to, type, payload, extra) { return raw(type, payload, to, extra); }

    // request/response: assign one task to one worker, await its 'result'
    function dispatch(workerId, task, timeoutMs) {
      return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
        var corr = uid('c_');
        var timer = setTimeout(function () { delete pending[corr]; reject(new Error('worker timeout: ' + workerId)); }, timeoutMs || 30000);
        pending[corr] = { resolve: resolve, reject: reject, timer: timer };
        raw('task', task, workerId, { corr: corr });
      });
    }

    // fan tasks out across live workers with bounded concurrency -> results in order.
    // Resilient: re-queries LIVE workers each cycle (so tabs that wake/recover rejoin and
    // pruned/frozen ones drop out), and reassigns a timed-out or failed task to a different
    // live worker up to `attempts` times, so one asleep tab doesn't lose its subtask.
    function dispatchMany(tasks, o) {
      o = o || {};
      var attempts = o.attempts || 3;
      var timeoutMs = o.timeoutMs || 30000;
      function live() { return livePeers('worker'); }
      if (!live().length) return Promise.reject(new Error('no workers available'));
      var results = new Array(tasks.length); var done = 0; var next = 0; var active = 0; var rr = 0;
      return new Promise(function (resolve) {
        function settle(idx, val) { results[idx] = val; done++; active--; if (done === tasks.length) resolve(results); else pump(); }
        function attempt(idx, tries) {
          var ws = live();
          if (!ws.length) { return settle(idx, { error: 'no workers available' }); }
          var w = ws[(rr++) % ws.length];
          dispatch(w.peerId, tasks[idx], timeoutMs).then(
            function (r) { settle(idx, r); },
            function (e) {
              // worker timed out / unreachable (e.g. a backgrounded, frozen tab) -> try another
              if (tries + 1 < attempts && live().length) return attempt(idx, tries + 1);
              settle(idx, { error: String(e && e.message || e) });
            });
        }
        function pump() {
          var limit = o.concurrency || live().length || 1;
          while (active < limit && next < tasks.length) {
            (function (idx) { active++; attempt(idx, 0); })(next++);
          }
        }
        pump();
      });
    }

    // worker convenience: auto-answer 'task' messages by running handler(payload) -> result
    var served = null;        // single active task subscription (serve is idempotent, never stacks)
    var handledCorrs = {};    // corr -> ts; drop duplicate deliveries of the same task
    function serve(handler) {
      if (served) { try { served(); } catch (e) {} }   // replace any prior handler -> no double-handling
      served = on('task', async function (msg) {
        if (!msg.corr) return;
        if (handledCorrs[msg.corr]) return;             // already handled this task -> ignore the duplicate
        handledCorrs[msg.corr] = now();
        var keys = Object.keys(handledCorrs); if (keys.length > 1024) { delete handledCorrs[keys[0]]; }
        var out;
        try { out = await handler(msg.payload, msg); } catch (e) { out = { error: String(e && e.message || e) }; }
        raw('result', out, msg.from, { corr: msg.corr });
      });
      return api;
    }

    // presence: announce, heartbeat, prune
    raw('register', { caps: opts.caps || [] }, '*');
    var hbMs = opts.heartbeatMs || 3000;
    var hbTimer = (opts.heartbeat === false) ? null : setInterval(function () { raw('heartbeat'); }, hbMs);
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.addEventListener) try { window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function () { raw('bye'); }); } catch (e) {}

    function leave() { if (hbTimer) clearInterval(hbTimer); raw('bye'); }

    var api = {
      id: selfId, role: role, transport: transport.kind,
      on: on, send: send,
      peers: function () { return livePeers(); },
      workers: function () { return livePeers('worker'); },
      users: function () { return livePeers('user'); },
      dispatch: dispatch, dispatchMany: dispatchMany,
      serve: serve, leave: leave,
      _ingest: handleIncoming   // exposed for tests
    };
    return api;
  }

  window.weld.swarm = {
    create: createSwarm,
    version: '1.2.1',
    build: BUILD
  };

  return window.weld.swarm;
  })();

  // ---- weld-markdown ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.markdown) return window.weld.markdown;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // HTML escape: the foundation of safety
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function escapeHtml(s) {
    return String(s)
      .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
      .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
      .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
      .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
      .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // URL sanitization: reject javascript:, vbscript:, data: (except images)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var SAFE_URL_RE = /^(?:https?:|mailto:|tel:|\/|#|\.\/|\.\.\/|[a-zA-Z0-9_\-]+\.)/;
  var SAFE_IMG_URL_RE = /^(?:https?:|data:image\/(?:png|jpe?g|gif|webp|svg\+xml);|\/|\.\/|\.\.\/)/;

  function safeUrl(url, forImg) {
    url = String(url).trim();
    var re = forImg ? SAFE_IMG_URL_RE : SAFE_URL_RE;
    return re.test(url) ? url : '#';
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Inline formatting: bold, italic, strikethrough, applied to text
  // where no HTML has been injected yet
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function applyFormatting(text) {
    // Bold first (longer marker wins)
    text = text.replace(/\*\*([^*\n]+)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
    text = text.replace(/__([^_\n]+)__/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
    // Italic (single marker)
    text = text.replace(/(^|[^*])\*([^*\n]+)\*(?!\*)/g, '$1<em>$2</em>');
    text = text.replace(/(^|[^_])_([^_\n]+)_(?!_)/g, '$1<em>$2</em>');
    // Strikethrough
    text = text.replace(/~~([^~\n]+)~~/g, '<del>$1</del>');
    return text;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Inline parsing: code, images, links, auto-links, then formatting
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function parseInline(text) {
    var slots = [];
    function slot(html) {
      slots.push(html);
      return '\u0001S' + (slots.length - 1) + '\u0001';
    }

    // 1. Code spans: extract first, content escaped, no further processing
    text = text.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, function(_, code) {
      return slot('<code>' + escapeHtml(code) + '</code>');
    });

    // 2. Images:  exclamation + label-in-brackets + paren-url
    text = text.replace(/!\[([^\]]*)\]\(([^)\s]+)(?:\s+"([^"]*)")?\)/g, function(_, alt, url, title) {
      var t = title ? ' title="' + escapeHtml(title) + '"' : '';
      return slot('<img src="' + safeUrl(url, true) + '" alt="' + escapeHtml(alt) + '"' + t + '>');
    });

    // 3. Links: label-in-brackets followed by paren-url
    text = text.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)\s]+)(?:\s+"([^"]*)")?\)/g, function(_, label, url, title) {
      var t = title ? ' title="' + escapeHtml(title) + '"' : '';
      // Allow inline formatting inside link label
      var inner = applyFormatting(escapeHtml(label));
      return slot('<a href="' + safeUrl(url) + '"' + t + ' target="_blank" rel="noopener">' + inner + '</a>');
    });

    // 4. Auto-links: bare URLs (not already inside a slot)
    text = text.replace(/\b(https?:\/\/[^\s<]+[^\s<.,;:?!])/g, function(url) {
      return slot('<a href="' + safeUrl(url) + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">' + escapeHtml(url) + '</a>');
    });

    // 5. Escape any remaining HTML in the plain text
    text = escapeHtml(text);

    // 6. Apply bold/italic/strikethrough on the now-safe text
    text = applyFormatting(text);

    // 7. Restore slot placeholders
    text = text.replace(/\u0001S(\d+)\u0001/g, function(_, idx) {
      return slots[parseInt(idx, 10)];
    });

    return text;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Block-level parsing
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function render(input, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    if (typeof input !== 'string') input = String(input == null ? '' : input);

    // Normalize line endings
    input = input.replace(/\r\n?/g, '\n');

    var lines = input.split('\n');
    var out = [];
    var i = 0;

    while (i < lines.length) {
      var line = lines[i];

      // Fenced code block: ``` or ~~~
      var fence = line.match(/^(```|~~~)\s*([a-zA-Z0-9_-]*)\s*$/);
      if (fence) {
        var marker = fence[1];
        var lang = fence[2] || '';
        i++;
        var code = [];
        while (i < lines.length && lines[i].indexOf(marker) !== 0) {
          code.push(lines[i]);
          i++;
        }
        i++;
        var langAttr = lang ? ' class="language-' + escapeHtml(lang) + '"' : '';
        out.push('<pre><code' + langAttr + '>' + escapeHtml(code.join('\n')) + '</code></pre>');
        continue;
      }

      // ATX header: # to ######
      var hdr = line.match(/^(#{1,6})\s+(.+)$/);
      if (hdr) {
        var n = hdr[1].length;
        out.push('<h' + n + '>' + parseInline(hdr[2]) + '</h' + n + '>');
        i++;
        continue;
      }

      // Horizontal rule
      if (/^\s*([-*_])\s*\1\s*\1[\s\1]*$/.test(line)) {
        out.push('<hr>');
        i++;
        continue;
      }

      // Blockquote
      if (line.charAt(0) === '>') {
        var quote = [];
        while (i < lines.length && lines[i].charAt(0) === '>') {
          quote.push(lines[i].replace(/^>\s?/, ''));
          i++;
        }
        out.push('<blockquote>' + render(quote.join('\n')) + '</blockquote>');
        continue;
      }

      // Unordered list
      if (/^\s*[-*+]\s+/.test(line)) {
        var items = [];
        while (i < lines.length && /^\s*[-*+]\s+/.test(lines[i])) {
          items.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*[-*+]\s+/, ''));
          i++;
        }
        out.push('<ul>' + items.map(function(it) { return '<li>' + parseInline(it) + '</li>'; }).join('') + '</ul>');
        continue;
      }

      // Ordered list
      if (/^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(line)) {
        var oitems = [];
        while (i < lines.length && /^\s*\d+\.\s+/.test(lines[i])) {
          oitems.push(lines[i].replace(/^\s*\d+\.\s+/, ''));
          i++;
        }
        out.push('<ol>' + oitems.map(function(it) { return '<li>' + parseInline(it) + '</li>'; }).join('') + '</ol>');
        continue;
      }

      // Empty line: skip
      if (line.trim() === '') {
        i++;
        continue;
      }

      // Paragraph: gather consecutive non-empty lines
      var para = [ line];
      i++;
      while (i < lines.length && lines[i].trim() !== '' && !/^(#{1,6}\s|```|~~~|>|\s*[-*+]\s|\s*\d+\.\s)/.test(lines[i])) {
        para.push(lines[i]);
        i++;
      }
      out.push('<p>' + parseInline(para.join(' ')) + '</p>');
    }

    return out.join('\n');
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Convenience: render into an element
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function renderInto(el, input, opts) {
    if (typeof el === 'string') el = document.querySelector(el);
    if (!el) throw new Error('weld.markdown.renderInto: element not found');
    el.innerHTML = render(input, opts);
    return el;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Sanitize an arbitrary HTML string: only allow safe tags/attrs
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var ALLOWED_TAGS = {
    p: 1, br: 1, hr: 1,
    h1: 1, h2: 1, h3: 1, h4: 1, h5: 1, h6: 1,
    strong: 1, em: 1, del: 1, b: 1, i: 1, u: 1, s: 1,
    ul: 1, ol: 1, li: 1,
    blockquote: 1, pre: 1, code: 1,
    a: 1, img: 1,
    table: 1, thead: 1, tbody: 1, tr: 1, th: 1, td: 1,
    div: 1, span: 1
  };
  var ALLOWED_ATTRS = {
    a: { href: 1, title: 1, target: 1, rel: 1 },
    img: { src: 1, alt: 1, title: 1, width: 1, height: 1 },
    '*': { 'class': 1 }
  };

  function sanitize(html) {
    var tmp = document.createElement('template');
    tmp.innerHTML = String(html);
    walk(tmp.content);
    return tmp.innerHTML;
  }

  function walk(node) {
    var children = Array.prototype.slice.call(node.childNodes);
    for (var i = 0; i < children.length; i++) {
      var child = children[i];
      if (child.nodeType === 1) { // element
        var tag = child.tagName.toLowerCase();
        if (!ALLOWED_TAGS[tag]) {
          // Replace with its text content
          var text = document.createTextNode(child.textContent);
          child.parentNode.replaceChild(text, child);
          continue;
        }
        // Strip unsafe attributes
        var attrs = Array.prototype.slice.call(child.attributes);
        for (var j = 0; j < attrs.length; j++) {
          var attr = attrs[j];
          var tagAllowed = ALLOWED_ATTRS[tag] && ALLOWED_ATTRS[tag][attr.name];
          var globalAllowed = ALLOWED_ATTRS['*'][attr.name];
          if (!tagAllowed && !globalAllowed) {
            child.removeAttribute(attr.name);
            continue;
          }
          // URL attrs: sanitize
          if (attr.name === 'href') child.setAttribute('href', safeUrl(attr.value));
          if (attr.name === 'src') {
            var isImg = tag === 'img';
            child.setAttribute('src', safeUrl(attr.value, isImg));
          }
        }
        walk(child);
      }
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // API
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  window.weld.markdown = {
    render: render,
    renderInto: renderInto,
    sanitize: sanitize,
    parseInline: parseInline,
    escapeHtml: escapeHtml,
    safeUrl: safeUrl,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.markdown;


  })();

  // ---- weld-dice ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.dice) return window.weld.dice;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.dice: the randomness primitives Perchance generators reach for,
  // in one tested place. Dice-notation roller with keep/drop and
  // advantage, weighted picks, decks that draw without replacement, and
  // a seedable RNG so a generator can be made reproducible. No model, no
  // DOM, no dependencies.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  // mulberry32: tiny, fast, seedable PRNG. Returns a function -> [0,1).
  function mulberry32(seed) {
    var a = seed >>> 0;
    return function () {
      a |= 0; a = (a + 0x6D2B79F5) | 0;
      var t = Math.imul(a ^ (a >>> 15), 1 | a);
      t = (t + Math.imul(t ^ (t >>> 7), 61 | t)) ^ t;
      return ((t ^ (t >>> 14)) >>> 0) / 4294967296;
    };
  }

  function hashSeed(input) {
    var str = String(input);
    var h = 2166136261 >>> 0;
    for (var i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
      h ^= str.charCodeAt(i);
      h = Math.imul(h, 16777619);
    }
    return h >>> 0;
  }

  // The default stream uses Math.random; rng(seed) returns a seeded one.
  var defaultRand = Math.random;

  function makeRng(seed) {
    var s = (typeof seed === 'number') ? seed : hashSeed(seed);
    var fn = mulberry32(s);
    return {
      next: fn,
      int: function (min, max) { return Math.floor(fn() * (max - min + 1)) + min; },
      pick: function (arr) { return arr[Math.floor(fn() * arr.length)]; },
      bool: function (p) { return fn() < (p == null ? 0.5 : p); }
    };
  }

  function randFor(opts) {
    if (opts && opts.rng && typeof opts.rng.next === 'function') return opts.rng.next;
    if (opts && typeof opts.rand === 'function') return opts.rand;
    if (opts && opts.seed != null) return makeRng(opts.seed).next;
    return defaultRand;
  }

  function rollDie(sides, rand) { return Math.floor(rand() * sides) + 1; }

  // Parse and evaluate dice notation. Supports:
  //   NdS            e.g. 3d6
  //   dS             single die, e.g. d20
  //   +N / -N        flat modifiers anywhere
  //   khN / klN      keep highest / lowest N of the dice
  //   dhN / dlN      drop highest / lowest N
  //   !              exploding dice (reroll+add on max)
  //   "adv" / "dis"  shorthand for 2d20kh1 / 2d20kl1
  // Returns { total, rolls, kept, notation }.
  function roll(notation, opts) {
    var rand = randFor(opts);
    var spec = String(notation == null ? '' : notation).trim().toLowerCase();
    if (spec === 'adv') spec = '2d20kh1';
    else if (spec === 'dis') spec = '2d20kl1';

    var total = 0;
    var allRolls = [];
    var keptAll = [];

    // Split into additive terms, keeping their signs.
    var terms = spec.replace(/\s+/g, '').match(/[+-]?[^+-]+/g) || [];
    for (var t = 0; t < terms.length; t++) {
      var term = terms[t];
      var sign = 1;
      if (term.charAt(0) === '+') term = term.slice(1);
      else if (term.charAt(0) === '-') { sign = -1; term = term.slice(1); }

      var dieMatch = term.match(/^(\d*)d(\d+)(!?)((?:k[hl]\d+|d[hl]\d+)?)$/);
      if (dieMatch) {
        var n = dieMatch[1] === '' ? 1 : parseInt(dieMatch[1], 10);
        var sides = parseInt(dieMatch[2], 10);
        var explode = dieMatch[3] === '!';
        var mod = dieMatch[4];
        var rolls = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) {
          var r = rollDie(sides, rand);
          rolls.push(r);
          if (explode) {
            var guard = 0;
            while (r === sides && guard < 50) { r = rollDie(sides, rand); rolls.push(r); guard += 1; }
          }
        }
        allRolls = allRolls.concat(rolls);

        var kept = rolls.slice();
        if (mod) {
          var keep = mod.charAt(0) === 'k';
          var high = mod.charAt(1) === 'h';
          var count = parseInt(mod.slice(2), 10);
          var sorted = rolls.slice().sort(function (a, b) { return b - a; }); // desc
          if (keep) kept = high ? sorted.slice(0, count) : sorted.slice(sorted.length - count);
          else kept = high ? sorted.slice(count) : sorted.slice(0, sorted.length - count);
        }
        keptAll = keptAll.concat(kept);
        var sum = kept.reduce(function (a, b) { return a + b; }, 0);
        total += sign * sum;
      } else if (/^\d+$/.test(term)) {
        total += sign * parseInt(term, 10);
      }
      // Unknown terms are ignored rather than throwing.
    }

    return { total: total, rolls: allRolls, kept: keptAll, notation: String(notation) };
  }

  // Just the number.
  function rollTotal(notation, opts) { return roll(notation, opts).total; }

  // Uniform integer in [min, max] inclusive.
  function between(min, max, opts) {
    var rand = randFor(opts);
    return Math.floor(rand() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
  }

  // Weighted pick. entries: array of { value, weight } OR a plain object
  // { value: weight, ... }. Returns the chosen value.
  function weighted(entries, opts) {
    var rand = randFor(opts);
    var list = [];
    if (Array.isArray(entries)) {
      list = entries.map(function (e) {
        if (e && typeof e === 'object' && 'weight' in e) return { value: e.value, weight: Math.max(0, +e.weight || 0) };
        return { value: e, weight: 1 };
      });
    } else if (entries && typeof entries === 'object') {
      list = Object.keys(entries).map(function (k) { return { value: k, weight: Math.max(0, +entries[k] || 0) }; });
    }
    var total = list.reduce(function (a, e) { return a + e.weight; }, 0);
    if (total <= 0) return undefined;
    var r = rand() * total;
    for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
      r -= list[i].weight;
      if (r < 0) return list[i].value;
    }
    return list[list.length - 1].value;
  }

  function pick(arr, opts) {
    if (!arr || !arr.length) return undefined;
    var rand = randFor(opts);
    return arr[Math.floor(rand() * arr.length)];
  }

  // Fisher-Yates shuffle (returns a new array).
  function shuffle(arr, opts) {
    var rand = randFor(opts);
    var a = arr.slice();
    for (var i = a.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
      var j = Math.floor(rand() * (i + 1));
      var tmp = a[i]; a[i] = a[j]; a[j] = tmp;
    }
    return a;
  }

  // Sample k distinct items (draw without replacement, single shot).
  function sample(arr, k, opts) {
    return shuffle(arr, opts).slice(0, k);
  }

  // A deck: draws without replacement until empty, then optionally reshuffles.
  // deck(items, { seed, reshuffle }) -> { draw, drawN, remaining, reset, size }
  function deck(items, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var rand = randFor(opts);
    var source = (items || []).slice();
    var pile = shuffle(source, { rand: rand });

    function draw() {
      if (!pile.length) {
        if (opts.reshuffle) pile = shuffle(source, { rand: rand });
        else return undefined;
      }
      return pile.shift();
    }
    function drawN(n) {
      var out = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        var c = draw();
        if (c === undefined) break;
        out.push(c);
      }
      return out;
    }
    return {
      draw: draw,
      drawN: drawN,
      remaining: function () { return pile.length; },
      reset: function () { pile = shuffle(source, { rand: rand }); },
      size: function () { return source.length; }
    };
  }

  window.weld.dice = {
    roll: roll,
    rollTotal: rollTotal,
    between: between,
    weighted: weighted,
    pick: pick,
    shuffle: shuffle,
    sample: sample,
    deck: deck,
    rng: makeRng,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.dice;

  })();

  // ---- weld-toast ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.toast) return window.weld.toast;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // CSS injection (once)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function injectCss() {
    if (window.__weldToastCss) return;
    window.__weldToastCss = true;
    var s = document.createElement('style');
    s.textContent =
      '.weld-toast-host{position:fixed;z-index:9999;display:flex;flex-direction:column;' +
        'gap:8px;pointer-events:none;font:14px system-ui,sans-serif;}' +
      '.weld-toast-host.top-right{top:20px;right:20px;align-items:flex-end;}' +
      '.weld-toast-host.top-left{top:20px;left:20px;align-items:flex-start;}' +
      '.weld-toast-host.top-center{top:20px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);align-items:center;}' +
      '.weld-toast-host.bottom-right{bottom:20px;right:20px;align-items:flex-end;}' +
      '.weld-toast-host.bottom-left{bottom:20px;left:20px;align-items:flex-start;}' +
      '.weld-toast-host.bottom-center{bottom:20px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);align-items:center;}' +
      '.weld-toast{pointer-events:auto;min-width:240px;max-width:360px;' +
        'padding:12px 16px;background:var(--weld-surface,#161b22);' +
        'border:1px solid var(--weld-border,rgba(255,255,255,0.10));border-radius:6px;' +
        'box-shadow:0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);color:var(--weld-ink,#e6edf3);' +
        'display:flex;gap:10px;align-items:flex-start;line-height:1.4;' +
        'transform:translateX(20px);opacity:0;transition:transform 220ms,opacity 220ms;}' +
      '.weld-toast.shown{transform:translateX(0);opacity:1;}' +
      '.weld-toast .weld-toast-icon{flex:0 0 18px;height:18px;border-radius:50%;margin-top:1px;' +
        'display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font:600 11px monospace;color:#fff;}' +
      '.weld-toast.info  .weld-toast-icon{background:#4493f8;}' +
      '.weld-toast.success .weld-toast-icon{background:#3fb950;}' +
      '.weld-toast.warn  .weld-toast-icon{background:#d29922;}' +
      '.weld-toast.error .weld-toast-icon{background:#f85149;}' +
      '.weld-toast .weld-toast-msg{flex:1;font-size:13px;word-wrap:break-word;}' +
      '.weld-toast .weld-toast-close{cursor:pointer;color:var(--weld-muted,#7d8590);' +
        'font-size:16px;line-height:1;background:none;border:none;padding:0;margin-left:6px;}' +
      '.weld-toast .weld-toast-close:hover{color:var(--weld-ink,#e6edf3);}' +
      '.weld-toast-backdrop{position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.5);z-index:9998;' +
        'display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font:14px system-ui,sans-serif;' +
        'opacity:0;transition:opacity 180ms;}' +
      '.weld-toast-backdrop.shown{opacity:1;}' +
      '.weld-toast-modal{background:var(--weld-surface,#161b22);' +
        'border:1px solid var(--weld-border,rgba(255,255,255,0.10));border-radius:8px;' +
        'padding:24px;min-width:320px;max-width:480px;' +
        'color:var(--weld-ink,#e6edf3);box-shadow:0 16px 64px rgba(0,0,0,0.6);' +
        'transform:scale(0.96);transition:transform 180ms;}' +
      '.weld-toast-backdrop.shown .weld-toast-modal{transform:scale(1);}' +
      '.weld-toast-modal h4{font-size:15px;font-weight:600;margin-bottom:10px;}' +
      '.weld-toast-modal p{font-size:13px;color:var(--weld-ink,#e6edf3);margin-bottom:14px;line-height:1.5;}' +
      '.weld-toast-modal input,.weld-toast-modal textarea{width:100%;padding:8px 10px;' +
        'background:var(--weld-faint,#21262d);' +
        'border:1px solid var(--weld-border,rgba(255,255,255,0.10));border-radius:4px;' +
        'color:var(--weld-ink,#e6edf3);font:13px system-ui,sans-serif;margin-bottom:14px;}' +
      '.weld-toast-modal textarea{resize:vertical;min-height:80px;font-family:inherit;}' +
      '.weld-toast-actions{display:flex;gap:8px;justify-content:flex-end;}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn{padding:6px 14px;border-radius:4px;font:600 13px system-ui,sans-serif;' +
        'cursor:pointer;border:1px solid transparent;}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn.primary{background:#4493f8;color:#fff;}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn.primary:hover{background:#3a85e0;}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn.danger{background:#f85149;color:#fff;}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn.danger:hover{background:#e0463f;}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn.ghost{background:transparent;color:var(--weld-ink,#e6edf3);' +
        'border-color:var(--weld-border,rgba(255,255,255,0.10));}' +
      '.weld-toast-btn.ghost:hover{background:var(--weld-faint,#21262d);}';
    document.head.appendChild(s);
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Toast host management
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var config = {
    position: 'top-right',
    duration: 4000,
    max: 5
  };
  var hosts = {};
  var activeToasts = [];

  function getHost(position) {
    if (hosts[position]) return hosts[position];
    var h = document.createElement('div');
    h.className = 'weld-toast-host ' + position;
    document.body.appendChild(h);
    hosts[position] = h;
    return h;
  }

  function configure(opts) {
    if (!opts) return;
    if (opts.position) config.position = opts.position;
    if (opts.duration != null) config.duration = opts.duration;
    if (opts.max != null) config.max = opts.max;
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Toast notification
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var ICONS = {
    info:    'i',
    success: '\u2713',
    warn:    '!',
    error:   'x'
  };

  function show(message, opts) {
    injectCss();
    opts = opts || {};
    var type = opts.type || 'info';
    var duration = opts.duration != null ? opts.duration : config.duration;
    var position = opts.position || config.position;
    var dismissible = opts.dismissible !== false;

    var host = getHost(position);

    var toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.className = 'weld-toast ' + type;

    var icon = document.createElement('div');
    icon.className = 'weld-toast-icon';
    icon.textContent = ICONS[type] || ICONS.info;
    toast.appendChild(icon);

    var msg = document.createElement('div');
    msg.className = 'weld-toast-msg';
    msg.textContent = String(message);
    toast.appendChild(msg);

    if (dismissible) {
      var close = document.createElement('button');
      close.className = 'weld-toast-close';
      close.textContent = '\u00d7';
      close.setAttribute('aria-label', 'close');
      close.addEventListener('click', function() { dismiss(handle); });
      toast.appendChild(close);
    }

    // Enforce max
    while (activeToasts.length >= config.max) {
      var oldest = activeToasts.shift();
      if (oldest) dismiss(oldest, true);
    }

    host.appendChild(toast);
    // Trigger CSS transition
    setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.add('shown'); }, 10);

    var timer = null;
    var handle = { toast: toast, host: host, dismissed: false, _t: null };
    activeToasts.push(handle);

    if (duration > 0) {
      handle._t = setTimeout(function() { dismiss(handle); }, duration);
    }

    return handle;
  }

  function dismiss(handle, immediate) {
    if (!handle || handle.dismissed) return;
    handle.dismissed = true;
    if (handle._t) clearTimeout(handle._t);
    var idx = activeToasts.indexOf(handle);
    if (idx !== -1) activeToasts.splice(idx, 1);

    if (immediate) {
      if (handle.toast.parentNode) handle.toast.parentNode.removeChild(handle.toast);
      return;
    }
    handle.toast.classList.remove('shown');
    setTimeout(function() {
      if (handle.toast.parentNode) handle.toast.parentNode.removeChild(handle.toast);
    }, 240);
  }

  function clearAll() {
    while (activeToasts.length) {
      dismiss(activeToasts[0], true);
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Modal helpers: prompt, confirm
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function buildBackdrop() {
    injectCss();
    var bg = document.createElement('div');
    bg.className = 'weld-toast-backdrop';
    document.body.appendChild(bg);
    setTimeout(function() { bg.classList.add('shown'); }, 10);
    return bg;
  }

  function teardown(bg) {
    bg.classList.remove('shown');
    setTimeout(function() {
      if (bg.parentNode) bg.parentNode.removeChild(bg);
    }, 200);
  }

  function confirmDialog(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var title = opts.title || 'Confirm';
    var message = opts.message || 'Are you sure?';
    var okLabel = opts.okLabel || 'OK';
    var cancelLabel = opts.cancelLabel || 'Cancel';
    var danger = opts.danger === true;

    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      var bg = buildBackdrop();
      var modal = document.createElement('div');
      modal.className = 'weld-toast-modal';

      var h = document.createElement('h4');
      h.textContent = title;
      modal.appendChild(h);

      var p = document.createElement('p');
      p.textContent = message;
      modal.appendChild(p);

      var actions = document.createElement('div');
      actions.className = 'weld-toast-actions';

      var cancel = document.createElement('button');
      cancel.className = 'weld-toast-btn ghost';
      cancel.textContent = cancelLabel;
      cancel.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(false); });
      actions.appendChild(cancel);

      var ok = document.createElement('button');
      ok.className = 'weld-toast-btn ' + (danger ? 'danger' : 'primary');
      ok.textContent = okLabel;
      ok.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(true); });
      actions.appendChild(ok);

      modal.appendChild(actions);
      bg.appendChild(modal);
      setTimeout(function() { ok.focus(); }, 100);
    });
  }

  function promptDialog(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var title = opts.title || 'Prompt';
    var message = opts.message || '';
    var placeholder = opts.placeholder || '';
    var defaultValue = opts.defaultValue || '';
    var multiline = opts.multiline === true;
    var okLabel = opts.okLabel || 'OK';
    var cancelLabel = opts.cancelLabel || 'Cancel';

    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      var bg = buildBackdrop();
      var modal = document.createElement('div');
      modal.className = 'weld-toast-modal';

      var h = document.createElement('h4');
      h.textContent = title;
      modal.appendChild(h);

      if (message) {
        var p = document.createElement('p');
        p.textContent = message;
        modal.appendChild(p);
      }

      var input;
      if (multiline) {
        input = document.createElement('textarea');
      } else {
        input = document.createElement('input');
        input.type = 'text';
      }
      input.placeholder = placeholder;
      input.value = defaultValue;
      modal.appendChild(input);

      var actions = document.createElement('div');
      actions.className = 'weld-toast-actions';

      var cancel = document.createElement('button');
      cancel.className = 'weld-toast-btn ghost';
      cancel.textContent = cancelLabel;
      cancel.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(null); });
      actions.appendChild(cancel);

      var ok = document.createElement('button');
      ok.className = 'weld-toast-btn primary';
      ok.textContent = okLabel;
      ok.addEventListener('click', function() { teardown(bg); resolve(input.value); });
      actions.appendChild(ok);

      modal.appendChild(actions);
      bg.appendChild(modal);
      setTimeout(function() { input.focus(); input.select(); }, 100);

      if (!multiline) {
        input.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
          if (e.key === 'Enter') { teardown(bg); resolve(input.value); }
          if (e.key === 'Escape') { teardown(bg); resolve(null); }
        });
      }
    });
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // API
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  window.weld.toast = {
    show: show,
    info:    function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'info';    return show(m, o); },
    success: function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'success'; return show(m, o); },
    warn:    function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'warn';    return show(m, o); },
    error:   function(m, o) { o = o || {}; o.type = 'error';   return show(m, o); },
    dismiss: dismiss,
    clear:   clearAll,
    configure: configure,
    confirm: confirmDialog,
    prompt:  promptDialog,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.toast;


  })();

  // ---- weld-confetti ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.confetti) return window.weld.confetti;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.confetti: a little joy. A single full-window canvas overlay
  // (pointer-events:none, so it never blocks clicks) renders gravity-y
  // confetti and tears down when the last particle settles. Cheap enough
  // to fire on every good outcome.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var DEFAULT_COLORS = ['#4493f8', '#3fb950', '#d29922', '#f85149', '#a371f7', '#58a6ff', '#ffffff'];

  var canvas = null, ctx = null, particles = [], raf = null, lastTs = 0;

  function ensureCanvas() {
    if (canvas) return;
    canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;inset:0;width:100%;height:100%;'
      + 'pointer-events:none;z-index:99999;';
    document.body.appendChild(canvas);
    ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    resize();
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
  }

  function resize() {
    if (!canvas) return;
    var dpr = (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.devicePixelRatio) || 1;
    canvas.width = Math.floor((window.innerWidth || 800) * dpr);
    canvas.height = Math.floor((window.innerHeight || 600) * dpr);
    if (ctx) ctx.setTransform(dpr, 0, 0, dpr, 0, 0);
  }

  function teardown() {
    if (raf) { cancelAnimationFrame(raf); raf = null; }
    if (canvas && canvas.parentNode) canvas.parentNode.removeChild(canvas);
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') window.removeEventListener('resize', resize);
    canvas = null; ctx = null; particles = []; lastTs = 0;
  }

  function spawn(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var W = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerWidth : 800) || 800;
    var H = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerHeight : 600) || 600;
    var count = opts.count || 120;
    var colors = opts.colors || DEFAULT_COLORS;
    var ox = opts.x != null ? opts.x : W / 2;
    var oy = opts.y != null ? opts.y : H / 3;
    var spread = opts.spread != null ? opts.spread : Math.PI * 2; // full circle by default
    var baseAngle = opts.angle != null ? opts.angle : -Math.PI / 2; // upward
    var power = opts.power || 9;

    for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      var angle = baseAngle + (Math.random() - 0.5) * spread;
      var speed = power * (0.4 + Math.random() * 0.9);
      particles.push({
        x: ox, y: oy,
        vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed,
        vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed,
        size: 4 + Math.random() * 5,
        color: colors[(Math.random() * colors.length) | 0],
        rot: Math.random() * Math.PI,
        vr: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.3,
        life: 0,
        ttl: 90 + Math.random() * 50,
        shape: Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'rect' : 'circle'
      });
    }
  }

  function step(ts) {
    if (!ctx) return;
    var dt = lastTs ? Math.min((ts - lastTs) / 16.67, 3) : 1;
    lastTs = ts;
    var W = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerWidth : 800) || 800;
    var H = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerHeight : 600) || 600;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

    for (var i = particles.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      var p = particles[i];
      p.vy += 0.22 * dt;       // gravity
      p.vx *= 0.99;
      p.x += p.vx * dt;
      p.y += p.vy * dt;
      p.rot += p.vr * dt;
      p.life += dt;
      var alpha = Math.max(0, 1 - p.life / p.ttl);

      ctx.save();
      ctx.globalAlpha = alpha;
      ctx.translate(p.x, p.y);
      ctx.rotate(p.rot);
      ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
      if (p.shape === 'rect') ctx.fillRect(-p.size / 2, -p.size / 2, p.size, p.size * 0.6);
      else { ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(0, 0, p.size / 2, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.fill(); }
      ctx.restore();

      if (p.life >= p.ttl || p.y > H + 40) particles.splice(i, 1);
    }

    if (particles.length) raf = requestAnimationFrame(step);
    else teardown();
  }

  function run() {
    if (!raf) { lastTs = 0; raf = requestAnimationFrame(step); }
  }

  // burst(opts): one celebratory pop. opts: count, colors, x, y, spread,
  // angle (radians), power.
  function burst(opts) {
    if (typeof document === 'undefined') return;
    ensureCanvas();
    spawn(opts);
    run();
  }

  // fireworks(opts): a few staggered bursts at random points up top.
  function fireworks(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var shots = opts.shots || 3;
    var gap = opts.gap || 350;
    for (var i = 0; i < shots; i++) {
      (function (n) {
        setTimeout(function () {
          var W = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerWidth : 800) || 800;
          var H = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerHeight : 600) || 600;
          burst({
            x: W * (0.2 + Math.random() * 0.6),
            y: H * (0.2 + Math.random() * 0.3),
            count: opts.count || 90,
            spread: Math.PI * 2,
            power: 8,
            colors: opts.colors
          });
        }, n * gap);
      })(i);
    }
  }

  // A celebratory side-cannon pair (left + right), good for "win" moments.
  function cannons(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var H = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerHeight : 600) || 600;
    var W = (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.innerWidth : 800) || 800;
    burst({ x: 0, y: H * 0.7, angle: -Math.PI / 4, spread: Math.PI / 3, count: opts.count || 80, power: 13, colors: opts.colors });
    burst({ x: W, y: H * 0.7, angle: -3 * Math.PI / 4, spread: Math.PI / 3, count: opts.count || 80, power: 13, colors: opts.colors });
  }

  function stop() { teardown(); }

  window.weld.confetti = {
    burst: burst,
    fireworks: fireworks,
    cannons: cannons,
    stop: stop,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.confetti;

  })();

  // ---- weld-clean ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.clean) return window.weld.clean;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.clean: the "scrub the raw model text" step every chat app
  // re-implements. A text model returns prose that often needs fixing
  // before you store or render it:
  //   - a half-finished trailing sentence when the output was truncated
  //   - the model echoing "Name:" or hallucinating the next speaker turn
  //   - repetition loops (the same line/word over and over)
  //   - an unclosed ``` code fence that breaks the markdown renderer
  //   - leftover hidden-from-AI marker blocks
  // Each fixer is exposed on its own; clean() runs a configurable pipe.
  // Everything here is pure string -> string, no dependencies.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var HIDDEN_START = '<!--hidden-from-ai-start-->';
  var HIDDEN_END   = '<!--hidden-from-ai-end-->';
  var FENCE = String.fromCharCode(96, 96, 96); // three backticks

  // Remove an incomplete final sentence. Use when a result was truncated
  // (stopReason "artificial") so you don't show a chopped-off fragment.
  function trimPartial(text) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    if (!s) return s;
    var trimmed = s.replace(/\s+$/, '');
    // Already ends cleanly on terminal punctuation or a closing quote/bracket.
    if (/[.!?\u2026\u3002\uff01\uff1f]["'\u201d\u2019)\]]?$/.test(trimmed)) return trimmed;
    // Otherwise cut back to the last sentence terminator we can find.
    var m = trimmed.match(/[\s\S]*[.!?\u2026\u3002\uff01\uff1f]["'\u201d\u2019)\]]?/);
    if (m && m[0].trim().length > 0) return m[0].replace(/\s+$/, '');
    return trimmed; // no terminator at all: leave it as-is rather than blank it
  }

  // Strip a leading "Name:" the model echoed, and cut the reply at the
  // point where it starts speaking AS another turn (role bleed).
  // names: optional array of speaker names to police; if omitted, any
  // capitalized "Word:" or "Word :" at the start of a line is treated
  // as a turn boundary.
  function stripRolePrefix(text, names) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    if (!s) return s;

    function speakerAlt() {
      if (names && names.length) {
        var esc = names.map(function (n) {
          return String(n).replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
        });
        return '(?:' + esc.join('|') + ')';
      }
      return '[A-Z][\\w .\u2019\'-]{0,30}';
    }
    var alt = speakerAlt();

    // 1. Drop a single leading "Name:" prefix on the whole reply.
    s = s.replace(new RegExp('^\\s*' + alt + '\\s*:\\s*'), '');

    // 2. Cut at the first mid-reply line that starts a new speaker turn.
    var boundary = new RegExp('\\n\\s*' + alt + '\\s*:\\s');
    var hit = s.search(boundary);
    if (hit !== -1) s = s.slice(0, hit);

    return s.replace(/\s+$/, '');
  }

  // Collapse runaway repetition: identical adjacent lines, identical
  // adjacent sentences, and long single-character runs.
  function collapseRepeats(text, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var maxLineRepeat = opts.maxLineRepeat || 2;
    var maxCharRun = opts.maxCharRun || 8;
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    if (!s) return s;

    // Long single-character runs (e.g. "okayyyyyyyy", "!!!!!!!!").
    s = s.replace(/(.)\1{7,}/g, function (m, ch) {
      return new Array(maxCharRun + 1).join(ch);
    });

    // Identical adjacent lines beyond the allowed repeat count.
    var lines = s.split('\n');
    var out = [];
    var run = 0, prev = null;
    for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
      var key = lines[i].trim();
      if (key !== '' && key === prev) {
        run += 1;
        if (run >= maxLineRepeat) continue;
      } else {
        run = 0; prev = key;
      }
      out.push(lines[i]);
    }
    return out.join('\n');
  }

  // Ensure triple-backtick code fences are balanced. If an odd fence is
  // left open, append a closing one so the markdown renderer recovers.
  function balanceFences(text) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    var count = 0, idx = s.indexOf(FENCE);
    while (idx !== -1) { count += 1; idx = s.indexOf(FENCE, idx + 3); }
    if (count % 2 === 1) {
      if (!/\n$/.test(s)) s += '\n';
      s += FENCE;
    }
    return s;
  }

  // Remove hidden-from-AI marker blocks and their contents.
  function stripHidden(text) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    var start = s.indexOf(HIDDEN_START);
    while (start !== -1) {
      var end = s.indexOf(HIDDEN_END, start);
      if (end === -1) { s = s.slice(0, start); break; }
      s = s.slice(0, start) + s.slice(end + HIDDEN_END.length);
      start = s.indexOf(HIDDEN_START);
    }
    return s;
  }

  // Apply an ordered list of find/replace rules.
  // rule = { find: string|RegExp, replace: string, flags?: string }
  function applyRules(text, ruleList) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    if (!ruleList || !ruleList.length) return s;
    for (var i = 0; i < ruleList.length; i++) {
      var r = ruleList[i];
      if (!r || r.find == null) continue;
      var re;
      if (r.find instanceof RegExp) re = r.find;
      else re = new RegExp(String(r.find), r.flags == null ? 'g' : r.flags);
      s = s.replace(re, r.replace == null ? '' : String(r.replace));
    }
    return s;
  }

  // The pipeline. Each stage is opt-in; pass a result object straight
  // from weld.stream and clean() will trimPartial only when truncated.
  // opts:
  //   truncated     (bool)    run trimPartial (auto-true if you pass result)
  //   roleNames     (array)   names for stripRolePrefix; \[\] enables generic mode
  //   roles         (bool)    enable stripRolePrefix even without names
  //   collapse      (bool)    collapseRepeats (default true)
  //   fences        (bool)    balanceFences (default true)
  //   hidden        (bool)    stripHidden (default true)
  //   rules         (array)   custom find/replace rules
  //   trim          (bool)    trim outer whitespace (default true)
  // Agency Shield: stop the model from speaking or acting AS the player.
  // Drops any line that opens with the player's name as a speaker
  // ("Alex:" or a bracket-wrapped "Alex" speaker label), and trims a trailing block where the model
  // begins narrating the player's own dialogue/action. Keeps the reply up
  // to the point the impersonation starts. Inspired by multi-speaker chat
  // engines that must protect player agency in a single-protagonist story.
  function stripImpersonation(text, playerName) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    if (!s || !playerName) return s;
    var name = String(playerName).trim();
    if (!name) return s;
    var esc = name.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');

    // 1. Cut at the first line that starts a player speaker turn, with or
    //    without bracket wrappers: "Name:", "[Name]:", or doubled brackets.
    var br = '\\[+\\s*' + esc + '\\s*\\]+';
    var boundary = new RegExp('(^|\\n)\\s*(?:' + esc + '|' + br + ')\\s*:', 'i');
    var hit = s.search(boundary);
    if (hit > 0) s = s.slice(0, hit);
    else if (hit === 0) {
      // whole reply is impersonation; drop the leading turn label only
      s = s.replace(new RegExp('^\\s*(?:' + esc + '|' + br + ')\\s*:\\s*', 'i'), '');
    }
    return s.replace(/\s+$/, '');
  }

  function clean(input, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var text, truncated;
    if (input && typeof input === 'object' && 'text' in input) {
      // A weld.stream result object.
      text = input.text;
      truncated = (opts.truncated != null) ? opts.truncated : !!input.truncated;
    } else {
      text = input;
      truncated = !!opts.truncated;
    }
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);

    if (opts.hidden !== false) s = stripHidden(s);
    if (opts.playerName || opts.player) s = stripImpersonation(s, opts.playerName || opts.player);
    if (opts.roles || (opts.roleNames != null)) s = stripRolePrefix(s, opts.roleNames);
    if (opts.collapse !== false) s = collapseRepeats(s, opts);
    if (truncated) s = trimPartial(s);
    if (opts.rules) s = applyRules(s, opts.rules);
    if (opts.fences !== false) s = balanceFences(s);
    if (opts.trim !== false) s = s.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, '');
    return s;
  }

  window.weld.clean = {
    clean: clean,
    trimPartial: trimPartial,
    stripRolePrefix: stripRolePrefix,
    collapseRepeats: collapseRepeats,
    balanceFences: balanceFences,
    stripHidden: stripHidden,
    rules: applyRules,
    stripImpersonation: stripImpersonation,
    version: '1.1.0'
  };

  return window.weld.clean;

  })();

  // ---- weld-reactions ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.reactions) return window.weld.reactions;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.reactions: a count of emoji on an id, plus "did I react".
  //
  // Discord and Twitch both attach lightweight aggregate reactions to
  // messages. The essence is tiny: per item, a map emoji -> set of user
  // ids; counts fall out of the set sizes, and "mine" is membership of the
  // current user. weld.reactions owns that bookkeeping and the events; the
  // app owns storage and identity.
  //
  //   var rx = weld.reactions.create({ me: currentUserId });
  //   rx.react(turnId, '\u {1F44D}');           // I add a thumbs-up
  //   rx.toggle(turnId, '\u2764\uFE0F');         // toggle a heart
  //   rx.countsFor(turnId);                       // { '\u {1F44D}': 3, '\u2764\uFE0F': 1 }
  //   rx.mine(turnId);                            // the emoji I reacted with
  //   rx.onChange(function (e) { rerender(e.itemId); });
  //
  // STORAGE is pluggable. By default reactions live in memory for the
  // session. Pass { store } with get(itemId)->data and set(itemId,data) to
  // persist: e.g. a weld.kv-backed store for counts shared across users,
  // or weld.persist for local. serialize()/load() round-trip the whole set.
  //
  // It RENDERS NOTHING. countsFor + mine give an app everything it needs to
  // draw a reaction bar however it likes (and weld.emotes can turn tokens
  // into images). That keeps it composable and testable.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function createReactions(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var me = opts.me != null ? String(opts.me) : 'me';   // current user id
    var store = opts.store || null;                       // optional { get, set }
    var listeners = new Array();

    // In-memory model: items keyed by itemId -> { emoji: { userId: true } }
    var items = {};

    function emit(itemId, emoji, action) {
      var e = { itemId: itemId, emoji: emoji, action: action };
      for (var i = 0; i < listeners.length; i++) {
        try { Reflect.get(listeners, i)(e); } catch (err) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }
    function onChange(fn) {
      if (typeof fn !== 'function') return function () {};
      listeners.push(fn);
      return function () { var ix = listeners.indexOf(fn); if (ix !== -1) listeners.splice(ix, 1); };
    }

    // ---- identity ----
    function setUser(id) { me = (id != null) ? String(id) : me; }

    // ---- internal item access (with optional backing store) ----
    function itemOf(itemId) {
      var key = String(itemId);
      var it = Reflect.get(items, key);
      if (it) return it;
      // try the backing store
      if (store && typeof store.get === 'function') {
        try {
          var loaded = store.get(key);
          if (loaded && typeof loaded === 'object') { Reflect.set(items, key, loaded); return loaded; }
        } catch (e) { /* fall through */ }
      }
      it = {};
      Reflect.set(items, key, it);
      return it;
    }
    function persistItem(itemId) {
      if (store && typeof store.set === 'function') {
        try { store.set(String(itemId), Reflect.get(items, String(itemId))); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }

    // ---- mutate ----
    // react(itemId, emoji, optional user): add a reaction. Idempotent per user.
    function react(itemId, emoji, user) {
      var u = (user != null) ? String(user) : me;
      var key = String(emoji);
      var it = itemOf(itemId);
      var bag = Reflect.get(it, key);
      if (!bag) { bag = {}; Reflect.set(it, key, bag); }
      if (Reflect.get(bag, u)) return false;     // already reacted
      Reflect.set(bag, u, true);
      persistItem(itemId);
      emit(itemId, key, 'add');
      return true;
    }
    // unreact(itemId, emoji, optional user): remove a reaction.
    function unreact(itemId, emoji, user) {
      var u = (user != null) ? String(user) : me;
      var key = String(emoji);
      var it = itemOf(itemId);
      var bag = Reflect.get(it, key);
      if (!bag || !Reflect.get(bag, u)) return false;
      Reflect.deleteProperty(bag, u);
      if (Object.keys(bag).length === 0) Reflect.deleteProperty(it, key);  // drop empty emoji
      persistItem(itemId);
      emit(itemId, key, 'remove');
      return true;
    }
    // toggle(itemId, emoji, optional user): add if absent, remove if present.
    function toggle(itemId, emoji, user) {
      var u = (user != null) ? String(user) : me;
      return hasReacted(itemId, emoji, u) ? (unreact(itemId, emoji, u), false) : (react(itemId, emoji, u), true);
    }

    // ---- query ----
    // countsFor(itemId): { emoji: count } sorted by descending count.
    function countsFor(itemId) {
      var it = itemOf(itemId);
      var out = {};
      var keys = Object.keys(it);
      keys.sort(function (a, b) { return Object.keys(Reflect.get(it, b)).length - Object.keys(Reflect.get(it, a)).length; });
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
        var k = Reflect.get(keys, i);
        Reflect.set(out, k, Object.keys(Reflect.get(it, k)).length);
      }
      return out;
    }
    // count(itemId, emoji): number of users who reacted with emoji.
    function count(itemId, emoji) {
      var bag = Reflect.get(itemOf(itemId), String(emoji));
      return bag ? Object.keys(bag).length : 0;
    }
    // total(itemId): total reactions across all emoji.
    function total(itemId) {
      var it = itemOf(itemId), n = 0, keys = Object.keys(it);
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) n += Object.keys(Reflect.get(it, Reflect.get(keys, i))).length;
      return n;
    }
    // mine(itemId, optional user): array of emoji the user reacted with.
    function mine(itemId, user) {
      var u = (user != null) ? String(user) : me;
      var it = itemOf(itemId), out = new Array(), keys = Object.keys(it);
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
        var k = Reflect.get(keys, i);
        if (Reflect.get(Reflect.get(it, k), u)) out.push(k);
      }
      return out;
    }
    // hasReacted(itemId, emoji, optional user): did the user react with this emoji?
    function hasReacted(itemId, emoji, user) {
      var u = (user != null) ? String(user) : me;
      var bag = Reflect.get(itemOf(itemId), String(emoji));
      return !!(bag && Reflect.get(bag, u));
    }
    // reactors(itemId, emoji): the user ids who reacted with emoji.
    function reactors(itemId, emoji) {
      var bag = Reflect.get(itemOf(itemId), String(emoji));
      return bag ? Object.keys(bag) : new Array();
    }

    // ---- maintenance ----
    function clearItem(itemId) {
      Reflect.deleteProperty(items, String(itemId));
      persistItem(itemId);
      emit(itemId, null, 'clear');
    }
    function clearAll() { items = {}; }

    // ---- persistence ----
    function serialize() { return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(items)); }
    function load(data) {
      if (data && typeof data === 'object') { items = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data)); return true; }
      return false;
    }

    return {
      setUser: setUser,
      react: react, unreact: unreact, toggle: toggle,
      countsFor: countsFor, count: count, total: total,
      mine: mine, hasReacted: hasReacted, reactors: reactors,
      clearItem: clearItem, clearAll: clearAll,
      serialize: serialize, load: load,
      onChange: onChange
    };
  }

  window.weld.reactions = {
    create: createReactions,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.reactions;

  })();
  // ---- weld-voice ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.voice) return window.weld.voice;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.voice: read replies aloud and (where the browser allows) take
  // voice input. TTS via SpeechSynthesis is broadly supported and works
  // inside the Perchance frame. STT via SpeechRecognition is best-effort:
  // it needs a mic permission and may be blocked in a sandboxed frame, so
  // every STT call is guarded and supported() tells you up front.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var synth = (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.speechSynthesis) ? window.speechSynthesis : null;
  var Recognition = (typeof window !== 'undefined')
    ? (window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition || null)
    : null;

  function supported() {
    return { tts: !!synth, stt: !!Recognition };
  }

  // ---- voices ----
  function voices() { return synth ? synth.getVoices() : []; }

  function pickVoice(want) {
    if (!synth || want == null) return null;
    var list = synth.getVoices();
    if (typeof want === 'number') return list[want] || null;
    var w = String(want).toLowerCase();
    for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
      var v = list[i];
      if (v.name.toLowerCase() === w || v.voiceURI.toLowerCase() === w) return v;
    }
    for (var j = 0; j < list.length; j++) {
      if (list[j].name.toLowerCase().indexOf(w) !== -1) return list[j];
      if (list[j].lang && list[j].lang.toLowerCase().indexOf(w) !== -1) return list[j];
    }
    return null;
  }

  // ---- text to speech ----
  // speak(text, opts) -> the utterance (or null). opts:
  //   rate (0.1-10, default 1), pitch (0-2, default 1), volume (0-1),
  //   voice (name/index/lang substring), lang, interrupt (bool),
  //   onStart, onEnd, onError, onBoundary
  function speak(text, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    if (!synth) { if (opts.onError) opts.onError('tts-unsupported'); return null; }
    var str = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    if (!str.trim()) return null;
    if (opts.interrupt) synth.cancel();

    var u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(str);
    if (opts.rate != null) u.rate = opts.rate;
    if (opts.pitch != null) u.pitch = opts.pitch;
    if (opts.volume != null) u.volume = opts.volume;
    if (opts.lang) u.lang = opts.lang;
    var v = pickVoice(opts.voice);
    if (v) u.voice = v;
    if (opts.onStart) u.onstart = function () { opts.onStart(); };
    if (opts.onEnd) u.onend = function () { opts.onEnd(); };
    if (opts.onError) u.onerror = function (e) { opts.onError((e && e.error) || 'tts-error'); };
    if (opts.onBoundary) u.onboundary = function (e) { opts.onBoundary(e); };
    synth.speak(u);
    return u;
  }

  function stop() { if (synth) synth.cancel(); }
  function pause() { if (synth) synth.pause(); }
  function resume() { if (synth) synth.resume(); }
  function speaking() { return !!(synth && synth.speaking); }

  // ---- speech to text (best-effort) ----
  // listen(opts) -> a session handle, or null if unsupported. opts:
  //   lang (default 'en-US'), interim (bool), continuous (bool),
  //   onResult(text, isFinal), onEnd, onError, onStart
  // handle: { stop(), abort(), active() }
  function listen(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    if (!Recognition) { if (opts.onError) opts.onError('stt-unsupported'); return null; }
    var rec;
    try { rec = new Recognition(); } catch (e) { if (opts.onError) opts.onError('stt-init-failed'); return null; }
    rec.lang = opts.lang || 'en-US';
    rec.interimResults = !!opts.interim;
    rec.continuous = !!opts.continuous;
    var active = true;

    rec.onresult = function (e) {
      if (!opts.onResult) return;
      for (var i = e.resultIndex; i < e.results.length; i++) {
        var r = e.results[i];
        opts.onResult(r[0] ? r[0].transcript : '', r.isFinal);
      }
    };
    rec.onerror = function (e) { if (opts.onError) opts.onError((e && e.error) || 'stt-error'); };
    rec.onend = function () { active = false; if (opts.onEnd) opts.onEnd(); };
    if (opts.onStart) rec.onstart = function () { opts.onStart(); };

    try { rec.start(); } catch (e) { if (opts.onError) opts.onError('stt-start-failed'); return null; }

    return {
      stop: function () { try { rec.stop(); } catch (e) {} },
      abort: function () { try { rec.abort(); } catch (e) {} },
      active: function () { return active; }
    };
  }

  window.weld.voice = {
    supported: supported,
    voices: voices,
    speak: speak,
    stop: stop,
    pause: pause,
    resume: resume,
    speaking: speaking,
    listen: listen,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.voice;

  })();
  // ---- weld-rules ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.rules) return window.weld.rules;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.rules: reactive "when X, do Y" for app-supplied signals.
  //
  // The app owns the signals and the actions; weld.rules owns the logic of
  // deciding WHEN to act. You register metric getters and an action handler,
  // declare rules as plain data, and tick the engine from your loop:
  //
  //   var r = weld.rules.create();
  //   r.metric('tokens', function () { return weld.tokens.count(buffer); });
  //   r.metric('idleSec', function () { return (Date.now() - lastInput) / 1000; });
  //   r.onAction(function (action, rule) {
  //     if (action.type === 'summarize') doSummary();
  //     if (action.type === 'autosave')  hist.save();
  //   });
  //   r.add({ when: { metric: 'tokens', op: '>', value: 3000 },
  //           then: { type: 'summarize' }, cooldownSec: 60 });
  //   r.add({ when: { metric: 'idleSec', op: '>=', value: 30 },
  //           then: { type: 'autosave' }, durationSec: 0, cooldownSec: 30 });
  //   setInterval(function () { r.tick(1); }, 1000);   // 1s frames
  //
  // A RULE is plain data so it can be saved/edited/imported:
  //   { id, enabled, when: { metric, op, value }, then: <action>,
  //     durationSec, cooldownSec }
  //   op is one of < > <= >= == != ; durationSec = the condition must hold
  //   this long before firing (debounce); cooldownSec = min gap between
  //   re-fires. Both default to 0.
  //
  // The engine bakes in no metrics and no actions; it compares numbers and
  // dispatches whatever 'then' you wrote to your handler. That keeps it
  // backend-agnostic and reusable across any weld app.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var OPS = {
    '<':  function (a, b) { return a <  b; },
    '>':  function (a, b) { return a >  b; },
    '<=': function (a, b) { return a <= b; },
    '>=': function (a, b) { return a >= b; },
    '==': function (a, b) { return a === b; },
    '!=': function (a, b) { return a !== b; }
  };

  var idSeq = 0;
  function uid() { idSeq++; return 'r' + Date.now().toString(36) + '_' + idSeq.toString(36); }

  function createEngine(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var metrics = {};        // name -> getter function
    var actionHandlers = new Array();
    var rules = new Array();
    var ruleState = {};      // id -> { heldSec, lastFiredAt }
    var clock = 0;           // absolute seconds, accumulated across ticks

    // ---- metrics ----
    // register(name, getter): getter() -> number (or anything == comparable).
    function metric(name, getter) {
      if (!name || typeof getter !== 'function') return;
      Reflect.set(metrics, String(name), getter);
      return engine;
    }
    function readMetric(name) {
      var g = Reflect.get(metrics, String(name));
      if (typeof g !== 'function') return undefined;
      try { return g(); } catch (e) { return undefined; }
    }
    function metricNames() { return Object.keys(metrics); }

    // ---- action handlers ----
    function onAction(fn) {
      if (typeof fn !== 'function') return function () {};
      actionHandlers.push(fn);
      return function () {
        var ix = actionHandlers.indexOf(fn);
        if (ix !== -1) actionHandlers.splice(ix, 1);
      };
    }
    function dispatch(action, rule) {
      for (var i = 0; i < actionHandlers.length; i++) {
        try { Reflect.get(actionHandlers, i)(action, rule); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
      // a rule may also carry its own callback in `then.run`
      if (rule && rule.then && typeof rule.then.run === 'function') {
        try { rule.then.run(rule); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }

    // ---- rule normalization (plain data in, valid rule out) ----
    function normalize(r) {
      r = r || {};
      var when = r.when || r.condition || {};
      var op = Reflect.get(OPS, when.op) ? when.op : '>';
      return {
        id: r.id || uid(),
        enabled: r.enabled !== false,
        when: {
          metric: String(when.metric || ''),
          op: op,
          value: when.value
        },
        then: r.then || r.action || { type: 'noop' },
        durationSec: numOr(r.durationSec, 0),
        cooldownSec: numOr(r.cooldownSec, 0),
        meta: r.meta || null
      };
    }
    function numOr(v, d) { var n = Number(v); return isFinite(n) && n >= 0 ? n : d; }

    // ---- CRUD on rules ----
    function add(r) {
      var rule = normalize(r);
      rules.push(rule);
      Reflect.set(ruleState, rule.id, { heldSec: 0, lastFiredAt: -Infinity });
      return rule;
    }
    function addAll(list) { return (list || new Array()).map(add); }
    function get(id) { for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i++) { var ru = Reflect.get(rules, i); if (ru.id === id) return ru; } return null; }
    function update(id, patch) {
      var rule = get(id);
      if (!rule) return null;
