      var merged = normalize(Object.assign({}, rule, patch, { id: id }));
      for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i++) { if (Reflect.get(rules, i).id === id) { Reflect.set(rules, i, merged); break; } }
      return merged;
    }
    function remove(id) {
      for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i++) {
        if (Reflect.get(rules, i).id === id) { rules.splice(i, 1); Reflect.deleteProperty(ruleState, id); return true; }
      }
      return false;
    }
    function toggle(id, on) {
      var rule = get(id);
      if (!rule) return null;
      rule.enabled = (on === undefined) ? !rule.enabled : (on === true);
      return rule.enabled;
    }
    function list() { return rules.map(function (r) { return Object.assign({}, r); }); }
    function clear() { rules = new Array(); ruleState = {}; }

    // ---- evaluation ----
    // evalRule(rule): is the condition currently true? (no side effects)
    function evalRule(rule) {
      var fn = Reflect.get(OPS, rule.when.op);
      if (!fn) return false;
      var actual = readMetric(rule.when.metric);
      if (actual === undefined) return false;
      return fn(actual, rule.when.value);
    }

    // tick(elapsedSec): advance the engine by elapsedSec seconds. For each
    // enabled rule, if its condition holds, accumulate hold time; once the
    // hold reaches durationSec AND the cooldown has elapsed since the last
    // fire, dispatch the action. A condition going false resets the hold.
    // Returns the rules that fired this tick.
    function tick(elapsedSec) {
      var dt = numOr(elapsedSec, 0);
      clock += dt;
      var fired = new Array();
      for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i++) {
        var rule = Reflect.get(rules, i);
        if (!rule.enabled) continue;
        var rs = Reflect.get(ruleState, rule.id) || { heldSec: 0, lastFiredAt: -Infinity };
        if (evalRule(rule)) {
          rs.heldSec += dt;
          if (rs.heldSec >= rule.durationSec) {
            var sinceFire = clock - rs.lastFiredAt;
            if (rs.lastFiredAt === -Infinity || sinceFire >= rule.cooldownSec) {
              rs.lastFiredAt = clock;
              rs.heldSec = 0;
              dispatch(rule.then, rule);
              fired.push(rule);
            }
          }
        } else {
          rs.heldSec = 0;
        }
        Reflect.set(ruleState, rule.id, rs);
      }
      return fired;
    }

    // evaluateNow(): fire any rules whose condition is true RIGHT NOW,
    // ignoring durationSec but still respecting cooldown. Handy for one-shot
    // checks outside a tick loop (e.g. right after an event).
    function evaluateNow() {
      var fired = new Array();
      for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i++) {
        var rule = Reflect.get(rules, i);
        if (!rule.enabled) continue;
        var rs = Reflect.get(ruleState, rule.id) || { heldSec: 0, lastFiredAt: -Infinity };
        if (evalRule(rule)) {
          var sinceFire = clock - rs.lastFiredAt;
          if (rs.lastFiredAt === -Infinity || sinceFire >= rule.cooldownSec) {
            rs.lastFiredAt = clock;
            rs.heldSec = 0;
            dispatch(rule.then, rule);
            fired.push(rule);
            Reflect.set(ruleState, rule.id, rs);
          }
        }
      }
      return fired;
    }

    // reset(): clear hold/cooldown state without removing rules (e.g. on a
    // session switch) so cooldowns don't carry across contexts.
    function reset() {
      clock = 0;
      for (var i = 0; i < rules.length; i++) {
        Reflect.set(ruleState, Reflect.get(rules, i).id, { heldSec: 0, lastFiredAt: -Infinity });
      }
    }

    // snapshot(): the rules as plain data (for saving). restore(list) loads.
    function snapshot() { return list(); }
    function restore(saved) { clear(); addAll(saved || new Array()); }

    var engine = {
      metric: metric, metricNames: metricNames,
      onAction: onAction,
      add: add, addAll: addAll, get: get, update: update, remove: remove,
      toggle: toggle, list: list, clear: clear,
      evalRule: evalRule, tick: tick, evaluateNow: evaluateNow, reset: reset,
      snapshot: snapshot, restore: restore,
      ops: function () { return Object.keys(OPS); }
    };
    return engine;
  }

  window.weld.rules = {
    create: createEngine,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.rules;

  })();

  // ---- weld-tokens ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.tokens) return window.weld.tokens;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Accurate tokenizer (DeepSeek-R1-0528) via transformers.js.
  // Same tokenizer Perchance uses for the AI broker, so counts are exact.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var tokenizerPromise = null;
  var tokenizer = null;
  var loadError = null;

  function load() {
    if (tokenizerPromise) return tokenizerPromise;
    tokenizerPromise = (function() {
      return Promise.resolve().then(function() {
        return import('https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@huggingface/transformers@latest/+esm');
      }).then(function(mod) {
        return mod.AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained('deepseek-ai/DeepSeek-R1-0528');
      }).then(function(t) {
        tokenizer = t;
        return t;
      }).catch(function(e) {
        loadError = e;
        throw e;
      });
    })();
    return tokenizerPromise;
  }

  function preload() { return load(); }
  function ready()   { return load(); }
  function isLoaded(){ return tokenizer !== null; }
  function getLoadError() { return loadError; }

  // Cheap fallback (~4 chars per token)
  function estimate(text) {
    return Math.ceil(String(text || '').length / 4);
  }

  // Exact count (async)
  function count(text) {
    return load().then(function(t) {
      return t.encode(String(text)).length;
    });
  }

  // Sync count: null if not loaded yet
  function countSync(text) {
    if (!tokenizer) return null;
    return tokenizer.encode(String(text)).length;
  }

  function encode(text) {
    return load().then(function(t) { return t.encode(String(text)); });
  }

  function decode(ids) {
    return load().then(function(t) {
      return t.decode(ids, { skip_special_tokens: true });
    });
  }

  function budget(text, maxTokens) {
    return count(text).then(function(used) {
      return {
        used: used,
        max: maxTokens,
        remaining: maxTokens - used,
        fits: used <= maxTokens,
        percent: Math.round((used / maxTokens) * 100)
      };
    });
  }

  // Truncate preserving the START of the text
  function truncate(text, maxTokens) {
    return load().then(function(t) {
      var ids = t.encode(String(text));
      if (ids.length <= maxTokens) return String(text);
      return t.decode(ids.slice(0, maxTokens), { skip_special_tokens: true });
    });
  }

  // Truncate preserving the END of the text (useful for chat histories)
  function truncateStart(text, maxTokens) {
    return load().then(function(t) {
      var ids = t.encode(String(text));
      if (ids.length <= maxTokens) return String(text);
      return t.decode(ids.slice(-maxTokens), { skip_special_tokens: true });
    });
  }

  // Split text into chunks of ~N tokens each
  function chunk(text, maxTokensPerChunk) {
    return load().then(function(t) {
      var ids = t.encode(String(text));
      var chunks = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i += maxTokensPerChunk) {
        chunks.push(t.decode(ids.slice(i, i + maxTokensPerChunk), { skip_special_tokens: true }));
      }
      return chunks;
    });
  }

  // Count tokens across an array of messages
  function countMessages(messages) {
    var total = 0;
    function step(i) {
      if (i >= messages.length) return Promise.resolve(total);
      var msg = messages[i];
      var txt = typeof msg === 'string' ? msg : (msg.content || msg.text || '');
      return count(txt).then(function(n) {
        total += n + 4;
        return step(i + 1);
      });
    }
    return step(0);
  }

  function info() {
    return {
      model: 'deepseek-ai/DeepSeek-R1-0528',
      loaded: tokenizer !== null,
      error: loadError ? String(loadError.message || loadError) : null,
      vocabSize: tokenizer ? tokenizer.vocab_size : null
    };
  }

  window.weld.tokens = {
    preload: preload,
    ready: ready,
    isLoaded: isLoaded,
    loadError: getLoadError,
    estimate: estimate,
    count: count,
    countSync: countSync,
    encode: encode,
    decode: decode,
    budget: budget,
    truncate: truncate,
    truncateStart: truncateStart,
    chunk: chunk,
    countMessages: countMessages,
    info: info,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.tokens;


  })();

  // ---- weld-structured ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.structured) return window.weld.structured;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.structured: coax dependable JSON out of a plain text model.
  //
  // A text model will not reliably emit clean JSON on its own; it wraps
  // it in prose, fences it, trails a comma, or stops mid-object. This
  // plugin makes the round-trip robust:
  //   1. prime:    append an explicit "respond with only JSON" directive
  //   2. parse:    pull the first balanced {...} / [...] out of the text,
  //                  stripping code fences, tolerating trailing commas
  //   3. validate: check it against a tiny field schema
  //   4. repair:   on parse/validation failure, re-ask with the error,
  //                  up to opts.repairAttempts times
  //
  // Generation goes through weld.stream (so boxed strings, stopReason,
  // and the serial queue are already handled). If weld.stream is absent
  // we fall back to window.root.aiTextPlugin directly.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function getStream() {
    return (window.weld && window.weld.stream) ? window.weld.stream : null;
  }

  // Strip ```json fences and surrounding prose noise.
  function stripFences(text) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    var fence = String.fromCharCode(96, 96, 96);
    var i = s.indexOf(fence);
    if (i === -1) return s;
    // Drop an opening fence + optional language tag, and a closing fence.
    s = s.replace(new RegExp(fence + '[a-zA-Z0-9_-]*\\n?'), '');
    var j = s.lastIndexOf(fence);
    if (j !== -1) s = s.slice(0, j);
    return s;
  }

  // Find the first complete balanced JSON value (object or array),
  // respecting strings and escapes so braces inside strings don't count.
  function extractBalanced(text) {
    var s = String(text == null ? '' : text);
    var startObj = s.indexOf('{');
    var startArr = s.indexOf('[');
    var start;
    if (startObj === -1) start = startArr;
    else if (startArr === -1) start = startObj;
    else start = Math.min(startObj, startArr);
    if (start === -1) return null;

    var open = s.charAt(start);
    var close = (open === '{') ? '}' : ']';
    var depth = 0, inStr = false, esc = false;
    for (var i = start; i < s.length; i++) {
      var c = s.charAt(i);
      if (inStr) {
        if (esc) { esc = false; }
        else if (c === '\\') { esc = true; }
        else if (c === '"') { inStr = false; }
        continue;
      }
      if (c === '"') { inStr = true; continue; }
      if (c === open) depth += 1;
      else if (c === close) {
        depth -= 1;
        if (depth === 0) return s.slice(start, i + 1);
      }
    }
    return null; // never closed (likely truncated)
  }

  function looseFix(jsonText) {
    var s = String(jsonText);
    // Remove trailing commas before } or ].
    s = s.replace(/,\s*([}\]])/g, '$1');
    return s;
  }

  // Parse text -> value. Returns { value } or { error }.
  function parse(text) {
    var candidate = extractBalanced(stripFences(text));
    if (candidate == null) return { error: 'no JSON object or array found in the output' };
    try {
      return { value: JSON.parse(candidate) };
    } catch (e1) {
      try {
        return { value: JSON.parse(looseFix(candidate)) };
      } catch (e2) {
        return { error: 'JSON parse failed: ' + String(e2.message || e2) };
      }
    }
  }

  // parsePartial(text): best-effort parse of an INCOMPLETE JSON object as
  // it streams in. Finds the first '{' or '[', closes any open string,
  // drops a trailing partial token, and balances open brackets, so the UI
  // can render fields the moment they arrive. Returns { value } or {} when
  // nothing parseable yet. Never throws.
  function parsePartial(text) {
    var raw = stripFences(String(text == null ? '' : text));
    var start = -1;
    for (var a = 0; a < raw.length; a++) { var ch0 = raw.charAt(a); if (ch0 === '{' || ch0 === '[') { start = a; break; } }
    if (start === -1) return {};
    var s = raw.slice(start);

    // Scan once to learn: open-bracket stack, whether we end inside a string,
    // and whether we end with a dangling structural token we must drop.
    var stack = [], inStr = false, esc = false;
    for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
      var c = s.charAt(i);
      if (inStr) {
        if (esc) esc = false;
        else if (c === '\\') esc = true;
        else if (c === '"') inStr = false;
        continue;
      }
      if (c === '"') inStr = true;
      else if (c === '{' || c === '[') stack.push(c === '{' ? '}' : ']');
      else if (c === '}' || c === ']') stack.pop();
    }

    function attempt(str) {
      var t = str;
      if (inStr) t += '"';                 // close an open string literal
      t = t.replace(/\s+$/, '');
      t = t.replace(/,\s*$/, '');          // dangling comma
      // "key": with no value yet -> drop the key and colon entirely
      if (/:\s*$/.test(t)) {
        t = t.replace(/:\s*$/, '');
        t = t.replace(/(\{|,)\s*"[^"]*"\s*$/, '$1');
        t = t.replace(/,\s*$/, '');
      }
      for (var k = stack.length - 1; k >= 0; k--) t += stack[k];
      try { return JSON.parse(looseFix(t)); } catch (e) { return undefined; }
    }

    var v = attempt(s);
    if (v !== undefined) return { value: v };
    return {};
  }
  // schema = { fields: { name: { type, required, enum, of } }, allowExtra }
  //   type: 'string' | 'number' | 'integer' | 'boolean' | 'array' | 'object'
  // Returns { ok:true } or { ok:false, error }.
  function typeOk(val, type) {
    switch (type) {
      case 'string':  return typeof val === 'string';
      case 'number':  return typeof val === 'number' && !isNaN(val);
      case 'integer': return typeof val === 'number' && !isNaN(val) && Math.floor(val) === val;
      case 'boolean': return typeof val === 'boolean';
      case 'array':   return Array.isArray(val);
      case 'object':  return val !== null && typeof val === 'object' && !Array.isArray(val);
      default:        return true;
    }
  }

  function validate(value, schema) {
    if (!schema || !schema.fields) return { ok: true };
    if (value === null || typeof value !== 'object' || Array.isArray(value)) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'expected a JSON object at the top level' };
    }
    var fields = schema.fields;
    var names = Object.keys(fields);
    for (var i = 0; i < names.length; i++) {
      var key = names[i];
      var spec = fields[key] || {};
      var present = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(value, key);
      if (!present) {
        if (spec.required) return { ok: false, error: 'missing required field "' + key + '"' };
        continue;
      }
      var v = value[key];
      if (spec.type && !typeOk(v, spec.type)) {
        return { ok: false, error: 'field "' + key + '" should be ' + spec.type };
      }
      if (spec.enum && spec.enum.indexOf(v) === -1) {
        return { ok: false, error: 'field "' + key + '" must be one of: ' + spec.enum.join(', ') };
      }
      if (spec.type === 'array' && spec.of && Array.isArray(v)) {
        for (var j = 0; j < v.length; j++) {
          if (!typeOk(v[j], spec.of)) {
            return { ok: false, error: 'every item of "' + key + '" should be ' + spec.of };
          }
        }
      }
    }
    if (schema.allowExtra === false) {
      var extra = Object.keys(value).filter(function (k) { return names.indexOf(k) === -1; });
      if (extra.length) return { ok: false, error: 'unexpected field(s): ' + extra.join(', ') };
    }
    return { ok: true };
  }

  // Describe a schema in words for the priming directive.
  function describeSchema(schema) {
    if (!schema || !schema.fields) return '';
    var parts = Object.keys(schema.fields).map(function (k) {
      var spec = schema.fields[k] || {};
      var bits = [k + ' (' + (spec.type || 'any')];
      if (spec.required) bits.push('required');
      if (spec.enum) bits.push('one of: ' + spec.enum.join('/'));
      return bits.join(', ') + ')';
    });
    return 'JSON object with fields: ' + parts.join('; ') + '.';
  }

  function buildInstruction(opts, repairNote) {
    var base = String(opts.instruction || '');
    var shape = opts.shape
      || describeSchema(opts.schema)
      || (opts.example ? 'JSON shaped like: ' + JSON.stringify(opts.example) : 'a single JSON value');
    var directive = 'Respond with ONLY ' + shape
      + ' Output strictly valid JSON and nothing else -- no prose, no markdown, no code fences.';
    var instruction = base ? (base + '\n\n' + directive) : directive;
    if (repairNote) {
      instruction += '\n\nYour previous reply could not be used (' + repairNote
        + '). Return corrected JSON only.';
    }
    return instruction;
  }

  // Run one generation through weld.stream (or the raw plugin).
  function generateOnce(instruction, opts) {
    var stream = getStream();
    var runOpts = {
      instruction: instruction,
      startWith: opts.startWith != null ? opts.startWith : '{',
      stopSequences: opts.stopSequences || null
    };
    if (stream) {
      return stream.run(runOpts).then(function (res) {
        return { text: res.text, error: res.error, truncated: res.truncated };
      });
    }
    // Fallback: call ai-text-plugin directly and normalize the boxed String.
    var plugin = null;
    try { if (window.root && typeof window.root.aiTextPlugin === 'function') plugin = window.root.aiTextPlugin; } catch (e) {}
    if (!plugin) {
      return Promise.resolve({ text: '', error: 'weld.structured: neither weld.stream nor ai-text-plugin is available' });
    }
    return Promise.resolve(plugin({ instruction: instruction, startWith: runOpts.startWith }))
      .then(function (raw) {
        var startWith = runOpts.startWith || '';
        var body = (raw && raw.generatedText != null) ? String(raw.generatedText) : String(raw);
        // startWith is echoed back when calling the raw plugin; re-attach it.
        return { text: startWith + body, error: null };
      }, function (err) {
        return { text: '', error: String((err && err.message) || err) };
      });
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Public: generate(opts) -> Promise<\{ ok, value, raw, error, attempts \}>
  //
  // opts:
  //   instruction     (string)  your task / system prompt
  //   schema          (object)  \{ fields: \{ name: \{ type, required, enum, of \} \} \}
  //   example         (object)  alternative to schema: a sample shape to mimic
  //   shape           (string)  free-text description of the desired JSON
  //   startWith       (string)  default '\{' to prime an object
  //   stopSequences   (array)   passthrough to weld.stream
  //   repairAttempts  (number)  extra tries on failure (default 1)
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function generate(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var maxRepairs = (opts.repairAttempts == null) ? 1 : opts.repairAttempts;
    var attempt = 0;
    var lastRaw = '', lastError = null;

    function step(repairNote) {
      attempt += 1;
      var instruction = buildInstruction(opts, repairNote);
      return generateOnce(instruction, opts).then(function (gen) {
        lastRaw = gen.text || '';
        if (gen.error) {
          lastError = gen.error;
          return maybeRetry('generation error: ' + gen.error);
        }
        var parsed = parse(lastRaw);
        if (parsed.error) {
          lastError = parsed.error;
          return maybeRetry(parsed.error);
        }
        var check = validate(parsed.value, opts.schema);
        if (!check.ok) {
          lastError = check.error;
          return maybeRetry(check.error);
        }
        return { ok: true, value: parsed.value, raw: lastRaw, error: null, attempts: attempt };
      });
    }

    function maybeRetry(note) {
      if (attempt <= maxRepairs) return step(note);
      return { ok: false, value: null, raw: lastRaw, error: lastError, attempts: attempt };
    }

    return step(null);
  }

  // generateStream(opts): like generate(), but reports the partially-parsed
  // object as it streams via opts.onPartial(obj). Resolves to the same
  // \{ ok, value, raw, error, attempts \} as generate(). Requires weld.stream
  // (which carries onChunk); without it, falls back to generate().
  function generateStream(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var stream = getStream();
    if (!stream || typeof opts.onPartial !== 'function') return generate(opts);
    var instruction = buildInstruction(opts, null);
    var onPartial = opts.onPartial;
    return stream.run({
      instruction: instruction,
      startWith: opts.startWith != null ? opts.startWith : '{',
      stopSequences: opts.stopSequences || null,
      onChunk: function (delta, full) {
        var p = parsePartial(full);
        if ('value' in p) { try { onPartial(p.value); } catch (e) {} }
      }
    }).then(function (res) {
      if (res.error) return { ok: false, value: null, raw: res.text, error: res.error, attempts: 1 };
      var parsed = parse(res.text);
      if (parsed.error) return { ok: false, value: null, raw: res.text, error: parsed.error, attempts: 1 };
      var check = validate(parsed.value, opts.schema);
      if (!check.ok) return { ok: false, value: parsed.value, raw: res.text, error: check.error, attempts: 1 };
      return { ok: true, value: parsed.value, raw: res.text, error: null, attempts: 1 };
    });
  }

  window.weld.structured = {
    generate: generate,
    generateStream: generateStream,
    parse: parse,
    parsePartial: parsePartial,
    validate: validate,
    extract: extractBalanced,
    describeSchema: describeSchema,
    version: '1.1.0'
  };

  return window.weld.structured;

  })();

  // ---- weld-summarize ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.summarize) return window.weld.summarize;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.summarize: keep a long chat inside the context window without
  // amnesia. weld.prompt can only DROP old turns when the budget is
  // blown; this CONDENSES them instead.
  //
  //   - rolling():   a stateful summarizer. Feed it messages; it keeps
  //                  the most recent N verbatim and rolls everything
  //                  older into a running summary, re-summarizing
  //                  (summary-of-summary) when the summary itself grows.
  //   - summarize(): a one-shot. Hand it text or messages, get a synopsis.
  //
  // Summaries are generated through weld.stream; token counting uses
  // weld.tokens when present, else a chars/4 estimate. Both are soft
  // dependencies: without weld.stream, summarize() reports an error
  // rather than throwing.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function getStream() { return (window.weld && window.weld.stream) ? window.weld.stream : null; }
  function getTokens() { return (window.weld && window.weld.tokens) ? window.weld.tokens : null; }

  function estimateTokens(text) {
    var t = getTokens();
    if (t && t.isLoaded && t.isLoaded() && t.countSync) {
      var n = t.countSync(String(text || ''));
      if (n != null) return n;
    }
    var stream = getStream();
    if (stream && stream.count) {
      var sc = stream.count(String(text || ''));
      if (sc != null) return sc;
    }
    return Math.ceil(String(text || '').length / 4);
  }

  // Normalize a message into "Name: text" wire form for summarizing.
  function lineOf(msg) {
    if (msg == null) return '';
    if (typeof msg === 'string') return msg;
    var who = msg.name || msg.role || msg.author || '';
    var body = msg.content != null ? msg.content : (msg.text != null ? msg.text : '');
    return who ? (who + ': ' + body) : String(body);
  }

  function joinMessages(messages) {
    if (!Array.isArray(messages)) return String(messages == null ? '' : messages);
    return messages.map(lineOf).filter(function (l) { return l && l.trim(); }).join('\n');
  }

  var DEFAULT_PROMPT =
    'Summarize the conversation excerpt below. Capture the durable facts, '
    + 'decisions, character details, and unresolved threads that matter for '
    + 'continuing the conversation. Write a tight third-person synopsis in past '
    + 'tense. Do not invent anything. Output only the summary.';

  // Generate a synopsis of some text via weld.stream.
  // Returns Promise<{ ok, summary, error }>.
  function runSummary(text, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var stream = getStream();
    if (!stream) {
      return Promise.resolve({ ok: false, summary: '', error: 'weld.summarize: weld.stream is not loaded' });
    }
    var body = String(text || '').trim();
    if (!body) return Promise.resolve({ ok: true, summary: '', error: null });

    var instruction = (opts.prompt || DEFAULT_PROMPT);
    if (opts.priorSummary) {
      instruction += '\n\nA summary of earlier events already exists; fold the new '
        + 'excerpt into it and return one consolidated summary.\n\nExisting summary:\n'
        + opts.priorSummary;
    }
    if (opts.maxWords) {
      instruction += '\n\nKeep the summary under about ' + opts.maxWords + ' words.';
    }
    instruction += '\n\nExcerpt:\n' + body;

    return stream.run({ instruction: instruction }).then(function (res) {
      if (res.error) return { ok: false, summary: '', error: res.error };
      return { ok: true, summary: String(res.text || '').trim(), error: null };
    });
  }

  // One-shot: summarize text or an array of messages.
  function summarize(input, opts) {
    var text = Array.isArray(input) ? joinMessages(input) : String(input == null ? '' : input);
    return runSummary(text, opts);
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // rolling(opts) -> a stateful summarizer.
  //
  // opts:
  //   keepRecent   (number)  messages kept verbatim (default 8)
  //   tokenBudget  (number)  compress when kept text exceeds this
  //                          (default: weld.stream.budget() or 5000)
  //   summaryMaxWords (number) cap on the running summary (default 200)
  //   prompt       (string)  override the summarization instruction
  //
  // methods:
  //   add(message)       append; may trigger async compression
  //   addMany(messages)
  //   compressNow()      -> Promise; force a compression pass
  //   state()            -> { summary, recent, generation }
  //   context()          -> "Summary of earlier events: ...\n\nName: msg..."
  //   summary()          -> the running summary string
  //   recent()           -> the verbatim-kept messages
  //   reset()
  //   onChange(fn)       subscribe to state changes; returns unsubscribe
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function rolling(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var keepRecent = opts.keepRecent || 8;
    var summaryMaxWords = opts.summaryMaxWords || 200;
    var budget = opts.tokenBudget;
    if (budget == null) {
      var stream = getStream();
      budget = (stream && stream.budget && stream.budget()) || 5000;
    }

    var recent = [];      // verbatim-kept messages
    var summary = '';     // running synopsis of everything older
    var generation = 0;   // how many compression passes have run
    var compressing = false;
    var listeners = [];

    function emit() {
      var snap = state();
      listeners.forEach(function (fn) { try { fn(snap); } catch (e) {} });
    }

    function overBudget() {
      return estimateTokens(joinMessages(recent)) > budget;
    }

    function compressNow() {
      if (compressing) return Promise.resolve(state());
      // Compress everything except the last keepRecent messages.
      if (recent.length <= keepRecent) return Promise.resolve(state());
      compressing = true;
      var cut = recent.length - keepRecent;
      var older = recent.slice(0, cut);
      var keptTail = recent.slice(cut);
      return runSummary(joinMessages(older), {
        priorSummary: summary || null,
        maxWords: summaryMaxWords,
        prompt: opts.prompt
      }).then(function (r) {
        compressing = false;
        if (r.ok && r.summary) {
          summary = r.summary;
          recent = keptTail;
          generation += 1;
          emit();
        }
        return state();
      }, function () { compressing = false; return state(); });
    }

    function maybeCompress() {
      if (recent.length > keepRecent && overBudget()) return compressNow();
      return Promise.resolve(state());
    }

    function add(message) {
      recent.push(message);
      emit();
      return maybeCompress();
    }

    function addMany(messages) {
      if (Array.isArray(messages)) recent = recent.concat(messages);
      emit();
      return maybeCompress();
    }

    function context(opts2) {
      opts2 = opts2 || {};
      var out = [];
      if (summary) out.push((opts2.label || 'Summary of earlier events') + ': ' + summary);
      var tail = joinMessages(recent);
      if (tail) out.push(tail);
      return out.join('\n\n');
    }

    function state() {
      return { summary: summary, recent: recent.slice(), generation: generation };
    }

    function reset() { recent = []; summary = ''; generation = 0; emit(); }

    function onChange(fn) {
      listeners.push(fn);
      return function () {
        var i = listeners.indexOf(fn);
        if (i !== -1) listeners.splice(i, 1);
      };
    }

    // Restore from a saved state() snapshot.
    function load(snap) {
      if (!snap) return;
      summary = snap.summary || '';
      recent = Array.isArray(snap.recent) ? snap.recent.slice() : [];
      generation = snap.generation || 0;
      emit();
    }

    return {
      add: add,
      addMany: addMany,
      compressNow: compressNow,
      context: context,
      state: state,
      load: load,
      summary: function () { return summary; },
      recent: function () { return recent.slice(); },
      reset: reset,
      onChange: onChange
    };
  }

  // extractFacts(input, opts) -> Promise<{ ok, facts, error }>.
  // Pulls discrete, standalone facts out of text or a set of summaries as
  // a JSON array of strings. Prefers weld.structured (robust JSON) and
  // falls back to weld.stream with a bracket-scan parse.
  var FACTS_PROMPT =
    'Extract all unique, discrete facts from the text below as a JSON array '
    + 'of strings. Each fact must be a complete, standalone statement; remove '
    + 'duplicates; preserve important names and details; keep each concise. '
    + 'Return ONLY a JSON array, e.g. ["fact one.", "fact two."]. If there is '
    + 'nothing worth keeping, return [].';

  function extractFacts(input, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var text = Array.isArray(input) ? joinMessages(input) : String(input == null ? '' : input);
    if (!text.trim()) return Promise.resolve({ ok: true, facts: [], error: null });
    var instruction = (opts.prompt || FACTS_PROMPT) + '\n\nText:\n' + text;

    var structured = (window.weld && window.weld.structured) ? window.weld.structured : null;
    if (structured) {
      return structured.generate({ instruction: instruction, startWith: '[', shape: 'a JSON array of short factual strings' })
        .then(function (r) {
          if (r.ok && Array.isArray(r.value)) return { ok: true, facts: r.value.map(String), error: null };
          return { ok: false, facts: [], error: r.error || 'no facts extracted' };
        });
    }
    var stream = getStream();
    if (!stream) return Promise.resolve({ ok: false, facts: [], error: 'weld.summarize: weld.stream is not loaded' });
    return stream.run({ instruction: instruction, startWith: '[' }).then(function (res) {
      if (res.error) return { ok: false, facts: [], error: res.error };
      var list = [];
      try {
        var raw = res.text, open = raw.indexOf('['), close = raw.lastIndexOf(']');
        if (open !== -1 && close > open) list = JSON.parse(raw.slice(open, close + 1));
      } catch (e) { list = []; }
      if (!Array.isArray(list)) list = [];
      return { ok: true, facts: list.map(String), error: null };
    });
  }

  // consolidate(summaries, opts) -> Promise<{ ok, summary, depth, error }>.
  // Merges several summaries (strings or { summary, depth }) into one, with
  // a hard depth cap so repeated re-summarization can't recurse forever.
  // opts: { maxDepth (default 3), maxWords (default 250), prompt }
  function consolidate(summaries, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var maxDepth = opts.maxDepth != null ? opts.maxDepth : 3;
    var list = (summaries || []).map(function (s) {
      return (typeof s === 'string') ? { summary: s, depth: 0 } : { summary: String(s.summary || ''), depth: s.depth || 0 };
    }).filter(function (s) { return s.summary.trim(); });

    if (!list.length) return Promise.resolve({ ok: true, summary: '', depth: 0, error: null });
    var inDepth = list.reduce(function (m, s) { return Math.max(m, s.depth); }, 0);
    var outDepth = inDepth + 1;
    if (inDepth >= maxDepth) {
      // refuse to recurse further: concatenate as-is
      return Promise.resolve({ ok: true, summary: list.map(function (s) { return s.summary; }).join('\n\n'), depth: inDepth, error: null, capped: true });
    }
    var combined = list.map(function (s) { return s.summary; }).join('\n\n---\n\n');
    return runSummary(combined, {
      prompt: opts.prompt || 'Merge the following summaries into one coherent, non-redundant summary that preserves every important fact, name, and unresolved thread.',
      maxWords: opts.maxWords || 250
    }).then(function (r) {
      if (!r.ok) return { ok: false, summary: '', depth: outDepth, error: r.error };
      return { ok: true, summary: r.summary, depth: outDepth, error: null };
    });
  }

  window.weld.summarize = {
    summarize: summarize,
    rolling: rolling,
    extractFacts: extractFacts,
    consolidate: consolidate,
    estimateTokens: estimateTokens,
    joinMessages: joinMessages,
    version: '1.1.0'
  };

  return window.weld.summarize;

  })();
  // ---- weld-promptforge ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.promptforge) return window.weld.promptforge;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.promptforge: stop hand-tuning image prompts; let good ones win.
  //
  // A community prompt optimizer cracked the loop: ask an LLM for several
  // prompt variants, render them, let the user upvote results, score each
  // prompt by its upvote rate (votes / uses, self-normalizing), and feed
  // the proven winners back into the next round, sometimes promoting a
  // top prompt into the instruction slot. weld.promptforge packages that:
  //
  //   var forge = weld.promptforge.create({ instruction, mode })
  //   var prompts = await forge.generate(4)   // candidate prompt strings
  //   forge.used(promptText)                  // mark it rendered
  //   forge.upvote(promptText)                // result was good
  //   forge.top(n) / forge.score(text) / forge.state() / forge.load(s)
  //
  // Generation goes through weld.stream; if weld.structured is present it
  // is used for a clean JSON array, else a numbered-list parse is used.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function getStream() { return (window.weld && window.weld.stream) ? window.weld.stream : null; }
  function getStructured() { return (window.weld && window.weld.structured) ? window.weld.structured : null; }

  var EXTRA = [
    'Look closely at the instruction: what is the underlying intent? Fulfill it deeply.',
    'Explore bold variations that still obey the instruction; avoid timid small changes.',
    'Prefer concrete, descriptive detail over generic adjectives.',
    'Try a concise comma-separated tag style for some prompts.',
    'Include camera language (lens, shot type, angle) only if consistent with the instruction.',
    'For one prompt focus on mood and lighting; for another, on composition.',
    'Vary specificity: some prompts terse, others richly detailed.'
  ];

  var MODE_DIRECTIVE = {
    faithful: 'EXACTLY satisfy the instruction. Stay strictly on the requested subject.',
    balanced: 'Keep the core subject and any explicit asks intact, but bring fresh angles, mood, lighting, and styling.',
    creative: 'Build on the instruction with a creative touch; reinterpret and remix freely, including bold departures, while keeping the core idea recognizable.'
  };

  function pick(arr) { return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)]; }

  // Curly-brace variant guidance, ~60% of the time, to inject diversity.
  // The literal characters are assembled at runtime so plugin source stays
  // clear of the Perchance brace scanner.
  function curlyGuidance() {
    if (Math.random() >= 0.6) return '';
    var ob = String.fromCharCode(123), cb = String.fromCharCode(125), bar = String.fromCharCode(124);
    var ex = ob + 'candid' + bar + 'studio' + bar + 'cinematic' + cb + ' '
      + ob + 'portrait' + bar + 'wide shot' + cb;
    return '\nUse brace-variant syntax for diversity: add a few brace blocks with '
      + 'pipe-separated options (lighting, expression, angle, styling) where every '
      + 'variant still obeys the instruction. Example: "' + ex + ' of ..."';
  }

  function buildInstruction(forge, n, promotedPrompt) {
    var base = promotedPrompt || forge.instruction;
    var lines = [];
    lines.push('You write image-generation prompts.');
    lines.push(MODE_DIRECTIVE[forge.mode] || MODE_DIRECTIVE.balanced);
    lines.push(pick(EXTRA));
    var top = forge.topList(forge.exampleCount);
    if (top.length) {
      var intro = forge.mixAcross
        ? 'Here are prompts the user has rated highly before. Treat them as a signal of taste, not a template; vary how much you borrow.'
        : 'Here are highly-rated prompts. Study what works and breed their best parts into new ones.';
      lines.push('\n' + intro + '\n<highly_rated>\n'
        + top.map(function (p) { return '- ' + p.text; }).join('\n') + '\n</highly_rated>');
    }
    lines.push(curlyGuidance());
    lines.push('\nInstruction:\n' + base);
    lines.push('\nWrite ' + n + ' distinct prompt' + (n > 1 ? 's' : '')
      + ', one per line, no numbering, no commentary. Each on its own line.');
    return lines.filter(Boolean).join('\n');
  }

  function parseList(text) {
    if (!text) return [];
    return String(text).split(/\r?\n/).map(function (l) {
      return l.replace(/^\s*(?:\d+[.)\-:]|[*\u2022\-\u2013])\s*/, '').replace(/^"(.*)"$/, '$1').trim();
    }).filter(function (l) { return l.length > 0; });
  }

  function create(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var forge = {
      instruction: String(opts.instruction || ''),
      mode: opts.mode || 'balanced',          // faithful | balanced | creative
      mixAcross: !!opts.mixAcross,
      promoteRate: opts.promoteRate != null ? opts.promoteRate : 0.6,
      exampleCount: opts.exampleCount != null ? opts.exampleCount : 6,
      prompts: {}        // text -> { text, used, votes, score, createdAt }
    };

    function recompute(p) { p.score = p.used > 0 ? p.votes / p.used : 0; }

    function ensure(text) {
      var key = String(text || '').trim();
      if (!key) return null;
      if (!forge.prompts[key]) forge.prompts[key] = { text: key, used: 0, votes: 0, score: 0, createdAt: Date.now() };
      return forge.prompts[key];
    }

    function all() { return Object.keys(forge.prompts).map(function (k) { return forge.prompts[k]; }); }
    function scored() { return all().filter(function (p) { return p.used > 0; }); }
    forge.topList = function (limit) {
      return scored().sort(function (a, b) { return b.score - a.score; }).slice(0, limit || 6);
    };
    function topList(limit) { return forge.topList(limit); }

    // roulette selection weighted by score (proven prompts chosen more often)
    function weightedPick(arr) {
      if (!arr.length) return null;
      var weights = arr.map(function (p) { return Math.max(0, p.score); });
      var sum = weights.reduce(function (a, b) { return a + b; }, 0);
      if (sum <= 0) return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)];
      var r = Math.random() * sum, c = 0;
      for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) { c += weights[i]; if (r <= c) return arr[i]; }
      return arr[arr.length - 1];
    }

    // generate(n) -> Promise<string[]> of candidate prompts.
    function generate(n) {
      n = n || 3;
      var stream = getStream();
      if (!stream) return Promise.resolve({ /* graceful */ }).then(function () { return []; });

      // Maybe promote a proven prompt into the instruction slot.
      var promoted = null;
      var pool = scored();
      if (pool.length && Math.random() < forge.promoteRate) {
        var winner = weightedPick(pool);
        if (winner) promoted = winner.text;
      }
      var instruction = buildInstruction(forge, n, promoted);

      var structured = getStructured();
      if (structured) {
        return structured.generate({
          instruction: instruction, startWith: '[',
          shape: 'a JSON array of ' + n + ' image-prompt strings'
        }).then(function (r) {
          var list = (r.ok && Array.isArray(r.value)) ? r.value.map(String) : [];
          if (!list.length && r.raw) list = parseList(r.raw);
          list.forEach(ensure);
          return list;
        });
      }
      return stream.run({ instruction: instruction }).then(function (res) {
        if (res.error) return [];
        var list = parseList(res.text);
        list.forEach(ensure);
        return list;
      });
    }

    function used(text) { var p = ensure(text); if (p) { p.used += 1; recompute(p); } return p; }
    function upvote(text, by) { var p = ensure(text); if (p) { p.votes += (by || 1); recompute(p); } return p; }
    function record(text, r) { r = r || {}; var p = ensure(text); if (!p) return null; if (r.used) p.used += r.used; if (r.votes) p.votes += r.votes; recompute(p); return p; }

    function score(text) { var p = forge.prompts[String(text || '').trim()]; return p ? p.score : 0; }
    function setInstruction(text) { forge.instruction = String(text || ''); }
    function setMode(m) { if (MODE_DIRECTIVE[m]) forge.mode = m; }

    function state() {
      return { instruction: forge.instruction, mode: forge.mode, mixAcross: forge.mixAcross,
        promoteRate: forge.promoteRate, prompts: forge.prompts };
    }
    function load(s) {
      if (!s) return;
      forge.instruction = s.instruction || forge.instruction;
      forge.mode = s.mode || forge.mode;
      if (s.mixAcross != null) forge.mixAcross = s.mixAcross;
      if (s.promoteRate != null) forge.promoteRate = s.promoteRate;
      forge.prompts = s.prompts || {};
    }

    return {
      generate: generate,
      used: used,
      upvote: upvote,
      record: record,
      score: score,
      top: function (n) { return topList(n); },
      all: all,
      setInstruction: setInstruction,
      setMode: setMode,
      state: state,
      load: load
    };
  }

  window.weld.promptforge = {
    create: create,
    MODES: ['faithful', 'balanced', 'creative'],
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.promptforge;

  })();

  // ---- weld-genparams ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.genparams) return window.weld.genparams;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.genparams: one shape for "how should this image be generated".
  //
  // Every image front-end ends up with the same sprawling parameter set --
  // prompt, negative prompt, aspect ratio, steps, guidance scale, sampler,
  // seed, batch size, and so on. Apps reinvent it, weld.promptforge emits a
  // prompt with no home for the rest, and weld.image just forwards whatever
  // opts it's handed. weld.genparams gives that set a name and a default:
  //
  //   var p = weld.genparams.create({ prompt: 'a fox in snow', steps: 30 });
  //   var fixed = weld.genparams.validate(p);          // clamps + warns
  //   var forImage = weld.genparams.toImageOpts(fixed); // -> weld.image.generate
  //   var remixed = weld.genparams.remix(p, { seed: 12345, cfgScale: 9 });
  //
  // It calls NO backend. It just normalizes, so the rest of the suite agrees
  // on one schema and an app can degrade gracefully: a backend that ignores
  // cfgScale still gets a valid prompt + size, never a crash.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  // Named aspect ratios -> Perchance-legal t2i sizes (512/768 grid).
  // (Perchance's text-to-image-plugin only accepts these four boxes.)
  var ASPECTS = {
    square:    { ratio: '1:1',  width: 512, height: 512 },
    portrait:  { ratio: '2:3',  width: 512, height: 768 },
    landscape: { ratio: '3:2',  width: 768, height: 512 },
    large:     { ratio: '1:1',  width: 768, height: 768 }
  };

  // The full default schema. Fields a backend doesn't understand are simply
  // ignored downstream; nothing here forces a particular generator.
  function defaults() {
    return {
      prompt: '',
      negativePrompt: '',
      aspect: 'square',          // a key of ASPECTS, or set width/height directly
      width: null,               // if set, overrides aspect
      height: null,
      steps: 25,                 // sampling steps
      cfgScale: 7,               // guidance / how hard to follow the prompt
      sampler: 'default',        // sampler/scheduler name (backend-specific)
      seed: null,                // null = random each run
      batchSize: 1,              // how many images to request
      clipSkip: 1,
      strength: null,            // img2img/denoise strength, 0..1 (null = n/a)
      style: null,               // a weld.image style preset name, optional
      conditioning: null,        // optional ControlNet-style block (see below)
      extra: null                // escape hatch for backend-specific fields
    };
  }

  // Allowed ranges for clamping. Kept deliberately generous; a backend may
  // narrow further. Each range is a two-element min/max pair.
  var RANGES = {
    steps:     [1, 150],
    cfgScale:  [1, 30],
    batchSize: [1, 8],
    clipSkip:  [1, 12],
    strength:  [0, 1]
  };

  function clampNum(v, lohi, fallback) {
    var n = Number(v);
    if (!isFinite(n)) return fallback;
    if (n < lohi[0]) return lohi[0];
    if (n > lohi[1]) return lohi[1];
    return n;
  }

  // create(overrides): a fully-populated params object (defaults + your keys).
  function create(overrides) {
    var p = defaults();
    if (overrides && typeof overrides === 'object') {
      for (var k in overrides) {
        if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(overrides, k)) Reflect.set(p, k, Reflect.get(overrides, k));
      }
    }
    return p;
  }

  // resolveSize(p): figure out the final width/height. Explicit width+height
  // win; otherwise the named aspect resolves to a legal box.
  function resolveSize(p) {
    if (p && p.width && p.height) return { width: p.width | 0, height: p.height | 0, ratio: null };
    var a = (p && Reflect.get(ASPECTS, p.aspect)) ? Reflect.get(ASPECTS, p.aspect) : ASPECTS.square;
    return { width: a.width, height: a.height, ratio: a.ratio };
  }

  // validate(p): returns { params, warnings }. Clamps numbers into range,
  // fills missing fields, and notes anything it had to correct. Never throws
  // on bad input; it repairs and warns, because a generator call shouldn't
  // die over a too-high step count.
  function validate(input) {
    var p = create(input);
    var warnings = new Array();

    if (!String(p.prompt || '').trim()) {
      warnings.push('empty prompt -- most backends will hang or error on this');
    }

    var before;
    before = p.steps;     p.steps = clampNum(p.steps, RANGES.steps, 25);          if (p.steps !== Number(before)) warnings.push('steps clamped to ' + p.steps);
    before = p.cfgScale;  p.cfgScale = clampNum(p.cfgScale, RANGES.cfgScale, 7);  if (p.cfgScale !== Number(before)) warnings.push('cfgScale clamped to ' + p.cfgScale);
    before = p.batchSize; p.batchSize = clampNum(p.batchSize, RANGES.batchSize, 1) | 0; if (p.batchSize !== (Number(before) | 0)) warnings.push('batchSize clamped to ' + p.batchSize);
    before = p.clipSkip;  p.clipSkip = clampNum(p.clipSkip, RANGES.clipSkip, 1) | 0; if (p.clipSkip !== (Number(before) | 0)) warnings.push('clipSkip clamped to ' + p.clipSkip);

    if (p.strength != null) {
      before = p.strength; p.strength = clampNum(p.strength, RANGES.strength, null);
      if (p.strength !== Number(before)) warnings.push('strength clamped to ' + p.strength);
    }

    if (p.seed != null) {
      var s = Number(p.seed);
      p.seed = isFinite(s) ? (s | 0) : null;
      if (p.seed == null) warnings.push('seed was not a number -- set to random (null)');
    }

    if (!p.width && !p.height && !Reflect.get(ASPECTS, p.aspect)) {
      warnings.push('unknown aspect "' + p.aspect + '" -- defaulting to square');
      p.aspect = 'square';
    }

    if (p.conditioning) {
      var c = normalizeConditioning(p.conditioning);
      if (!c) { warnings.push('conditioning block was malformed -- dropped'); p.conditioning = null; }
      else p.conditioning = c;
    }

    return { params: p, warnings: warnings };
  }

  // Optional ControlNet-style conditioning. Normalized but never required.
  function normalizeConditioning(c) {
    if (!c || typeof c !== 'object') return null;
    if (!c.image && !c.type) return null;
    return {
      type: String(c.type || 'reference'),     // pose | depth | canny | reference | ...
      image: c.image || null,                  // url/dataURL the backend understands
      strength: c.strength != null ? clampNum(c.strength, [0, 2], 1) : 1,
      scale: c.scale != null ? Number(c.scale) : 1,
      endPercent: c.endPercent != null ? clampNum(c.endPercent, [0, 1], 1) : 1
    };
  }

  // merge(base, overrides): shallow merge producing a NEW params object.
  function merge(base, overrides) {
    var p = create(base);
    if (overrides && typeof overrides === 'object') {
      for (var k in overrides) {
        if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(overrides, k)) Reflect.set(p, k, Reflect.get(overrides, k));
      }
    }
    return p;
  }

  // remix(base, overrides): like merge, but tuned for "take this generation
  // and tweak it"; by default it randomizes the seed (a remix should look
  // different) unless you pin one in the overrides.
  function remix(base, overrides) {
    var p = merge(base, overrides);
    var pinnedSeed = overrides && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(overrides, 'seed');
    if (!pinnedSeed) p.seed = randomSeed();
    return p;
  }

  function randomSeed() { return (Math.floor(Math.random() * 2147483647)) | 0; }

  // toImageOpts(p): produce the opts object weld.image.generate expects.
  // Resolves the size, maps names, and forwards the rest so a richer backend
  // can pick up what it understands. weld.image only needs prompt+resolution,
  // so this always yields something it can run.
  function toImageOpts(input) {
    var v = validate(input);
    var p = v.params;
    var size = resolveSize(p);
    var opts = {
      prompt: p.prompt,
      negativePrompt: p.negativePrompt || undefined,
      resolution: size.width + 'x' + size.height,
      width: size.width,
      height: size.height,
      steps: p.steps,
      cfgScale: p.cfgScale,
      guidanceScale: p.cfgScale,     // alias many backends use
      sampler: p.sampler !== 'default' ? p.sampler : undefined,
      seed: p.seed != null ? p.seed : undefined,
      batchSize: p.batchSize,
      clipSkip: p.clipSkip,
      strength: p.strength != null ? p.strength : undefined,
      style: p.style || undefined
    };
    if (p.conditioning) opts.conditioning = p.conditioning;
    if (p.extra && typeof p.extra === 'object') {
      for (var k in p.extra) { if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(p.extra, k)) Reflect.set(opts, k, Reflect.get(p.extra, k)); }
    }
    return opts;
  }

  // A compact human-readable description of a params set, for UIs/tooltips.
  function describe(input) {
    var p = create(input);
    var size = resolveSize(p);
    var bits = new Array();
    bits.push(size.width + 'x' + size.height + (size.ratio ? ' (' + size.ratio + ')' : ''));
    bits.push(p.steps + ' steps');
    bits.push('cfg ' + p.cfgScale);
    if (p.seed != null) bits.push('seed ' + p.seed);
    if (p.batchSize > 1) bits.push('x' + p.batchSize);
    if (p.style) bits.push('style: ' + p.style);
    if (p.conditioning) bits.push('+' + p.conditioning.type);
    return bits.join(' / ');
  }

  function aspectNames() { return Object.keys(ASPECTS); }

  window.weld.genparams = {
    defaults: defaults,
    create: create,
    validate: validate,
    merge: merge,
    remix: remix,
    toImageOpts: toImageOpts,
    resolveSize: resolveSize,
    describe: describe,
    aspects: ASPECTS,
    aspectNames: aspectNames,
    ranges: RANGES,
    randomSeed: randomSeed,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.genparams;

  })();
  // ---- weld-quota ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.quota) return;

  var STORAGE_KEY = 'weld-quota-state';
  var watchers = [];
  var lastEstimate = null;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // STORAGE ESTIMATION
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function estimate() {
    if (!navigator.storage || typeof navigator.storage.estimate !== 'function') {
      var unsupported = {
        used: 0, available: 0, total: 0, percentUsed: 0,
        supported: false, usageDetails: null
      };
      lastEstimate = unsupported;
      return Promise.resolve(unsupported);
    }
    return navigator.storage.estimate().then(function(est) {
      var used = est.usage || 0;
      var total = est.quota || 0;
      var available = Math.max(0, total - used);
      var percentUsed = total > 0 ? (used / total) * 100 : 0;
      var result = {
        used: used,
        available: available,
        total: total,
        percentUsed: percentUsed,
        supported: true,
        usageDetails: est.usageDetails || null
      };
      lastEstimate = result;
      checkWatchers(result);
      return result;
    });
  }

  function formatBytes(bytes) {
    if (bytes == null || isNaN(bytes)) return '?';
    if (bytes < 1024) return bytes + ' B';
    if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) return (bytes / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB';
    if (bytes < 1024 * 1024 * 1024) return (bytes / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' MB';
    return (bytes / 1024 / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2) + ' GB';
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // STORAGE WATCHERS
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function watch(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var w = {
      threshold: opts.threshold != null ? opts.threshold : 80,
      onCross: typeof opts.onCross === 'function' ? opts.onCross : function(){},
      every: opts.every || 60000,
      crossed: false,
      interval: null
    };
    watchers.push(w);
    w.interval = setInterval(estimate, w.every);
    estimate(); // initial check
    return function stop() {
      clearInterval(w.interval);
      var i = watchers.indexOf(w);
      if (i !== -1) watchers.splice(i, 1);
    };
  }

  function checkWatchers(est) {
    for (var i = 0; i < watchers.length; i++) {
      var w = watchers[i];
      var over = est.percentUsed >= w.threshold;
      if (over !== w.crossed) {
        w.crossed = over;
        try { w.onCross(est, over); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // RATE LIMITERS - sliding window, persisted
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  var rateConfigs = {};

  function loadRateState() {
    try {
      var raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (!raw) return {};
      return JSON.parse(raw) || {};
    } catch (e) { return {}; }
  }

  function saveRateState(state) {
    try { localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state)); }
    catch (e) { /* quota or disabled */ }
  }

  function pruneOld(timestamps, windowMs) {
    var cutoff = Date.now() - windowMs;
    var out = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < timestamps.length; i++) {
      if (timestamps[i] >= cutoff) out.push(timestamps[i]);
    }
    return out;
  }

  function makeStatus(name, timestamps, cfg, allowed) {
    var remaining = Math.max(0, cfg.maxPerWindow - timestamps.length);
    var resetsIn = timestamps.length > 0
      ? Math.max(0, (timestamps[0] + cfg.windowMs) - Date.now())
      : 0;
    return {
      name: name,
      allowed: allowed,
      remaining: remaining,
      used: timestamps.length,
      total: cfg.maxPerWindow,
      windowMs: cfg.windowMs,
      resetsIn: resetsIn
    };
  }

  function createRate(name, opts) {
    if (!name || typeof name !== 'string') throw new Error('rate name required');
    opts = opts || {};
    rateConfigs[name] = {
      maxPerWindow: opts.maxPerWindow || 60,
      windowMs: opts.windowMs || 60000
    };
    return getRate(name);
  }

  function getRate(name) {
    return {
      name: name,
      check: function() { return checkRate(name); },
      consume: function() { return consumeRate(name); },
      reset: function() { return resetRate(name); },
      history: function() { return rateHistory(name); }
    };
  }

  function checkRate(name) {
    var cfg = rateConfigs[name];
    if (!cfg) throw new Error('unknown rate: ' + name);
    var state = loadRateState();
    var timestamps = pruneOld(state[name] || [], cfg.windowMs);
    return makeStatus(name, timestamps, cfg, timestamps.length < cfg.maxPerWindow);
  }

  function consumeRate(name) {
    var cfg = rateConfigs[name];
    if (!cfg) throw new Error('unknown rate: ' + name);
    var state = loadRateState();
    var timestamps = pruneOld(state[name] || [], cfg.windowMs);
    if (timestamps.length >= cfg.maxPerWindow) {
      return makeStatus(name, timestamps, cfg, false);
    }
    timestamps.push(Date.now());
    state[name] = timestamps;
    saveRateState(state);
    return makeStatus(name, timestamps, cfg, true);
  }

  function resetRate(name) {
    var state = loadRateState();
    delete state[name];
    saveRateState(state);
    return true;
  }

  function rateHistory(name) {
    var cfg = rateConfigs[name];
    if (!cfg) return [];
    var state = loadRateState();
    return pruneOld(state[name] || [], cfg.windowMs);
  }

  function listRates() { return Object.keys(rateConfigs); }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // API
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  window.weld.quota = {
    // Storage
    estimate: estimate,
    lastEstimate: function() { return lastEstimate; },
    watch: watch,
    formatBytes: formatBytes,

    // Rate limiting
    rate: {
      create: createRate,
      get: getRate,
      check: checkRate,
      consume: consumeRate,
      reset: resetRate,
      history: rateHistory,
      list: listRates
    },

    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.quota;


  })();

  // ---- weld-backup ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.backup) return window.weld.backup;

  var FORMAT_VERSION = 1;     // bumped only if envelope format changes (not the data inside)
  var SIGNATURE = 'weld-backup';

  // Build an export envelope from arbitrary data
  function exportData(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var envelope = {
      signature: SIGNATURE,
      formatVersion: FORMAT_VERSION,
      dataVersion: opts.version != null ? opts.version : 1,
      generator: opts.generator || 'unknown',
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      metadata: opts.metadata || {},
      data: opts.data || {},
    };
    return envelope;
  }

  // Serialize envelope to a JSON Blob
  function exportBlob(opts) {
    var env = exportData(opts);
    var json = JSON.stringify(env, null, 2);
    return new Blob([ json], { type: 'application/json' });
  }

  // Trigger a browser download
  function download(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var blob = exportBlob(opts);
    var fname = opts.filename;
    if (!fname) {
      var stamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-').slice(0, 19);
      fname = (opts.generator || 'backup') + '-' + stamp + '.weld.json';
    }
    var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = fname;
    document.body.appendChild(a);
    a.click();
    document.body.removeChild(a);
    setTimeout(function(){ URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 1000);
    return fname;
  }

  // Read a File/Blob/string into an envelope, validating signature
  function readEnvelope(source) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      if (typeof source === 'string') {
        try { resolve(JSON.parse(source)); }
        catch (e) { reject(new Error('Not valid JSON: ' + e.message)); }
        return;
      }
      if (source instanceof Blob || source instanceof File) {
        var reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(){
          try { resolve(JSON.parse(reader.result)); }
          catch (e) { reject(new Error('Not valid JSON: ' + e.message)); }
        };
        reader.onerror = function(){ reject(reader.error); };
        reader.readAsText(source);
        return;
      }
      if (source && typeof source === 'object') {
        resolve(source);
        return;
      }
      reject(new Error('Unsupported source type'));
    });
  }

  function validateEnvelope(env) {
    if (!env || typeof env !== 'object') {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Not an object' };
    }
    if (env.signature !== SIGNATURE) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Missing or wrong signature (expected "' + SIGNATURE + '")' };
    }
    if (env.formatVersion == null) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Missing formatVersion' };
    }
    if (env.formatVersion > FORMAT_VERSION) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Envelope is newer (format v' + env.formatVersion + ') than this importer (v' + FORMAT_VERSION + ')' };
    }
    return {
      ok: true,
      formatVersion: env.formatVersion,
      dataVersion: env.dataVersion,
      generator: env.generator,
      createdAt: env.createdAt,
      metadata: env.metadata || {},
    };
  }

  function validate(source) {
    return readEnvelope(source).then(validateEnvelope).catch(function(e){
      return { ok: false, error: e.message };
    });
  }

  // Apply data migrations (provided by caller) to bring dataVersion up to current
  function migrateData(env, migrations) {
    migrations = migrations || {};
    var versions = Object.keys(migrations).map(Number).sort(function(a, b){ return a - b; });
    var maxVer = versions.length ? Math.max.apply(null, versions) : env.dataVersion;
    var data = env.data;
    var fromVer = env.dataVersion;
    if (fromVer < maxVer) {
      for (var v = fromVer + 1; v <= maxVer; v++) {
        if (migrations[v]) {
          data = migrations[v](data) || data;
        }
      }
    }
    return { data: data, fromVersion: fromVer, toVersion: maxVer };
  }

  // Import an envelope - returns the data (optionally migrated)
  function importData(source, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    return readEnvelope(source).then(function(env){
      var v = validateEnvelope(env);
      if (!v.ok) throw new Error(v.error);
      var migrated = migrateData(env, opts.migrations);
      return {
        data: migrated.data,
        generator: env.generator,
        fromVersion: migrated.fromVersion,
        toVersion: migrated.toVersion,
        metadata: env.metadata || {},
        createdAt: env.createdAt,
        importedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
    });
  }

  // Show a hidden file picker, resolve with selected File
  function pickFile(accept) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
      var input = document.createElement('input');
      input.type = 'file';
      input.accept = accept || '.json,.weld.json,application/json';
      input.style.display = 'none';
      input.onchange = function(){
        var f = input.files && input.files[0];
        document.body.removeChild(input);
        if (f) resolve(f);
        else reject(new Error('No file selected'));
      };
      document.body.appendChild(input);
      input.click();
    });
  }

  // Dump an entire weld.migrate DB to an envelope
  function fromDb(db, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var stores = opts.stores || db.storeNames.filter(function(s){ return s.indexOf('_weld') !== 0; });
    var data = {};
    var chain = Promise.resolve();
    stores.forEach(function(s){
      chain = chain.then(function(){
        return db.getAll(s).then(function(items){ data[s] = items; });
      });
    });
    return chain.then(function(){
      return exportData({
        version: opts.version != null ? opts.version : (db.version || 1),
        generator: opts.generator || db.name,
        metadata: Object.assign({ stores: stores, recordCount: countTotal(data) }, opts.metadata || {}),
        data: data,
      });
    });
  }

  // Convenience - dump and download in one call
  function downloadFromDb(db, opts) {
    return fromDb(db, opts).then(function(env){
      var blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(env, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
      var fname = (opts && opts.filename) || (env.generator + '-' + new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-').slice(0, 19) + '.weld.json');
      var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      var a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url; a.download = fname;
      document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); document.body.removeChild(a);
      setTimeout(function(){ URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 1000);
      return { filename: fname, env: env };
    });
  }

  // Restore an envelope into a weld.migrate DB
  // mode: 'merge' (default) - put each item, overwriting same-key
  //       'replace'          - clear store first, then put all
  //       'append'           - only put items whose key doesn't exist
  function toDb(source, db, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var mode = opts.mode || 'merge';
    var onConflict = opts.onConflict; // (existing, incoming) => resolved | null to skip

    return importData(source, { migrations: opts.migrations }).then(function(result){
      var data = result.data;
      var stores = opts.stores || Object.keys(data);
      var summary = { imported: {}, skipped: {}, conflicts: {} };

      var chain = Promise.resolve();
      stores.forEach(function(s){
        if (!data[s]) return;
        var items = data[s];

        chain = chain.then(function(){
          if (mode === 'replace') {
            return db.clear(s).then(function(){
              return db.bulkPut(s, items);
            }).then(function(){
              summary.imported[s] = items.length;
            });
          }

          if (mode === 'append') {
            // Check each item's key
            var skipped = 0, imported = 0;
            var toPut = [];
            var lookups = items.map(function(item){
              // We need the keyPath of the store to know the key - use raw IDB
              var t = db._db.transaction([ s], 'readonly');
              var store = t.objectStore(s);
              var keyPath = store.keyPath;
              var key = (typeof keyPath === 'string') ? item[keyPath] : null;
              return new Promise(function(resolve){
                if (key == null) { toPut.push(item); imported++; resolve(); return; }
                var r = store.get(key);
                r.onsuccess = function(){
                  if (r.result == null) { toPut.push(item); imported++; }
                  else { skipped++; }
                  resolve();
                };
                r.onerror = function(){ resolve(); };
              });
            });
            return Promise.all(lookups).then(function(){
              summary.imported[s] = imported;
              summary.skipped[s] = skipped;
              if (toPut.length) return db.bulkPut(s, toPut);
            });
          }

          // merge mode
          if (!onConflict) {
            return db.bulkPut(s, items).then(function(){
              summary.imported[s] = items.length;
            });
          }

          // merge with conflict resolution
          var imported = 0, conflicts = 0;
          var resolved = [];
          var lookups = items.map(function(item){
            var t = db._db.transaction([ s], 'readonly');
            var store = t.objectStore(s);
            var keyPath = store.keyPath;
            var key = (typeof keyPath === 'string') ? item[keyPath] : null;
            return new Promise(function(resolve){
              if (key == null) { resolved.push(item); imported++; resolve(); return; }
              var r = store.get(key);
              r.onsuccess = function(){
                var existing = r.result;
                if (existing == null) { resolved.push(item); imported++; }
                else {
                  conflicts++;
                  var merged = onConflict(existing, item, s);
                  if (merged != null) resolved.push(merged);
                }
                resolve();
              };
              r.onerror = function(){ resolve(); };
            });
          });
          return Promise.all(lookups).then(function(){
            summary.imported[s] = imported;
            summary.conflicts[s] = conflicts;
            if (resolved.length) return db.bulkPut(s, resolved);
          });
        });
      });

      return chain.then(function(){
        summary.fromVersion = result.fromVersion;
        summary.toVersion = result.toVersion;
        summary.generator = result.generator;
        return summary;
      });
    });
  }

  // Count total records across all stores
  function countTotal(data) {
    var n = 0;
    Object.keys(data).forEach(function(k){
      if (Array.isArray(data[k])) n += data[k].length;
    });
    return n;
  }

  // SHARE LINK: compress + upload + URL
  // uploader: the uploadPlugin function (from DSL import)
  // opts: { paramName?, generatorName? }
  function share(data, uploader, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    if (typeof uploader !== 'function') {
      return Promise.reject(new Error('backup.share: uploader function required (pass uploadPlugin)'));
    }
    var json = JSON.stringify(data);
    // Compress with gzip if available, otherwise send raw
    var blobPromise;
    if (typeof CompressionStream !== 'undefined') {
      blobPromise = new Response(
        new Blob([ json]).stream().pipeThrough(new CompressionStream('gzip'))
      ).blob();
    } else {
      blobPromise = Promise.resolve(new Blob([ json], { type: 'application/json' }));
    }
    return blobPromise.then(function(blob) {
      return Promise.resolve(uploader(blob));
    }).then(function(result) {
      if (!result || result.error) {
        throw new Error('upload failed: ' + (result && result.error || 'unknown'));
      }
      var url = String(result.url || result);
      // Extract filename from CDN URL
      var fileName = url.replace('https://user.uploads.dev/file/', '');
      var paramName = opts.paramName || 'data';
      var base = 'https://perchance.org/' + (opts.generatorName || window.generatorName || 'generator');
      return base + '?' + paramName + '=' + encodeURIComponent(fileName);
    });
  }

  // CONSUME SHARE: check URL for shared data, fetch + decompress
  // fetcher: a fetch-compatible function (superFetch or window.fetch)
  // opts: { paramName?, onFound? }
  function consumeShare(fetcher, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var paramName = opts.paramName || 'data';
    var params;
    try { params = new URL(window.location.href).searchParams; }
    catch (e) { return Promise.resolve(null); }
    var raw = params.get(paramName);
    if (!raw) return Promise.resolve(null);

    // Extract just the filename (handle legacy formats with ~ separator)
    var fileName = raw.split('~').slice(-1)[0];
    if (!fileName) return Promise.resolve(null);

    var fetchFn = typeof fetcher === 'function' ? fetcher : window.fetch;
    var cdnUrl = 'https://user.uploads.dev/file/' + fileName;
    return Promise.resolve(fetchFn(cdnUrl, {
      signal: typeof AbortSignal !== 'undefined' && AbortSignal.timeout ? AbortSignal.timeout(15000) : undefined
    })).then(function(r) {
      if (r && typeof r.blob === 'function') return r.blob();
      // superFetch might return different shape
      if (r instanceof Blob) return r;
      return new Blob([typeof r === 'string' ? r : JSON.stringify(r)]);
    }).then(function(blob) {
      // Try to decompress
      if (typeof DecompressionStream !== 'undefined') {
        return new Response(
          blob.stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip'))
        ).text().catch(function() {
          // Not gzipped, try raw
          return blob.text();
        });
      }
      return blob.text();
    }).then(function(text) {
      try { return JSON.parse(text); }
      catch (e) { throw new Error('backup.consumeShare: invalid JSON in share data'); }
    }).then(function(data) {
      if (typeof opts.onFound === 'function') opts.onFound(data);
      return data;
    });
  }

  // PUBLIC API
  // ---- upload-plugin helpers: unguessable-id blob store / link-identity
  //      (same injected-uploader style as share/consumeShare) ----
  var UPLOAD_PREFIX = 'https://user.uploads.dev/file/';
  function parseUploadId(url) {
    try {
      var base = (typeof location !== 'undefined' && location.href) ? location.href : 'https://x/';
      var path = new URL(String(url), base).pathname;
      var name = (path.split('/').filter(Boolean).pop() || '');
      var id = (name.split('.')[0] || '').toLowerCase().replace(/[^0-9a-f]/g, '');
      return (id.length === 32 && /^[0-9a-f]+$/.test(id)) ? id : '';
    } catch (e) { return ''; }
  }
  function safeUploadUrl(url) {
    try { var u = new URL(String(url)); if (u.protocol !== 'https:') return ''; if (u.hostname !== 'user.uploads.dev') return ''; if (u.pathname.indexOf('/file/') !== 0) return ''; return u.href; } catch (e) { return ''; }
  }
  function upload(uploader, blobOrString) {
    if (typeof uploader !== 'function') return Promise.reject(new Error('backup.upload: uploader function required (pass uploadPlugin)'));
    return Promise.resolve(uploader(blobOrString)).then(function (res) {
      if (!res || res.error || !res.url) throw new Error('backup.upload: upload failed: ' + ((res && res.error) || 'unknown'));
      return { url: res.url, id: parseUploadId(res.url) };
    });
  }
  function uploadJson(uploader, obj) { return upload(uploader, JSON.stringify(obj)); }
  function fetchJson(fetcher, url) {
    var f = fetcher || (typeof fetch !== 'undefined' ? fetch : null);
    if (typeof f !== 'function') return Promise.reject(new Error('backup.fetchJson: fetcher function required'));
    return Promise.resolve(f(url)).then(function (r) { return (r && typeof r.text === 'function') ? r.text() : r; }).then(function (t) { try { return JSON.parse(t); } catch (e) { throw new Error('backup.fetchJson: invalid JSON'); } });
  }

  window.weld.backup = {
    exportData: exportData,
    exportBlob: exportBlob,
    download: download,
    importData: importData,
    validate: validate,
    pickFile: pickFile,
    fromDb: fromDb,
    downloadFromDb: downloadFromDb,
    toDb: toDb,
    share: share,
    upload: upload,
    uploadJson: uploadJson,
    fetchJson: fetchJson,
    parseUploadId: parseUploadId,
    safeUploadUrl: safeUploadUrl,
    consumeShare: consumeShare,
    FORMAT_VERSION: FORMAT_VERSION,
    version: '1.1.0',
  };

  return window.weld.backup;


  })();
  // ---- weld-privacy ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.privacy) return window.weld.privacy;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.privacy: make an app legible about where its data goes.
  //
  // Duck.ai's best idea is showing, per model, what privacy guarantee
  // applies before you use it: anonymized, zero-retention, no-training,
  // and so on. weld.privacy ports the *pattern* (not the guarantees, which
  // are platform-specific): a small claim vocabulary, an honest registry of
  // how the suite's own backends behave, and a way to render a data-handling
  // summary an app can show its users.
  //
  //   weld.privacy.claimsFor('kv')   returns an array of claim objects
  //   weld.privacy.summary of the backends an app uses -> human-readable text
  //   weld.privacy.register a backend with its claim kinds
  //
  // IMPORTANT HONESTY RULE: a claim describes data-handling POSTURE; it does
  // NOT enforce anything. The labels here reflect what Perchance's backends
  // actually do, to the best of documented behavior. An app must not attach
  // a claim it can't stand behind; an overstated label is worse than none.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  // The claim vocabulary. Each kind has a stable id, a short title, a
  // plain-language detail, and a coarse 'leaves-device' flag apps can sort on.
  var KINDS = {
    'local-only': {
      title: 'Stays on this device',
      detail: 'Data is kept in this browser only (IndexedDB / localStorage) and is never sent anywhere. Clearing your browser data removes it.',
      leavesDevice: false
    },
    'anonymized': {
      title: 'Sent without identifying you',
      detail: 'Data is sent to a backend with identifying metadata stripped or proxied, so the request is not tied to your identity.',
      leavesDevice: true
    },
    'server-stored': {
      title: 'Stored on a server',
      detail: 'Data is stored on a remote server and persists there (often so it can sync across your devices). It is not only on this device.',
      leavesDevice: true
    },
    'public': {
      title: 'Publicly accessible',
      detail: 'Data is uploaded to a public URL that anyone with the link can access. Do not put anything sensitive here.',
      leavesDevice: true
    },
    'expiring': {
      title: 'Auto-deletes later',
      detail: 'Data is stored with an expiry and is removed automatically after a set time.',
      leavesDevice: true
    },
    'third-party': {
      title: 'Handled by a third party',
      detail: 'Data passes through a service outside your control, whose own data-handling policy applies.',
      leavesDevice: true
    },
    'transient': {
      title: 'Not stored at all',
      detail: 'Data is used for a single request and not retained after the response.',
      leavesDevice: true
    }
  };

  function kindIds() { return Object.keys(KINDS); }
  function describeKind(id) {
    var k = Reflect.get(KINDS, id);
    return k ? { kind: id, title: k.title, detail: k.detail, leavesDevice: k.leavesDevice } : null;
  }
