  // Honest, pre-registered claims for the suite's own backends. These reflect
  // documented Perchance behavior; an app can override or extend them.
  //   persist/history/backup -> local IndexedDB only          -> local-only
  //   cache/state            -> in-memory or local            -> local-only
  //   kv                     -> kv-plugin, server cross-device -> server-stored
  //   upload                 -> public URL (+ optional expiry) -> public (+expiring)
  //   stream/image           -> Perchance broker (proxied)     -> anonymized + third-party
  //   fetch                  -> superFetch proxy (strips hdrs) -> anonymized + third-party
  //   registry               -> reads Perchance public API     -> transient + third-party
  //   report                 -> encrypted, expiring upload     -> public + expiring
  var REGISTRY = {
    persist:  ['local-only'],
    history:  ['local-only'],
    backup:   ['local-only'],
    cache:    ['local-only'],
    state:    ['local-only'],
    memory:   ['local-only'],
    kv:       ['server-stored'],
    upload:   ['public', 'expiring'],
    report:   ['public', 'expiring'],
    stream:   ['anonymized', 'third-party'],
    image:    ['anonymized', 'third-party'],
    fetch:    ['anonymized', 'third-party'],
    registry: ['transient', 'third-party']
  };

  // register(name, kinds): declare (or override) the claims for a backend.
  // kinds is an array of claim ids; unknown ids are dropped with no throw.
  function register(name, kinds) {
    if (!name) return null;
    var list = (Array.isArray(kinds) ? kinds : Array.of(kinds)).filter(function (k) { return !!Reflect.get(KINDS, k); });
    Reflect.set(REGISTRY, String(name), list);
    return claimsFor(name);
  }

  // claimsFor(name): the resolved claim objects for a backend (or empty array).
  function claimsFor(name) {
    var ids = Reflect.get(REGISTRY, String(name)) || new Array();
    return ids.map(describeKind).filter(Boolean);
  }

  // worst-case posture across a set of backends: does ANY of them leave the
  // device? Useful for a single at-a-glance indicator.
  function leavesDevice(names) {
    return toArray(names).some(function (n) {
      return claimsFor(n).some(function (c) { return c.leavesDevice; });
    });
  }

  function toArray(x) { return Array.isArray(x) ? x : (x == null ? new Array() : Array.of(x)); }

  // summary(names): a human-readable data-handling digest for the backends an
  // app uses. Apps can show this in a privacy panel or an info modal.
  function summary(names) {
    var list = toArray(names);
    if (!list.length) return 'No backends declared.';
    var lines = new Array();
    lines.push(leavesDevice(list)
      ? 'Some data leaves this device:'
      : 'All data stays on this device.');
    if (cspRestricted()) {
      lines.push('(Running in Perchance ?$csp restricted mode: outbound external requests are blocked by the platform.)');
    }
    list.forEach(function (n) {
      var claims = claimsFor(n);
      if (!claims.length) {
        lines.push('  ' + n + ': (no privacy claim declared)');
      } else {
        lines.push('  ' + n + ': ' + claims.map(function (c) { return c.title; }).join('; '));
      }
    });
    return lines.join('\n');
  }

  // report(names): a structured version of summary() for building UI.
  function report(names) {
    var list = toArray(names);
    return {
      leavesDevice: leavesDevice(list),
      cspRestricted: cspRestricted(),
      backends: list.map(function (n) { return { name: n, claims: claimsFor(n) }; })
    };
  }

  // Audit helper: which declared backends keep data only on-device?
  function localOnly(names) {
    return toArray(names).filter(function (n) {
      var c = claimsFor(n);
      return c.length && c.every(function (x) { return !x.leavesDevice; });
    });
  }

  // Perchance's ?$csp URL mode (perchance.org/custom-content-security-policy)
  // restricts a generator's ability to talk to external servers; adding
  // ?$csp to a page's URL reduces how much a user must trust the author.
  // It's a real, current data-handling fact, so weld.privacy surfaces it:
  // an app can tell the user "you're running in restricted mode" and adjust
  // claims accordingly (outbound third-party calls won't go through).
  function cspRestricted() {
    try {
      var q = (typeof location !== 'undefined' && location.search) ? location.search : '';
      var h = (typeof location !== 'undefined' && location.href) ? location.href : '';
      // Perchance uses a bare ?$csp flag; match it in the query or full URL.
      return /[?&]\$csp(\b|=|&|$)/.test(q) || /[?&]\$csp(\b|=|&|$)/.test(h);
    } catch (e) { return false; }
  }

  window.weld.privacy = {
    kinds: KINDS,
    kindIds: kindIds,
    describeKind: describeKind,
    register: register,
    claimsFor: claimsFor,
    leavesDevice: leavesDevice,
    localOnly: localOnly,
    summary: summary,
    report: report,
    cspRestricted: cspRestricted,
    version: '1.1.0'
  };

  return window.weld.privacy;

  })();

  // ---- weld-persona ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.persona) return window.weld.persona;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.persona: a richer character model than a freeform bio string.
  //
  // Eight 0-100 trait sliders are interpolated into a 4-axis vector
  // (warmth, energy, control, openness), matched to the nearest archetype,
  // and rendered as a prose dossier you prepend to the system prompt.
  // Moods become concrete physical tells + speech patterns + inner
  // sensations, scaled by intensity. Relationships become a few sharp
  // lines about how the character treats someone. All deterministic
  // tables and arithmetic: no model, no network, no dependencies.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  // Each anchor maps a slider band to an adjective + a contribution to the
  // 4-axis vector { w: warmth, e: energy, c: control, o: openness }.
  var ANCHORS = {
    warmth: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'icy and hostile',            d: { w:-1.0, e:-0.2, c: 0.3, o:-0.8 } },
      { min: 21,  adj: 'guarded and aloof',          d: { w:-0.5, e:-0.3, c: 0.1, o:-0.5 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'neutral and even',           d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 61,  adj: 'warm and approachable',      d: { w: 0.6, e: 0.3, c:-0.2, o: 0.4 } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'affectionate and doting',    d: { w: 1.0, e: 0.6, c:-0.4, o: 0.6 } }
    ],
    assertiveness: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'deferential and apologetic', d: { w: 0.2, e:-0.6, c:-1.0, o:-0.3 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'balanced and compromising',  d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 61,  adj: 'confident and bold',         d: { w:-0.1, e: 0.5, c: 0.7, o: 0.2 } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'dominant and commanding',    d: { w:-0.4, e: 0.8, c: 1.0, o:-0.2 } }
    ],
    reactivity: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'stoic and unflappable',      d: { w:-0.2, e:-0.7, c: 0.8, o:-0.5 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'emotionally steady',         d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'volatile and intense',       d: { w: 0.2, e: 1.0, c:-0.7, o: 0.3 } }
    ],
    curiosity: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'concrete and closed-minded', d: { w:-0.4, e:-0.5, c: 0.2, o:-1.0 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'moderately inquisitive',     d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'restless and probing',       d: { w: 0.1, e: 0.6, c:-0.2, o: 1.0 } }
    ],
    empathy: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'detached and callous',       d: { w:-0.9, e:-0.4, c: 0.4, o:-0.6 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'reasonably understanding',   d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'deeply attuned to others',   d: { w: 1.0, e: 0.3, c:-0.6, o: 0.6 } }
    ],
    caution: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'reckless and impulsive',     d: { w:-0.1, e: 0.9, c:-0.5, o: 0.7 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'calculated and careful',     d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'wary and risk-averse',       d: { w:-0.3, e:-0.8, c: 0.7, o:-0.7 } }
    ],
    playfulness: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'earnest and humorless',      d: { w:-0.5, e:-0.6, c: 0.5, o:-0.7 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'balanced in humor',          d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'witty and mischievous',      d: { w: 0.6, e: 0.9, c:-0.5, o: 0.8 } }
    ],
    confidence: [
      { min: 0,   adj: 'self-doubting and timid',    d: { w:-0.1, e:-0.5, c:-0.7, o:-0.4 } },
      { min: 41,  adj: 'secure in themselves',       d: { w: 0,   e: 0,   c: 0,   o: 0   } },
      { min: 81,  adj: 'unshakably self-assured',    d: { w: 0.1, e: 0.6, c: 0.8, o: 0.2 } }
    ]
  };

  var ARCHETYPES = {
    'The Stoic':      { w:-0.7, e:-1.0, c: 0.9, o:-0.5 },
    'The Empath':     { w: 1.0, e: 0.5, c:-0.8, o: 0.8 },
    'The Scholar':    { w:-0.4, e:-0.5, c: 0.5, o: 1.2 },
    'The Instigator': { w: 0.4, e: 1.5, c: 0.8, o: 0.6 },
    'The Guardian':   { w: 0.8, e:-0.4, c: 1.2, o:-0.8 },
    'The Maverick':   { w: 0.2, e: 1.0, c:-1.0, o: 1.0 },
    'The Charmer':    { w: 1.0, e: 0.8, c: 0.2, o: 0.4 },
    'The Recluse':    { w:-0.8, e:-0.8, c:-0.2, o: 0.2 }
  };

  function clamp(v) { return Math.max(0, Math.min(100, Number(v) || 0)); }

  // Interpolate a slider value across its anchor bands.
  function interpolate(val, key) {
    var list = ANCHORS[key];
    if (!list) return { adj: '', d: { w:0, e:0, c:0, o:0 } };
    val = clamp(val);
    if (val <= list[0].min) return { adj: list[0].adj, d: list[0].d };
    if (val >= list[list.length - 1].min) return { adj: list[list.length - 1].adj, d: list[list.length - 1].d };
    var low = list[0], high = list[list.length - 1];
    for (var i = 0; i < list.length - 1; i++) {
      if (val >= list[i].min && val <= list[i + 1].min) { low = list[i]; high = list[i + 1]; break; }
    }
    var f = (val - low.min) / ((high.min - low.min) || 1);
    return {
      adj: val > (low.min + (high.min - low.min) / 2) ? high.adj : low.adj,
      d: {
        w: low.d.w + (high.d.w - low.d.w) * f,
        e: low.d.e + (high.d.e - low.d.e) * f,
        c: low.d.c + (high.d.c - low.d.c) * f,
        o: low.d.o + (high.d.o - low.d.o) * f
      }
    };
  }

  function nearestArchetype(vec) {
    var best = 'Balanced Individual', min = Infinity;
    for (var name in ARCHETYPES) {
      var c = ARCHETYPES[name];
      var dist = Math.sqrt(
        Math.pow(vec.w - c.w, 2) + Math.pow(vec.e - c.e, 2) +
        Math.pow(vec.c - c.c, 2) + Math.pow(vec.o - c.o, 2));
      if (dist < min) { min = dist; best = name; }
    }
    return best;
  }

  // dossier(traits) -> { archetype, vector, text, results }.
  // traits: { warmth, assertiveness, reactivity, curiosity, empathy,
  //           caution, playfulness, confidence } each 0-100 (missing = 50).
  function dossier(traits) {
    traits = traits || {};
    var vec = { w: 0, e: 0, c: 0, o: 0 };
    var results = {};
    var keys = Object.keys(ANCHORS);
    keys.forEach(function (k) {
      var val = traits[k] == null ? 50 : traits[k];
      var interp = interpolate(val, k);
      results[k] = { value: clamp(val), adj: interp.adj };
      vec.w += interp.d.w; vec.e += interp.d.e; vec.c += interp.d.c; vec.o += interp.d.o;
    });
    var archetype = nearestArchetype(vec);

    var drivers = [], anchors = [];
    keys.forEach(function (k) {
      var v = results[k].value;
      if (v < 30 || v > 70) drivers.push(results[k].adj);
      else anchors.push(results[k].adj);
    });

    // A "bridge" line for an interesting internal contrast.
    var bridge = '';
    if ((traits.empathy || 50) > 75 && (traits.reactivity || 50) < 35) {
      bridge = 'Beneath a ' + results.reactivity.adj + ' surface, they are ' + results.empathy.adj + '. ';
    } else if ((traits.warmth || 50) > 75 && (traits.playfulness || 50) < 25) {
      bridge = 'Their ' + results.warmth.adj + ' nature is carried with a ' + results.playfulness.adj + ' seriousness. ';
    } else if ((traits.confidence || 50) < 25 && (traits.assertiveness || 50) > 70) {
      bridge = 'They push hard and ' + results.assertiveness.adj + ', yet underneath they are ' + results.confidence.adj + '. ';
    }

    var headline = 'They embody the archetype of ' + archetype + '.';
    var core = drivers.length ? ('At core, they are ' + listJoin(drivers) + '.') : 'They are a balanced individual.';
    var base = anchors.length ? (' This rests on a ' + listJoin(anchors) + ' baseline.') : '';
    var text = headline + '\n\n' + bridge + core + base;

    return { archetype: archetype, vector: vec, text: text, results: results };
  }

  function listJoin(arr) {
    if (arr.length <= 1) return arr.join('');
    if (arr.length === 2) return arr[0] + ' and ' + arr[1];
    return arr.slice(0, -1).join(', ') + ', and ' + arr[arr.length - 1];
  }

  // --- moods: concrete sensory tells, scaled by intensity ---
  var MOODS = {
    rage:    { tells:['clenched jaw','white knuckles','flushed face','flared nostrils','a pulsing vein at the temple'], speech:['words come out as snarls','voice rises to a shout','a deadly low whisper','clipped, barking phrases'], inner:['heat flooding the chest','a pounding heart','a roar in the ears','tunnel vision'] },
    anxiety: { tells:['shallow breathing','fidgeting hands','darting eyes','a bitten lip','tightly crossed arms'], speech:['a thin, shaky voice','sentences that trail off','rapid stuttering','frequent throat-clearing'], inner:['a knot in the stomach','jittery energy','cold hands','a sense of being watched'] },
    euphoria:{ tells:['an uncontrollable smile','dilated pupils','wild gestures','bounding energy','bright eyes'], speech:['a fast, musical voice','laughing mid-sentence','excited rambling','a breathless tone'], inner:['lightness in the chest','a feeling of invincibility','a warm glow','crystal mental clarity'] },
    sorrow:  { tells:['downcast eyes','slumped shoulders','a trembling lip','slow movements','a distant stare'], speech:['a quiet, flat voice','long pauses','words that catch','near-silence'], inner:['a heaviness in the chest','a hollow ache','exhaustion','a lump in the throat'] },
    affection:{tells:['soft eyes','a gentle smile','leaning in','an unguarded posture','lingering glances'], speech:['a warm, lowered voice','easy laughter','tender phrasing','using their name often'], inner:['a flutter in the chest','warmth spreading','a pull toward them','quiet contentment'] },
    suspicion:{tells:['narrowed eyes','a half-step back','arms folded','glances at the exits','a tight mouth'], speech:['careful, measured words','probing questions','a cool tone','long deliberate pauses'], inner:['a prickle of doubt','heightened alertness','a coiled readiness','calculation behind the eyes'] },
    neutral: { tells:['a steady gaze','relaxed shoulders','still hands'], speech:['a measured tone','even pacing'], inner:['calm breathing','a quiet mind'] }
  };

  function pickN(arr, n, rand) {
    rand = rand || Math.random;
    var a = arr.slice();
    for (var i = a.length - 1; i > 0; i--) { var j = Math.floor(rand() * (i + 1)); var t = a[i]; a[i] = a[j]; a[j] = t; }
    return a.slice(0, Math.max(0, Math.min(n, a.length)));
  }

  // mood(name, intensity, opts) -> prose injecting physical reality.
  // intensity 0-100; more intensity -> more cues. opts.rand for determinism.
  function mood(name, intensity, opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var key = String(name || '').toLowerCase();
    var known = MOODS[key];
    var prof = known || MOODS.neutral;
    var label = known ? key : 'neutral';
    intensity = clamp(intensity == null ? 50 : intensity);
    var n = intensity > 75 ? 3 : intensity > 40 ? 2 : 1;
    var level = intensity > 75 ? 'overwhelming' : intensity > 40 ? 'evident' : 'subtle';
    var tells = pickN(prof.tells, n, opts.rand);
    var speech = pickN(prof.speech, Math.max(1, n - 1), opts.rand);
    var inner = pickN(prof.inner, Math.max(1, n - 1), opts.rand);
    return 'They are feeling ' + level + ' ' + label + '.\n'
      + 'Physical tells: ' + listJoin(tells) + '.\n'
      + 'In speech: ' + listJoin(speech) + '.\n'
      + 'Inwardly: ' + listJoin(inner) + '.';
  }

  // relationship(rel) -> prose about how they regard someone.
  // rel: { closeness, trust, tension, attraction } each 0-100.
  function relationship(rel) {
    if (!rel) return 'They have no prior history with this person.';
    var p = [];
    var c = rel.closeness || 0, t = rel.trust == null ? 50 : rel.trust, x = rel.tension || 0, a = rel.attraction || 0;
    if (c > 80) p.push('This person is vital to them; the bond is deep.');
    else if (c > 40) p.push('They are friendly and at ease together.');
    else if (c > 15) p.push('They are acquaintances, still feeling each other out.');
    else p.push('This person is essentially a stranger; they keep a polite distance.');
    if (t < 25) p.push('They distrust this person and read hidden motives into their actions.');
    else if (t > 80) p.push('They trust this person almost without reservation.');
    if (x > 70) p.push('The air between them is charged; words feel loaded.');
    if (a > 70) p.push('They feel a strong, distracting pull toward this person.');
    return p.join(' ');
  }

  // systemPrompt(opts) -> one assembled block ready to prepend.
  // opts: { name, traits, mood:{name,intensity}, relationship, extra }
  function systemPrompt(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var parts = [];
    if (opts.name) parts.push('You are ' + opts.name + '.');
    if (opts.traits) parts.push(dossier(opts.traits).text);
    if (opts.mood && opts.mood.name) parts.push(mood(opts.mood.name, opts.mood.intensity, opts));
    if (opts.relationship) parts.push(relationship(opts.relationship));
    if (opts.extra) parts.push(String(opts.extra));
    return parts.join('\n\n');
  }

  window.weld.persona = {
    dossier: dossier,
    mood: mood,
    relationship: relationship,
    systemPrompt: systemPrompt,
    interpolate: interpolate,
    nearestArchetype: nearestArchetype,
    TRAITS: Object.keys(ANCHORS),
    MOODS: Object.keys(MOODS),
    ARCHETYPES: Object.keys(ARCHETYPES),
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.persona;

  })();
  // ---- weld-gen ----
  (function(){
  var dynamicImport = null;   // DSL import line not carried into the standalone app; gen.load() degrades gracefully
  var superFetch = (window.weld && window.weld.__superFetch) || null;

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.gen) { window.weld.gen.attach({dynamicImport: dynamicImport, superFetch: superFetch}); return window.weld.gen; }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.gen: Generator introspection, dynamic import, runtime mutation.
  // Provides three capability groups:
  //   1. Self-inspection: read this generator's DSL source, lists, meta
  //   2. Remote loading: fetch / parse / inspect other public generators
  //   3. Runtime mutation: read/write root.* properties
  // Two dependencies must be imported in the DSL panel for full functionality:
  //   dynamicImport = the import of dynamic-import-plugin
  //   superFetch    = the import of super-fetch-plugin
  // The DSL form passes those in via weld.gen.attach; see docs for keys.
  // Without them, only self-inspection works.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  var deps = {
    dynamicImport: null,
    superFetch: null
  };

  function attach(d) {
    if (d && d.dynamicImport) deps.dynamicImport = d.dynamicImport;
    if (d && d.superFetch) deps.superFetch = d.superFetch;
  }

  function _safe(fn, fallback) {
    try { return fn(); } catch (e) { return fallback; }
  }

  // -------- SELF-INSPECTION --------

  function source() {
    return _safe(function() {
      var r = window.root;
      return (r && r.$perchanceCode) || '';
    }, '');
  }

  function meta() {
    return _safe(function() {
      var r = window.root;
      return (r && r.$meta) || null;
    }, null);
  }

  function moduleName() {
    return _safe(function() {
      var r = window.root;
      return (r && r.$moduleName) || window.generatorName || '';
    }, '');
  }

  function children() {
    return _safe(function() {
      var r = window.root;
      return (r && r.$children) || {};
    }, {});
  }

  function lists() {
    var result = {};
    _safe(function() {
      var ch = children();
      if (!ch) return;
      var keys;
      try { keys = Object.keys(ch); } catch (e) { keys = []; }
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
        var k = keys[i];
        if (k.charAt(0) === '$') continue;
        var node = ch[k];
        var info = { name: k, type: typeof node };
        try {
          if (node && typeof node === 'object') {
            if (node.getLength !== undefined) info.length = node.getLength;
            if (node.getChildNames) info.childNames = node.getChildNames;
            if (node.getPropertyNames) info.propertyNames = node.getPropertyNames;
            if (node.getFunctionNames) info.functionNames = node.getFunctionNames;
            if (node.rawText !== undefined) info.rawText = node.rawText;
          }
        } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
        result[k] = info;
      }
    });
    return result;
  }

  // Search items within lists by keyword (case-insensitive substring)
  function search(listName, query) {
    var hits = [];
    var ch = children();
    if (!ch || !query) return hits;
    var q = String(query).toLowerCase();
    var keys = listName ? [listName] : Object.keys(ch);
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
      var k = keys[i];
      if (k.charAt(0) === '$') continue;
      var node = ch[k];
      if (!node || typeof node.getLength !== 'number') continue;
      var len = node.getLength;
      for (var j = 0; j < len; j++) {
        try {
          var item = node[j];
          var s = String(item == null ? '' : (item.rawText || item.toString()));
          if (s.toLowerCase().indexOf(q) !== -1) {
            hits.push({ list: k, index: j, item: s });
          }
        } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }
    return hits;
  }

  // -------- REMOTE LOADING --------

  function load(name) {
    if (!deps.dynamicImport) {
      return Promise.reject(new Error('weld.gen: dynamicImport not attached. Pass it via weld.gen.attach({ dynamicImport}).'));
    }
    return Promise.resolve(deps.dynamicImport(String(name)));
  }

  function exists(name) {
    if (!deps.superFetch) {
      return Promise.reject(new Error('weld.gen: superFetch not attached.'));
    }
    var url = 'https://perchance.org/api/checkIfGeneratorExists?generatorName=' + encodeURIComponent(String(name));
    return Promise.resolve(deps.superFetch(url)).then(function(r) {
      try {
        var data = typeof r === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r) : r;
        return !!(data && (data.exists || data === true));
      } catch (e) { return false; }
    });
  }

  function sourceOf(name) {
    if (!deps.superFetch) {
      return Promise.reject(new Error('weld.gen: superFetch not attached.'));
    }
    var url = 'https://perchance.org/api/downloadGenerator?generatorName=' + encodeURIComponent(String(name)) + '&listsOnly=true';
    return Promise.resolve(deps.superFetch(url)).then(function(r) { return String(r || ''); });
  }

  function inspect(name) {
    var info = {
      name: String(name),
      type: null,
      arity: null,
      source: '',
      lists: {},
      functions: [],
      imports: [],
      loadError: null
    };

    return sourceOf(name).then(function(src) {
      info.source = src;
      // Extract imports from DSL source
      var importRe = /(\w+)\s*=\s*\{\s*import\s*:\s*([^}]+)\}/g;
      var m;
      while ((m = importRe.exec(src)) !== null) {
        info.imports.push(String(m[2]).trim());
      }
      return load(name).catch(function(e) {
        info.loadError = String(e && e.message || e);
        return null;
      });
    }).then(function(result) {
      if (result == null) return info;
      info.type = typeof result;
      if (typeof result === 'function') {
        info.arity = result.length;
      } else if (typeof result === 'object') {
        var keys;
        try { keys = Object.keys(result); } catch (e) { keys = []; }
        for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
          var k = keys[i];
          if (k.charAt(0) === '$') continue;
          var node = result[k];
          if (node && typeof node === 'object' && node.getLength !== undefined) {
            info.lists[k] = { length: node.getLength };
          } else if (typeof node === 'function') {
            info.functions.push(k);
          }
        }
      }
      return info;
    });
  }

  // -------- RUNTIME MUTATION --------

  function setProp(name, value) {
    _safe(function() {
      if (window.root) window.root[name] = value;
    });
    return value;
  }

  function getProp(name) {
    return _safe(function() {
      return window.root ? window.root[name] : undefined;
    });
  }

  function delProp(name) {
    return _safe(function() {
      if (window.root && (name in window.root)) {
        delete window.root[name];
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    }, false);
  }

  function hasProp(name) {
    return _safe(function() {
      return !!(window.root && (name in window.root));
    }, false);
  }

  window.weld.gen = {
    attach: attach,
    source: source,
    meta: meta,
    moduleName: moduleName,
    children: children,
    lists: lists,
    search: search,
    load: load,
    exists: exists,
    sourceOf: sourceOf,
    inspect: inspect,
    set: setProp,
    get: getProp,
    del: delProp,
    has: hasProp,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  window.weld.gen.attach({dynamicImport: dynamicImport, superFetch: superFetch});

  return window.weld.gen;


  })();

  // ---- weld-director ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.director) return window.weld.director;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.director: the conductor every serious chat app hand-rolls. A turn
  // is rarely one call; it is "write the reply (fast, streamed), then in
  // the background reconcile state, extract memory facts, and illustrate
  // the scene." Done naively the background work blocks the reply, or a
  // failing illustrate pass takes down the whole turn.
  //
  // weld.director formalizes it:
  //   var dir = weld.director.create();
  //   dir.define('reply',      replyFn);                       // foreground
  //   dir.define('audit',      auditFn,      { background:true, after:['reply'] });
  //   dir.define('illustrate', illustrateFn, { background:true, after:['reply'] });
  //   var run = dir.run(input);
  //   var ctx = await run.foreground;   // resolves when reply is done
  //   // ... render ctx.reply immediately ...
  //   await run.background;             // optional: when audit+illustrate finish
  //
  // Each pass fn receives (ctx, input); ctx carries prior passes' results
  // by name (ctx.reply, ctx.audit, ...) plus ctx.errors. Passes run in
  // dependency order, in parallel where independent. A thrown/rejected
  // pass is caught, recorded in ctx.errors[name], and reported via onError;
  // dependents that needed it are skipped, everything else proceeds.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function create(createOpts) {
    createOpts = createOpts || {};
    var passes = {};   // name -> { fn, background, after }
    var order = [];    // insertion order for stable scheduling
    var hooks = { onPass: createOpts.onPass || null, onError: createOpts.onError || null };

    function define(name, fn, opts) {
      opts = opts || {};
      if (typeof fn !== 'function') throw new Error('weld.director: pass "' + name + '" needs a function');
      if (!passes[name]) order.push(name);
      passes[name] = { fn: fn, background: !!opts.background, after: opts.after || [] };
      return api;
    }

    function remove(name) {
      delete passes[name];
      var i = order.indexOf(name); if (i !== -1) order.splice(i, 1);
      return api;
    }

    // Topologically schedule a set of pass-names, then run respecting
    // dependencies and running independents concurrently. Mutates ctx.
    function runGroup(names, ctx, input) {
      var pending = {};
      names.forEach(function (n) { pending[n] = true; });
      var done = {};      // name -> true once settled (ok or skipped/failed)
      var running = {};

      function depsSatisfied(name) {
        var after = passes[name].after || [];
        for (var i = 0; i < after.length; i++) {
          var dep = after[i];
          // only wait on deps that are part of this run at all
          if ((pending[dep] || running[dep]) && !done[dep]) return false;
        }
        return true;
      }

      function depFailed(name) {
        var after = passes[name].after || [];
        for (var i = 0; i < after.length; i++) {
          if (ctx.errors[after[i]]) return after[i];
        }
        return null;
      }

      return new Promise(function (resolve) {
        function tick() {
          var launched = false;
          names.forEach(function (name) {
            if (done[name] || running[name]) return;
            if (!depsSatisfied(name)) return;

            // a required upstream pass failed -> skip this one
            var failedDep = depFailed(name);
            if (failedDep) {
              ctx.errors[name] = 'skipped: dependency "' + failedDep + '" failed';
              done[name] = true; delete pending[name];
              if (hooks.onError) try { hooks.onError(name, ctx.errors[name], ctx); } catch (e) {}
              launched = true; // state changed; re-evaluate
              return;
            }

            running[name] = true; delete pending[name]; launched = true;
            Promise.resolve().then(function () { return passes[name].fn(ctx, input); })
              .then(function (result) {
                ctx[name] = result;
                if (hooks.onPass) try { hooks.onPass(name, result, ctx); } catch (e) {}
              }, function (err) {
                ctx.errors[name] = String((err && err.message) || err);
                if (hooks.onError) try { hooks.onError(name, ctx.errors[name], ctx); } catch (e) {}
              })
              .then(function () {
                running[name] = false; done[name] = true;
                if (allDone()) resolve(ctx); else tick();
              });
          });
          if (allDone()) resolve(ctx);
          else if (!launched && !anyRunning()) {
            // deadlock guard (e.g. a dependency cycle): settle the rest as errors
            names.forEach(function (n) {
              if (!done[n]) { ctx.errors[n] = 'unresolved dependencies (cycle?)'; done[n] = true; }
            });
            resolve(ctx);
          }
        }
        function allDone() { return names.every(function (n) { return done[n]; }); }
        function anyRunning() { return names.some(function (n) { return running[n]; }); }
        if (!names.length) { resolve(ctx); return; }
        tick();
      });
    }

    // run(input, opts) -> { foreground, background, ctx }.
    // foreground resolves with ctx once all non-background passes finish;
    // background resolves once background passes finish (started after fg).
    function run(input, runOpts) {
      runOpts = runOpts || {};
      var ctx = { input: input, errors: {} };
      var fgNames = order.filter(function (n) { return !passes[n].background; });
      var bgNames = order.filter(function (n) { return passes[n].background; });

      var bgResolve;
      var background = new Promise(function (res) { bgResolve = res; });

      var foreground = runGroup(fgNames, ctx, input).then(function () {
        // kick background work without blocking the foreground resolution
        if (bgNames.length) {
          runGroup(bgNames, ctx, input).then(function () { bgResolve(ctx); });
        } else {
          bgResolve(ctx);
        }
        return ctx;
      });

      return { foreground: foreground, background: background, ctx: ctx };
    }

    function onPass(fn) { hooks.onPass = fn; return api; }
    function onError(fn) { hooks.onError = fn; return api; }
    function list() { return order.slice(); }

    var api = {
      define: define,
      remove: remove,
      run: run,
      onPass: onPass,
      onError: onError,
      list: list
    };
    return api;
  }

  window.weld.director = {
    create: create,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.director;

  })();

  // ---- weld-branching ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.branching) return window.weld.branching;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Node id generator
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function uid() {
    return 'n_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8);
  }

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // Tree instance factory
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  function createTree(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var storage = opts.storage;
    var storageKey = opts.storageKey || 'weld-branching';

    // Internal state
    var nodes = {};      // id -> node
    var rootIds = [];    // ordered list of root node ids
    var activeId = null; // currently active leaf

    function save() {
      if (!storage) return;
      try {
        storage.setItem(storageKey, JSON.stringify({
          nodes: nodes,
          rootIds: rootIds,
          activeId: activeId
        }));
      } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
    }

    function load() {
      if (!storage) return false;
      try {
        var raw = storage.getItem(storageKey);
        if (!raw) return false;
        var parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
        if (parsed && typeof parsed === 'object') {
          nodes = parsed.nodes || {};
          rootIds = parsed.rootIds || [];
          activeId = parsed.activeId || null;
          return true;
        }
      } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      return false;
    }

    // Try loading initial state
    load();

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Core: append a node
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function append(data, parentId) {
      if (data === undefined) data = null;
      if (parentId === undefined) {
        // Default parent: the currently active leaf, if any
        parentId = activeId;
      }
      var id = uid();
      var node = {
        id: id,
        parentId: parentId || null,
        childIds: [],
        data: data,
        createdAt: Date.now()
      };
      nodes[id] = node;

      if (parentId && nodes[parentId]) {
        nodes[parentId].childIds.push(id);
      } else {
        // New root
        rootIds.push(id);
      }
      activeId = id;
      save();
      return id;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Branch: explicit alias for append with parent
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function branch(fromId, data) {
      if (!nodes[fromId]) throw new Error('branching: unknown node ' + fromId);
      var parentId = nodes[fromId].parentId;
      var id = append(data, parentId);
      return id;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Get / list
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function get(id) {
      var n = nodes[id];
      if (!n) return null;
      return {
        id: n.id,
        parentId: n.parentId,
        childIds: n.childIds.slice(),
        data: n.data,
        createdAt: n.createdAt
      };
    }

    function getAll() {
      var out = [];
      for (var id in nodes) out.push(get(id));
      return out;
    }

    function getRoots() {
      return rootIds.map(get);
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Path: from root to a given node (or active leaf)
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function path(toId) {
      var target = toId || activeId;
      if (!target || !nodes[target]) return [];
      var chain = [];
      var cursor = nodes[target];
      while (cursor) {
        chain.unshift(get(cursor.id));
        cursor = cursor.parentId ? nodes[cursor.parentId] : null;
      }
      return chain;
    }

    function activeBranch() {
      return path(activeId);
    }

    function setActive(id) {
      if (!nodes[id]) throw new Error('branching: unknown node ' + id);
      activeId = id;
      save();
      return id;
    }

    function getActiveId() {
      return activeId;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Siblings: nodes with the same parent
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function siblings(id) {
      var n = nodes[id];
      if (!n) return [];
      var parentChildren;
      if (n.parentId && nodes[n.parentId]) {
        parentChildren = nodes[n.parentId].childIds;
      } else {
        parentChildren = rootIds;
      }
      return parentChildren.map(get);
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Switching to a sibling: pick by index relative to current
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function switchSibling(id, direction) {
      var sibs = siblings(id);
      if (sibs.length === 0) return null;
      var idx = sibs.findIndex(function(s) { return s.id === id; });
      if (idx === -1) return null;
      var newIdx;
      if (direction === 'next' || direction === 1) {
        newIdx = (idx + 1) % sibs.length;
      } else if (direction === 'prev' || direction === -1) {
        newIdx = (idx - 1 + sibs.length) % sibs.length;
      } else if (typeof direction === 'number') {
        newIdx = Math.max(0, Math.min(sibs.length - 1, direction));
      } else {
        return null;
      }
      return sibs[newIdx].id;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Switch branch by selecting a node; updates active to that node's deepest descendant
    // along its primary (first-child) path
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function switchTo(id) {
      if (!nodes[id]) throw new Error('branching: unknown node ' + id);
      // Walk down following first child until leaf
      var cursor = nodes[id];
      while (cursor.childIds.length > 0) {
        cursor = nodes[cursor.childIds[0]];
      }
      activeId = cursor.id;
      save();
      return activeId;
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Remove a node and all its descendants
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function remove(id) {
      var n = nodes[id];
      if (!n) return false;
      // Collect descendants
      var toRemove = [];
      var stack = [ id];
      while (stack.length) {
        var cur = stack.pop();
        toRemove.push(cur);
        var node = nodes[cur];
        if (node) {
          for (var i = 0; i < node.childIds.length; i++) stack.push(node.childIds[i]);
        }
      }
      // Detach from parent
      if (n.parentId && nodes[n.parentId]) {
        nodes[n.parentId].childIds = nodes[n.parentId].childIds.filter(function(c) { return c !== id; });
      } else {
        rootIds = rootIds.filter(function(r) { return r !== id; });
      }
      // Delete all
      for (var k = 0; k < toRemove.length; k++) delete nodes[toRemove[k]];
      // Reset active if needed
      if (toRemove.indexOf(activeId) !== -1) {
        activeId = (n.parentId && nodes[n.parentId]) ? n.parentId : (rootIds[0] || null);
      }
      save();
      return true;
    }

    function clear() {
      nodes = {};
      rootIds = [];
      activeId = null;
      save();
    }

    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    // Serialize / deserialize
    // -----------------------------------------------------------------
    function serialize() {
      return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify({
        nodes: nodes,
        rootIds: rootIds,
        activeId: activeId
      }));
    }

    function deserialize(state) {
      if (!state || typeof state !== 'object') throw new Error('branching: invalid state');
      nodes = state.nodes ? JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(state.nodes)) : {};
      rootIds = state.rootIds ? state.rootIds.slice() : [];
      activeId = state.activeId || null;
      save();
    }

    function size() {
      var n = 0;
      for (var k in nodes) n++;
      return n;
    }

    function isLeaf(id) {
      var n = nodes[id];
      return n && n.childIds.length === 0;
    }

    return {
      append: append,
      branch: branch,
      get: get,
      getAll: getAll,
      getRoots: getRoots,
      path: path,
      activeBranch: activeBranch,
      setActive: setActive,
      getActiveId: getActiveId,
      siblings: siblings,
      switchSibling: switchSibling,
      switchTo: switchTo,
      remove: remove,
      clear: clear,
      serialize: serialize,
      deserialize: deserialize,
      size: size,
      isLeaf: isLeaf
    };
  }

  window.weld.branching = {
    create: createTree,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.branching;


  })();
  // ---- weld-session ----
  (function(){

  'use strict';

  if (!window.weld) window.weld = {};
  if (window.weld.session) return window.weld.session;

  // -----------------------------------------------------------------
  // weld.session: the timeline an app talks to, instead of five plugins.
  //
  // Frosting's dreamChat models a chat and its generated images as ONE
  // timeline. Weld split that across stream (text), image (pictures),
  // branching (alternates/tree), regen (swipe), and history (persistence) --
  // and left every app (Smart-story included) to weave them by hand. That
  // weave is where the seams and bugs live. weld.session owns the weave.
  //
  //   var s = weld.session.create();
  //   s.addUser('draw me a fox in snow');
  //   await s.addAssistant({ stream: true });        // streams via weld.stream
  //   await s.addImage({ prompt: 'a fox in snow' });  // via weld.image
  //   var turns = s.timeline();                        // what to render
  //   await s.regenerate(turnId);                      // a new sibling take
  //   s.swipe(turnId, +1);                             // move between takes
  //
  // A TURN is { id, role, kind, content, meta, createdAt }:
  //   role: 'user' | 'assistant' | 'system'
  //   kind: 'text' | 'image'
  //   content: the text string, or for images { url, prompt, params }
  // The active path through the branching tree IS the visible conversation;
  // siblings of a node are its alternate takes.
  //
  // Every dependency is SOFT. With weld.branching it gets real per-turn
  // branching; without it, a flat linear list. With weld.stream/image it can
  // generate; without, you add turns manually. With weld.history it persists.
  // -----------------------------------------------------------------

  function createSession(opts) {
    opts = opts || {};
    var listeners = new Array();
    var idSeq = 0;
    function uid() { idSeq++; return 't' + Date.now().toString(36) + '_' + idSeq.toString(36); }

    // ---- the backing store: a branching tree if available, else linear ----
    var tree = null;
    var linear = null;          // fallback: ordered array of turn objects
    var linearActive = null;    // id of the last turn in linear mode
    if (window.weld && window.weld.branching && typeof window.weld.branching.create === 'function') {
      tree = window.weld.branching.create();
    } else {
      linear = new Array();
    }

    function emit(event, data) {
      for (var i = 0; i < listeners.length; i++) {
        try { Reflect.get(listeners, i)(event, data); } catch (e) { /* swallow */ }
      }
    }
    function onChange(fn) {
      if (typeof fn !== 'function') return function () {};
      listeners.push(fn);
      return function () {
        var ix = listeners.indexOf(fn);
        if (ix !== -1) listeners.splice(ix, 1);
      };
    }

    // ---- turn construction --------------------------------------------
    function makeTurn(role, kind, content, meta) {
      return {
        id: uid(),
        role: role,
        kind: kind || 'text',
        content: content,
        meta: meta || null,
        createdAt: Date.now()
      };
    }

    // Append a turn after the current active leaf. Returns the turn.
    function appendTurn(turn) {
      if (tree) {
        var parentId = tree.getActiveId ? tree.getActiveId() : null;
        var nodeId = tree.append(turn, parentId);
        turn.id = nodeId;                 // adopt the tree's id as the turn id
        if (tree.setActive) tree.setActive(nodeId);
      } else {
        linear.push(turn);
        linearActive = turn.id;
      }
      emit('turn', { turn: turn });
      return turn;
    }

    // ---- public: add turns --------------------------------------------
    function addUser(text, meta) {
      return appendTurn(makeTurn('user', 'text', String(text == null ? '' : text), meta));
    }
    function addSystem(text, meta) {
      return appendTurn(makeTurn('system', 'text', String(text == null ? '' : text), meta));
    }

    // addAssistant(textOrOpts): if given a string, appends it directly. If
    // given { stream:true } (and weld.stream is present), streams a reply,
    // emitting 'stream' events as chunks arrive, then finalizes the turn.
    function addAssistant(arg, meta) {
      if (typeof arg === 'string') {
        return Promise.resolve(appendTurn(makeTurn('assistant', 'text', arg, meta)));
      }
      var o = arg || {};
      var turn = makeTurn('assistant', 'text', '', o.meta || meta);
      // place the (empty) turn now so the UI can show a streaming bubble
      appendTurn(turn);

      var stream = window.weld && window.weld.stream;
      if (!o.stream || !stream || typeof stream.generate !== 'function') {
        // no streaming available: if a prompt was given but we can't run it,
        // just return the (possibly empty) turn for the app to fill.
        if (typeof o.text === 'string') { turn.content = o.text; emit('turn', { turn: turn }); }
        return Promise.resolve(turn);
      }

      var prompt = o.prompt != null ? o.prompt : promptFromTimeline();
      return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
        var acc = '';
        stream.generate({
          prompt: prompt,
          onChunk: function (chunk) {
            acc += String(chunk == null ? '' : chunk);
            turn.content = acc;
            emit('stream', { turn: turn, chunk: chunk, content: acc });
          }
        }).then(function (result) {
          // weld.stream returns normalized text; prefer it over our accumulation
          var finalText = (result && (result.text != null)) ? String(result.text) : acc;
          turn.content = finalText;
          if (result && result.stopReason) turn.meta = Object.assign({}, turn.meta, { stopReason: result.stopReason });
          emit('turn', { turn: turn });
          resolve(turn);
        }).catch(function (e) {
          turn.meta = Object.assign({}, turn.meta, { error: String(e && e.message || e) });
          emit('turn', { turn: turn });
          reject(e);
        });
      });
    }

    // addImage(opts): append an image turn. With weld.image present it
    // generates (normalizing params through weld.genparams if available);
    // otherwise it records the request so the app can fulfill it.
    function addImage(arg) {
      var o = arg || {};
      var image = window.weld && window.weld.image;
      var genparams = window.weld && window.weld.genparams;

      var params = o;
      var imgOpts = o;
      if (genparams && typeof genparams.toImageOpts === 'function') {
        params = genparams.create ? genparams.create(o) : o;
        imgOpts = genparams.toImageOpts(o);
      }

      var turn = makeTurn('assistant', 'image', { url: null, prompt: o.prompt || '', params: params }, o.meta);
      appendTurn(turn);

      if (!image || typeof image.generate !== 'function') {
        return Promise.resolve(turn);   // no backend; app fills turn.content.url
      }
      return image.generate(imgOpts).then(function (res) {
        var url = res && (res.url || res.imageURL || res.dataURL || res.src);
        turn.content = { url: url || null, prompt: o.prompt || '', params: params };
        emit('turn', { turn: turn });
        return turn;
      }).catch(function (e) {
        turn.meta = Object.assign({}, turn.meta, { error: String(e && e.message || e) });
        emit('turn', { turn: turn });
        throw e;
      });
    }

    // ---- the visible conversation -------------------------------------
    // timeline(): the active path through the tree (or the linear list),
    // as an ordered array of turns. This is what an app renders.
    function timeline() {
      if (tree) {
        var nodes = tree.activeBranch ? tree.activeBranch() : (tree.path ? tree.path() : new Array());
        return nodes.map(function (n) { return n.data || n; }).filter(Boolean);
      }
      return linear.slice();
    }

    // Build a text prompt from the current timeline (simple role-tagged join).
    // Apps with weld.promptforge can ignore this and pass their own prompt.
    function promptFromTimeline() {
      return timeline().filter(function (t) { return t.kind === 'text'; })
        .map(function (t) { return t.role + ': ' + t.content; })
        .join('\n') + '\nassistant:';
    }

    // ---- alternates: regenerate + swipe -------------------------------
    // regenerate(turnId): create a NEW sibling take of an assistant/image
    // turn (a branch off the same parent), then generate into it. Needs the
    // tree; without branching it appends a fresh turn instead.
    function regenerate(turnId, genOpts) {
      genOpts = genOpts || {};
      var existing = getTurn(turnId);
      if (!existing) return Promise.reject(new Error('weld.session: no such turn ' + turnId));

      if (tree && typeof tree.branch === 'function') {
        var fresh = makeTurn(existing.role, existing.kind, existing.kind === 'image' ? { url: null, prompt: (existing.content && existing.content.prompt) || '', params: existing.content && existing.content.params } : '', existing.meta);
        // branch(fromId, data) creates a sibling carrying our fresh turn as its
        // node data in one step; get() returns a node copy, so setting
        // node.data afterward would not stick. Pass the data up front.
        var newId = tree.branch(turnId, fresh);
        fresh.id = newId;
        if (tree.setActive) tree.setActive(newId);
        emit('turn', { turn: fresh, regenerated: true });
        // generate into it
        if (existing.kind === 'image') return fillImage(fresh, Object.assign({ prompt: fresh.content.prompt, params: fresh.content.params }, genOpts));
        return fillAssistant(fresh, genOpts);
      }
      // no branching: just add a new turn
      if (existing.kind === 'image') return addImage(Object.assign({ prompt: existing.content && existing.content.prompt }, genOpts));
      return addAssistant(Object.assign({ stream: true }, genOpts));
    }

    // helpers that generate into an EXISTING turn (used by regenerate)
    function fillAssistant(turn, o) {
      o = o || {};
      var stream = window.weld && window.weld.stream;
      if (!stream || typeof stream.generate !== 'function') return Promise.resolve(turn);
      var prompt = o.prompt != null ? o.prompt : promptFromTimeline();
      var acc = '';
      return stream.generate({
        prompt: prompt,
        onChunk: function (chunk) { acc += String(chunk == null ? '' : chunk); turn.content = acc; emit('stream', { turn: turn, chunk: chunk, content: acc }); }
      }).then(function (result) {
        turn.content = (result && result.text != null) ? String(result.text) : acc;
        emit('turn', { turn: turn });
        return turn;
      });
    }
    function fillImage(turn, o) {
      o = o || {};
      var image = window.weld && window.weld.image;
      var genparams = window.weld && window.weld.genparams;
      if (!image || typeof image.generate !== 'function') return Promise.resolve(turn);
      var imgOpts = (genparams && genparams.toImageOpts) ? genparams.toImageOpts(o) : o;
      return image.generate(imgOpts).then(function (res) {
        var url = res && (res.url || res.imageURL || res.dataURL || res.src);
        turn.content = { url: url || null, prompt: o.prompt || '', params: o.params || null };
        emit('turn', { turn: turn });
        return turn;
      });
    }

    // swipe(turnId, dir): move between sibling takes of a turn. dir is +1/-1
    // (or 'next'/'prev'). Normalizes the tree's return (id-string OR node) the
    // same way weld.regen does, and CLAMPS at the ends (no wraparound).
    function swipe(turnId, dir) {
      if (!tree || typeof tree.siblings !== 'function') return null;
      var sibs = tree.siblings(turnId) || new Array();
      if (sibs.length <= 1) return getTurn(turnId);
      var ids = sibs.map(function (s) { return (typeof s === 'object') ? s.id : s; });
      var cur = ids.indexOf(turnId);
      if (cur === -1) cur = 0;
      var step = (dir === 'prev' || dir === -1 || dir < 0) ? -1 : 1;
      var next = cur + step;
      if (next < 0) next = 0;                     // clamp, don't wrap
      if (next >= ids.length) next = ids.length - 1;
      var targetId = Reflect.get(ids, next);
      if (tree.setActive) tree.setActive(targetId);
      emit('swipe', { from: turnId, to: targetId, index: next, count: ids.length });
      return getTurn(targetId);
    }

    // sibling info for a turn -> { index, count, ids } for swipe UIs.
    function takes(turnId) {
      if (!tree || typeof tree.siblings !== 'function') return { index: 0, count: 1, ids: Array.of(turnId) };
      var sibs = tree.siblings(turnId) || new Array();
      var ids = sibs.map(function (s) { return (typeof s === 'object') ? s.id : s; });
      if (!ids.length) ids = Array.of(turnId);
      var idx = ids.indexOf(turnId);
      return { index: idx === -1 ? 0 : idx, count: ids.length, ids: ids };
    }

    // branchFrom(turnId): fork the conversation from a turn (make it active,
    // so the next append continues from there). Returns the turn.
    function branchFrom(turnId) {
      if (tree && tree.setActive) tree.setActive(turnId);
      else linearActive = turnId;
      emit('branch', { turnId: turnId });
      return getTurn(turnId);
    }

    // ---- lookup -------------------------------------------------------
    function getTurn(turnId) {
      if (tree && tree.get) {
        var n = tree.get(turnId);
        return n ? (n.data || n) : null;
      }
      for (var i = 0; i < linear.length; i++) { var lt = Reflect.get(linear, i); if (lt.id === turnId) return lt; }
      return null;
    }

    // ---- persistence --------------------------------------------------
    // serialize(): a plain snapshot { turns/tree }. load(snap): restore it.
    // With weld.branching we serialize the tree; otherwise the linear list.
    function serialize() {
      if (tree && tree.serialize) return { mode: 'tree', tree: tree.serialize() };
      return { mode: 'linear', turns: linear.slice(), active: linearActive };
    }
    function load(snap) {
      if (!snap) return false;
      if (snap.mode === 'tree' && tree && tree.deserialize) { tree.deserialize(snap.tree); emit('load', {}); return true; }
      if (snap.mode === 'linear' && linear) { linear = (snap.turns || new Array()).slice(); linearActive = snap.active || null; emit('load', {}); return true; }
      return false;
    }

    function clear() {
      if (tree && tree.clear) tree.clear();
      if (linear) { linear = new Array(); linearActive = null; }
      emit('clear', {});
    }

    return {
      addUser: addUser,
      addSystem: addSystem,
      addAssistant: addAssistant,
      addImage: addImage,
      timeline: timeline,
      regenerate: regenerate,
      swipe: swipe,
      takes: takes,
      branchFrom: branchFrom,
      getTurn: getTurn,
      promptFromTimeline: promptFromTimeline,
      serialize: serialize,
      load: load,
      clear: clear,
      onChange: onChange,
      hasBranching: function () { return !!tree; }
    };
  }

  window.weld.session = {
    create: createSession,
    version: '1.0.0'
  };

  return window.weld.session;

  })();

  (function () {
    function $(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
    // tiny DOM builder: make an element, optionally set class/text and append to a parent
    function el(tag, cls, text, parent) {
      var n = document.createElement(tag);
      if (cls) n.className = cls;
      if (text != null) n.textContent = text;
      if (parent) parent.appendChild(n);
      return n;
    }
    function showModal(id, on) { var m = $(id); if (m) m.style.display = on ? 'flex' : 'none'; }
    function beginRun() { $('go').disabled = true; $('stop').disabled = false; if ($('agg')) $('agg').style.display = 'none'; }
    var SW = (window.weld && window.weld.swarm) || null;
    var CR = (window.weld && window.weld.crew) || null;
    var sb = (window.weld && window.weld.skybridge) || null;
    var APP_BUILD = 'swarm-app/2026-06-05.24';
    // native ai-text is slow and serialized through one broker, so multi-step ReAct runs take
    // minutes, not seconds, so give each dispatched subtask a generous ceiling before timing out.
    var TASK_TIMEOUT = 240000;

    // app-level storage: routes companion -> weld.kv -> weld.persist(IndexedDB) -> memory.
    // weld.persist is inlined, so drafts survive a reload even with no companion.
    function appStore() { return (sb && sb.storage) ? sb.storage : null; }
    // debounced writer so typing doesn't slam the backend db
    function debounce(fn, ms) { var t = null; return function () { var a = arguments, self = this; if (t) clearTimeout(t); t = setTimeout(function () { t = null; fn.apply(self, a); }, ms); }; }
    var DRAFT_KEY = 'swarm:draft';
    function draftSnapshot() { return { goal: $('goal').value, tasks: $('tasks').value, workers: $('workers').value, conc: $('conc').value, decomp: $('decomp').value, theme: themePref, audit: auditOn(), image: { resolution: imgCfg.resolution, style: imgCfg.style, guidance: imgCfg.guidance, suffix: imgCfg.suffix, seed: imgCfg.seed, evolve: imgCfg.evolve } }; }
    var saveDraft = debounce(function () { var st = appStore(); if (!st) return; try { st.set(DRAFT_KEY, draftSnapshot()); } catch (e) {} }, 600);
    async function restoreDraft() {
      var st = appStore(); if (!st) return false;
      try {
        var d = await st.get(DRAFT_KEY); if (!d) return false;
        if (d.goal != null) $('goal').value = d.goal;
        if (d.tasks != null) $('tasks').value = d.tasks;
        if (d.workers != null) { $('workers').value = d.workers; $('workers-v').textContent = d.workers; }
        if (d.conc != null) { $('conc').value = d.conc; $('conc-v').textContent = d.conc; }
        if (d.decomp != null) { $('decomp').value = d.decomp; }
        if (d.audit && $('audit')) { $('audit').checked = true; }
        if (d.image) { Object.assign(imgCfg, d.image); applyImgCfgUI(); }
        if (d.theme) applyTheme(d.theme);
        syncTaskN();
        return true;
      } catch (e) { return false; }
    }

    // ---------- export results ----------
    function downloadFile(name, text, mime) {
      try {
        var blob = new Blob([ text ], { type: mime || 'text/plain' });
        var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        var a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = url; a.download = name;
        document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();
        setTimeout(function () { try { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); a.remove(); } catch (e) {} }, 1500);
        feed('info', 'exported ' + name); toast('success', 'exported ' + name);
      } catch (e) { feed('error', 'export failed: ' + (e && e.message || e)); toast('error', 'export failed'); }
    }
    function exportData() {
      var subs = readTasks(); var cards = [];
      for (var i = 0; ; i++) { var c = $('card-' + i); if (!c) break;
        var ans = c.querySelector('.ans'); var img = c.querySelector('.cardimg img'); var who = $('who-' + i);
        cards.push({ agent: i + 1, subtask: subs[i] || '', worker: who ? who.textContent : '', answer: ans ? (ans.dataset.md != null ? ans.dataset.md : ans.textContent) : '', image: img ? img.src : null });
      }
      return { type: 'swarm-snapshot', version: 1,
        objective: $('goal').value.trim(), generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        model: caps.ai ? 'your model (companion)' : (caps.stream ? 'perchance native' : 'scripted'),
        settings: { workers: $('workers').value, conc: $('conc').value, decomp: $('decomp').value, tools: currentTools(), image: { resolution: imgCfg.resolution, style: imgCfg.style, guidance: imgCfg.guidance, suffix: imgCfg.suffix, seed: imgCfg.seed, evolve: imgCfg.evolve } },
        inputs: { goal: $('goal').value, tasks: $('tasks').value },   // raw strings, restored verbatim on import
        subtasks: subs, agents: cards, synthesis: $('agg-body') ? ($('agg-body').dataset.md != null ? $('agg-body').dataset.md : $('agg-body').textContent) : '' };
    }
    function toMarkdown(d) {
      var L = ['# Page run'];
      if (d.objective) L.push('\n**Objective:** ' + d.objective);
      L.push('\n_' + d.generatedAt + ' \u00b7 model: ' + d.model + '_\n');
      L.push('## Agent results\n');
      d.agents.forEach(function (a) {
        L.push('### Agent ' + a.agent + (a.worker ? ' \u2014 ' + a.worker : ''));
        if (a.subtask) L.push('*' + a.subtask + '*\n');
        L.push((a.answer || '(no answer)') + '\n');
        if (a.image) L.push('!' + '[generated image](' + a.image + ')\n');
      });
      if (d.synthesis) { L.push('## Synthesis\n', d.synthesis + '\n'); }
      return L.join('\n');
    }
    function exportMd() { downloadFile('page-run-' + Date.now() + '.md', toMarkdown(exportData()), 'text/markdown'); }
    function exportJson() { downloadFile('page-run-' + Date.now() + '.json', JSON.stringify(exportData(), null, 2), 'application/json'); }
    // restore settings + input strings from an exported snapshot. results in the file are not
    // re-rendered (read the .md for those); this loads the *setup* so a run can be reproduced.
    function importData(obj) {
      if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') throw new Error('not a snapshot object');
      var inp = obj.inputs || {};
      if (typeof inp.goal === 'string') $('goal').value = inp.goal;
      else if (typeof obj.objective === 'string') $('goal').value = obj.objective;
      if (typeof inp.tasks === 'string') $('tasks').value = inp.tasks;
      else if (Array.isArray(obj.subtasks)) $('tasks').value = obj.subtasks.join('\n');
      var st = obj.settings || {};
      if (st.workers != null) { $('workers').value = st.workers; $('workers-v').textContent = $('workers').value; }
      if (st.conc != null) { $('conc').value = st.conc; $('conc-v').textContent = $('conc').value; }
      if (st.decomp != null) $('decomp').value = st.decomp;
      if (st.tools) Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.tg'), function (b) {
        var k = b.getAttribute('data-tool'); if (st.tools.hasOwnProperty(k)) b.classList.toggle('on', !!st.tools[k]);
      });
      if (st.image) { Object.assign(imgCfg, st.image); applyImgCfgUI(); }
      syncTaskN(); saveDraft();
      feed('info', 'imported settings + inputs' + (obj.agents && obj.agents.length ? ' (results are in the .md, not re-rendered)' : '')); toast('success', 'imported settings + inputs');
    }
    function importFile(file) {
      if (!file) return;
      var r = new FileReader();
      r.onload = function () { try { importData(JSON.parse(String(r.result))); } catch (e) { feed('error', 'import failed: ' + ((e && e.message) || e)); toast('error', 'import failed'); } };
      r.onerror = function () { feed('error', 'import: could not read file'); };
      r.readAsText(file);
    }

    // ---------- share link (weld.backup: versioned envelope; serverless gzip+base64 #fragment) ----------
    function b64urlFromBytes(u8) { var s = ''; for (var i = 0; i < u8.length; i++) s += String.fromCharCode(u8[i]); return btoa(s).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=+$/, ''); }
    function bytesFromB64url(b) { b = String(b).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/'); var s = atob(b); var u = new Uint8Array(s.length); for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) u[i] = s.charCodeAt(i); return u; }
    function b64urlFromStr(s) { return btoa(unescape(encodeURIComponent(s))).replace(/\+/g, '-').replace(/\//g, '_').replace(/=+$/, ''); }
    function strFromB64url(b) { b = String(b).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/'); return decodeURIComponent(escape(atob(b))); }
    function backupEnvelope(payload) { try { var B = window.weld && window.weld.backup; if (B && B.exportData) return B.exportData({ data: payload, version: 1, metadata: { app: 'swarm' } }); } catch (e) {} return { signature: 'plain', data: payload }; }
    async function unwrapEnvelope(env) {
      try { var B = window.weld && window.weld.backup; if (B && B.importData && env && env.signature === 'weld-backup') { var r = await B.importData(env); return r && r.data; } } catch (e) {}
      return (env && env.data) || env;
    }
    async function encodeShare(payload) {
      var json = JSON.stringify(backupEnvelope(payload));
      try { if (typeof CompressionStream !== 'undefined') { var cs = new Blob([ json ]).stream().pipeThrough(new CompressionStream('gzip')); var buf = await new Response(cs).arrayBuffer(); return 'g' + b64urlFromBytes(new Uint8Array(buf)); } } catch (e) {}
      return 'j' + b64urlFromStr(json);
    }
    async function decodeShare(tok) {
      var flag = String(tok).charAt(0), body = String(tok).slice(1);
      if (flag === 'g') { try { var ds = new Blob([bytesFromB64url(body)]).stream().pipeThrough(new DecompressionStream('gzip')); var txt = await new Response(ds).text(); return JSON.parse(txt); } catch (e) {} }
      if (flag === 'j') return JSON.parse(strFromB64url(body));
      return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(tok));   // legacy plain
    }
    async function shareLink() {
      try {
        var tok = await encodeShare(exportData());
        var url = location.origin + location.pathname + '#swarm=' + tok;
        try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText(url); } catch (e) {}
        window.__lastShareLink = url;   // harness hook
        toast('success', 'share link copied'); feed('info', 'share link copied (' + url.length + ' chars)');
      } catch (e) { toast('error', 'could not build share link'); }
    }
    async function maybeImportFromHash() {
      var h = location.hash || ''; var m = h.match(/#swarm=(.+)$/); if (!m) return;
      try {
        var env = await decodeShare(m[1]);
        var data = await unwrapEnvelope(env);
        if (data) { importData(data); toast('info', 'loaded shared setup'); }
        try { history.replaceState(null, '', location.pathname + location.search); } catch (e) {}   // strip the hash after consuming
      } catch (e) { feed('error', 'shared link could not be read'); }
    }

    // ---------- data-handling panel (weld.privacy) ----------
    function registerPrivacy() {
      try {
        var P = window.weld && window.weld.privacy; if (!P || !P.register) return;
        P.register('AI text generation', ['third-party']);     // Perchance native model; leaves device
        P.register('Image generation', ['third-party']);        // Perchance text-to-image; leaves device
        P.register('Local storage (drafts & history)', ['local-only']);
        P.register('Swarm bus & presence', ['local-only']);     // cross-tab / peer, no server
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    var PRIV_BACKENDS = ['AI text generation', 'Image generation', 'Local storage (drafts & history)', 'Swarm bus & presence'];
    function openDataModal() {
      var P = window.weld && window.weld.privacy;
      var body = $('priv-body'); if (!body) return; body.innerHTML = '';
      PRIV_BACKENDS.forEach(function (name) {
        var claims = []; try { claims = (P && P.claimsFor) ? P.claimsFor(name) : []; } catch (e) {}
        var leaves = claims.some(function (c) { return c.leavesDevice; });
        var row = el('div', 'priv-row', null, body);
        el('div', 'priv-name', null, row).innerHTML = '<span class="priv-dot ' + (leaves ? 'out' : 'local') + '"></span>' + name + ' <span class="priv-tag">' + (leaves ? 'leaves device' : 'on device') + '</span>';
        el('div', 'priv-detail', claims.length ? claims.map(function (c) { return c.title + ' \u2014 ' + c.detail; }).join(' ') : 'No privacy claim declared.', row);
      });
      showModal('priv-modal', true);
    }
    function closeDataModal() { showModal('priv-modal', false); }

    // which reasoner a worker will actually use (the single most useful diagnostic)
    function reasonerChoice() {
      if (caps.ai) return 'companion (your model)';
      if (caps.stream) return 'perchance native [' + (streamWrap() ? 'weld.stream' : 'builtin ai-text-plugin') + ']';
      return 'SCRIPTED ECHO -- no AI detected (see [root.*]/[window.weld.*] below)';
    }
    // structured, copy-pasteable diagnostics: typeof probes only, never calls a plugin
    function diagnostics() {
      var r = rootObj();
      function ty(v) { return typeof v; }
      function rootHas(k) { return r ? (typeof r[k] === 'function' ? 'function \u2713' : (k in r ? ty(r[k]) : 'MISSING')) : 'no root'; }
      function weldHas(k) { var w = window.weld && window.weld[k]; return w ? ('present' + (w.version ? ' v' + w.version : '')) : 'MISSING'; }
      var L = [];
      L.push('=== Page // DIAGNOSTICS ===');
      L.push('time:      ' + new Date().toISOString());
      L.push('app build: ' + APP_BUILD);
      L.push('mode:      ' + mode + '    role: ' + (roleSwarm ? roleSwarm.role : '-') + '    transport: ' + caps.transport);
      L.push('');
      L.push('-> reasoner that will run on this tab: ' + reasonerChoice());
      L.push('');
      L.push('--- root.* imports  (from the generator DSL import lines) ---');
      ['aiTextPlugin', 'textToImagePlugin', 'weldSkybridge', 'weldSync', 'weldFetch', 'weldStream', 'weldImage', 'weldCrew', 'weldSwarm'].forEach(function (k) { L.push('  root.' + k + ': ' + rootHas(k)); });
      L.push('');
      L.push('--- window.weld.*  (built by the inlined plugin code) ---');
      ['skybridge', 'sync', 'fetch', 'stream', 'image', 'crew', 'swarm', 'markdown', 'dice', 'toast', 'confetti', 'clean', 'reactions', 'voice', 'rules', 'tokens', 'structured', 'summarize', 'promptforge', 'genparams', 'quota', 'backup', 'privacy', 'persona', 'gen', 'director', 'branching', 'session'].forEach(function (k) { L.push('  weld.' + k + ': ' + weldHas(k)); });
      if (window.weld && window.weld.stream) L.push('    weld.stream.run: ' + ty(window.weld.stream.run));
      if (window.weld && window.weld.image) L.push('    weld.image.generate: ' + ty(window.weld.image.generate));
      L.push('');
      L.push('--- capabilities ---');
      L.push('  caps.ai     (your model via companion): ' + caps.ai);
      L.push('  caps.stream (native AI text): ' + caps.stream + '   source: ' + (streamWrap() ? 'weld.stream' : (builtinAI() ? 'builtin root.aiTextPlugin' : 'NONE')));
      L.push('  caps.image  (native text-to-image): ' + caps.image + '   source: ' + (imageWrap() ? 'weld.image' : (builtinT2I() ? 'builtin root.textToImagePlugin' : 'NONE')));
      L.push('  caps.bus: ' + caps.bus + '   caps.fetch: ' + caps.fetch + '   caps.store: ' + caps.store);
      L.push('');
      L.push('--- skybridge ---');
      if (sb) { L.push('  connected: ' + !!sb.connected); ['ai', 'bus', 'fetch', 'storage'].forEach(function (c) { L.push('  has(' + c + '): ' + (sb.has ? sb.has(c) : '?')); }); }
      else L.push('  skybridge: MISSING');
      L.push('');
      L.push('--- presence ---');
      if (roleSwarm && roleSwarm.peers) { var ps = roleSwarm.peers(); L.push('  self: ' + roleSwarm.id + ' [' + roleSwarm.role + ']'); L.push('  peers: ' + ps.length); ps.forEach(function (p) { L.push('    - ' + p.peerId + ' [' + p.role + ']'); }); }
      else L.push('  no role swarm yet (Local mode, or not started)');
      if (quotaLine) { L.push('--- storage ---'); L.push('  ' + quotaLine); }
      L.push('=== END ===');
      return L.join('\n');
    }
    // weld.quota: refresh a formatted storage-usage line (async) for diagnostics + a one-time near-full warning
    var quotaLine = '';
    function refreshQuota(warn) {
      try {
        var Q = window.weld && window.weld.quota;
        if (!Q || !Q.estimate) return;
        Q.estimate().then(function (e) {
          if (!e || !e.supported) { quotaLine = 'storage estimate unavailable in this browser'; return; }
          var fmt = (Q.formatBytes ? Q.formatBytes : function (n) { return n + ' B'; });
          var pct = Math.round(e.percentUsed || 0);
          quotaLine = 'used ' + fmt(e.used) + ' / ' + fmt(e.total) + ' (' + pct + '%)';
          if (warn && pct > 85) toast('warn', 'local storage almost full (' + pct + '%)');
        }, function () {});
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    function copyDiagnostics() {
      var report = diagnostics();
      try { console.log(report); } catch (e) {}
      try { if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) navigator.clipboard.writeText(report).then(function () { feed('info', 'diagnostics copied to clipboard (also in console)'); }, function () { feed('info', 'diagnostics printed to console (clipboard blocked)'); }); else feed('info', 'diagnostics printed to console'); } catch (e) { feed('info', 'diagnostics printed to console'); }
    }

    // ---------- capability probe ----------
    var caps = { ai:false, stream:false, image:false, fetch:false, bus:false, store:false, transport:'memory' };
    function setPill(id, on, text, cls) { var p = $(id); p.textContent = text; p.className = 'pill ' + (cls || '') + (on ? ' on' : ''); }
    function rootObj() { try { if (typeof root !== 'undefined' && root) return root; } catch (e) {} return (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.root) ? window.root : null; }
    function builtinAI() { var r = rootObj(); return (r && typeof r.aiTextPlugin === 'function') ? r.aiTextPlugin : null; }
    function builtinT2I() { var r = rootObj(); return (r && typeof r.textToImagePlugin === 'function') ? r.textToImagePlugin : null; }
    function streamWrap() { return (window.weld && window.weld.stream && typeof window.weld.stream.run === 'function') ? window.weld.stream : null; }
    function imageWrap() { return (window.weld && window.weld.image && typeof window.weld.image.generate === 'function') ? window.weld.image : null; }
    async function probe() {
      var connected = sb && sb.connected;
      caps.bus = !!(connected && sb.has && sb.has('bus'));
      caps.fetch = !!((connected && sb.has && sb.has('fetch')) || (window.weld && window.weld.fetch));
      caps.store = !!(sb && sb.storage);
      caps.stream = !!(streamWrap() || builtinAI());   // Perchance native AI text (wrapper or built-in)
      caps.image = !!(imageWrap() || builtinT2I());     // Perchance native image (wrapper or built-in)
      caps.transport = caps.bus ? 'bus' : ((window.weld && window.weld.sync) ? 'sync' : 'memory');
      if (connected && sb.has && sb.has('ai') && typeof sb.ai === 'function') {
        try { var r = await sb.ai('ok', { system: 'Reply with the single word ok.' }); caps.ai = !!(r && r.ok); } catch (e) { caps.ai = false; }
      }
      // model source: your own model (companion) > Perchance native > scripted echo
      var modelText = caps.ai ? 'model: yours' : (caps.stream ? 'model: perchance' : 'model: scripted');
      setPill('cap-ai', caps.ai || caps.stream, modelText, (caps.ai || caps.stream) ? '' : 'warn');
      setPill('cap-bus', caps.bus, caps.bus ? 'bus: live' : 'bus: off', 'bus');
      setPill('cap-fetch', caps.fetch, caps.fetch ? 'web: on' : 'web: off');
      setPill('cap-store', caps.store, caps.store ? ('store: ' + (sb.storage.backend ? sb.storage.backend() : 'on')) : 'store: off');
      setPill('cap-transport', caps.transport !== 'memory', 'transport: ' + caps.transport, caps.bus ? 'bus on' : '');
    }

    // ---------- activity feed ----------
    var t0 = 0;
    function feed(kind, text) {
      var l = document.createElement('span'); l.className = 'l';
      var ts = document.createElement('span'); ts.className = 'ts'; ts.textContent = t0 ? ('+' + (Date.now() - t0) + 'ms ') : '';
      var k = document.createElement('span'); k.className = 'k-' + kind; k.textContent = kind.toUpperCase() + ' ';
      var b = document.createElement('span'); b.textContent = text;
      l.appendChild(ts); l.appendChild(k); l.appendChild(b);
      $('feed').appendChild(l); $('feed').scrollTop = $('feed').scrollHeight;
    }
    // ephemeral notifications (weld.toast); complements the persistent feed log
    function toast(kind, msg) { try { var T = window.weld && window.weld.toast; if (T && typeof T[kind] === 'function') T[kind](msg, { duration: 3200 }); } catch (e) {} }
    // celebrate a fully-successful run (weld.confetti)
    function celebrate() { try { if (window.weld && window.weld.confetti) window.weld.confetti.burst({ count: 90 }); } catch (e) {} }

    // ---------- worker cards ----------
    function clearCards() { $('cards').innerHTML = ''; }
    function emptyCards() { $('cards').innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No mission deployed. Set an objective and press <b>DEPLOY</b>.</div>'; }
    function makeCard(idx, goal) {
      var c = el('div', 'card', null, $('cards')); c.style.animationDelay = (idx * 60) + 'ms'; c.id = 'card-' + idx;
      var ch = el('div', 'ch', null, c);
      el('span', 'dot queued', null, ch).id = 'dot-' + idx;
      el('span', 'idx', 'AGENT ' + (idx + 1), ch);
      el('span', 'who', 'queued', ch).id = 'who-' + idx;
      el('span', 'phase', '', ch).id = 'phase-' + idx;
      el('div', 'goal', goal, c);
      el('div', 'trace', null, c).id = 'trace-' + idx;
    }
    function cardStatus(idx, status, who) {
      var dot = $('dot-' + idx); if (dot) dot.className = 'dot ' + status;
      var w = $('who-' + idx); if (w && who != null) w.textContent = who;
    }
    function traceLine(idx, cls, label, text) {
      var tr = $('trace-' + idx); if (!tr) return;
      var l = el('span', 'tl ' + cls, null, tr);
      el('span', 'lbl', label, l);
      el('span', null, ' ' + text, l);
      tr.scrollTop = tr.scrollHeight;
    }
    function mdRender(s) {
      try { if (window.weld && window.weld.markdown && window.weld.markdown.render) return window.weld.markdown.render(String(s || '')); } catch (e) {}
      return el('div', null, String(s || '')).innerHTML;   // escaped fallback
    }
    // accurate token count via weld.tokens when its tokenizer has loaded; ~chars/4 estimate otherwise
    function tokenCount(s) {
      try { var T = window.weld && window.weld.tokens; if (T) { var c = T.countSync ? T.countSync(String(s || '')) : null; if (typeof c === 'number') return c; if (T.estimate) return T.estimate(String(s || '')); } } catch (e) {}
      return Math.ceil(String(s || '').length / 4);
    }
    var SYNTH_BUDGET = 6000;   // approx ideal input budget for the native synthesis model
