    // scrub model scaffolding that the native model leaks into finals/synthesis (weld.clean):
    // dangling sentences, role/title bleed, repetition, plus rules for the specific artifacts seen
    // ("Remember - ONLY JSON", "Final ... Profile:" headers, stray leading enumerators / punctuation).
    function cleanText(s) {
      var t = String(s == null ? '' : s);
      try {
        if (window.weld && window.weld.clean) {
          var out = window.weld.clean.clean(t, { roles: true, collapse: true, rules: [
            { find: '^\\s*Remember\\b[^\\n]*?ONLY JSON[^\\n]*\\n+', flags: 'i' },
            { find: 'Remember\\s*[-\\u2013\\u2014]?\\s*ONLY JSON[^\\n.]*\\.?', flags: 'gi' },
            { find: '^\\s*[2-9]\\d*[.)]\\s+', flags: '' },
            { find: '^\\s*[.,;:]+\\s+', flags: '' }
          ] });
          if (out && out.trim()) return out;
        }
      } catch (e) {}
      return t;
    }
    function cardResult(idx, ok, text) {
      var c = $('card-' + idx); if (!c) return;
      var a = document.createElement('div'); a.className = 'ans md' + (ok ? '' : ' err');
      a.dataset.md = String(text == null ? '' : text);                 // keep the raw markdown for export
      if (ok) a.innerHTML = mdRender(text); else a.textContent = text; // render answers; errors stay literal
      c.appendChild(a);
      // per-output action row: copy / re-run / read-aloud / 👍👎
      try { c.appendChild(actionRow('card:' + idx, function () { return a.dataset.md || a.textContent || ''; }, idx)); } catch (e) {}
    }
    function setPhase(idx, text) { var p = $('phase-' + idx); if (p) p.textContent = text || ''; }
    function clearThinking(idx) { var tr = $('trace-' + idx); if (!tr) return; var th = tr.querySelector('.thinking'); if (th) th.parentNode.removeChild(th); }
    function showThinking(idx) {
      var tr = $('trace-' + idx); if (!tr) return; clearThinking(idx);
      var l = document.createElement('span'); l.className = 'tl thinking';
      l.innerHTML = '<span class="lbl">model</span> <span class="live"></span><span class="cur"></span>';
      tr.appendChild(l); tr.scrollTop = tr.scrollHeight;
    }
    function liveToken(idx, chunk) {
      var tr = $('trace-' + idx); if (!tr) return;
      var live = tr.querySelector('.thinking .live'); if (!live) { showThinking(idx); live = tr.querySelector('.thinking .live'); }
      if (live) { live.textContent += chunk; tr.scrollTop = tr.scrollHeight; }
    }
    function cardImage(idx, dataUrl, prompt) {
      var c = $('card-' + idx); if (!c || !dataUrl) return;
      var wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'cardimg';
      var im = document.createElement('img'); im.src = dataUrl; im.alt = prompt || 'generated image'; im.loading = 'lazy';
      wrap.appendChild(im); var cap = document.createElement('div'); cap.className = 'cap'; cap.textContent = prompt || ''; wrap.appendChild(cap);
      var tr = $('trace-' + idx); if (tr && tr.nextSibling) c.insertBefore(wrap, tr.nextSibling); else c.appendChild(wrap);
    }
    function verbose() { return $('verbose').classList.contains('on'); }

    // ===================== Phase 2.5: action row + reactions + voice + rerun + theme + autopilot =====================
    var rx = (window.weld && window.weld.reactions) ? window.weld.reactions.create({}) : null;   // per-output 👍/👎 (session-scoped)
    var lastToolset = null;     // tools captured at run start, so a single card can be re-run with the same config
    var autopilot = null;       // weld.rules engine, recreated per run
    var runT0 = 0;              // run start timestamp, for the elapsed-time rule
    var themePref = 'light';

    function copyClip(t) { try { navigator.clipboard.writeText(String(t == null ? '' : t)); return true; } catch (e) { return false; } }
    function reactText(b) { var rc = b.querySelector('.rc'); return rc; }
    function syncReact(b, id, kind) {
      if (!rx) return;
      var n = rx.count(id, kind); var rc = reactText(b); if (rc) rc.textContent = n ? String(n) : '';
      b.classList.toggle('on', rx.hasReacted(id, kind));
    }
    // build a per-output action row. rerunIdx is the card index (number) for outputs that can be re-run; omit for the synthesis.
    function actionRow(itemId, getText, rerunIdx) {
      var row = el('div', 'act-row');
      function mk(glyph, aria, fn) {
        var b = document.createElement('button'); b.type = 'button'; b.className = 'act-btn';
        b.innerHTML = glyph; b.title = aria; b.setAttribute('aria-label', aria);
        b.onclick = function () { fn.call(b); }; return b;
      }
      var copyB = mk('\u29C9', 'Copy output', function () {
        if (copyClip(getText())) { var self = this; self.classList.add('on'); setTimeout(function () { self.classList.remove('on'); }, 900); }
      });
      row.appendChild(copyB);
      if (typeof rerunIdx === 'number') row.appendChild(mk('\u21BB', 'Re-run this agent', function () { rerunCard(rerunIdx); }));
      var v = window.weld && window.weld.voice;
      if (v && v.supported && v.supported()) {
        row.appendChild(mk('\uD83D\uDD0A', 'Read aloud', function () {
          var self = this;
          if (v.speaking()) { v.stop(); self.classList.remove('on'); }
          else { v.stop(); v.speak(getText(), { onend: function () { self.classList.remove('on'); } }); self.classList.add('on'); }
        }));
      }
      if (rx) {
        ['up', 'down'].forEach(function (kind) {
          var glyph = (kind === 'up' ? '\uD83D\uDC4D' : '\uD83D\uDC4E') + ' <span class="rc"></span>';
          var b = mk(glyph, kind === 'up' ? 'Mark as good' : 'Mark as bad', function () { rx.toggle(itemId, kind); syncReact(this, itemId, kind); });
          syncReact(b, itemId, kind); row.appendChild(b);
        });
      }
      return row;
    }
    // re-run a single agent's subtask in place (the "Retry" verb), reusing the run config captured at deploy time
    async function rerunCard(idx) {
      if ($('go') && $('go').disabled) { feed('info', 're-run unavailable while a run is active'); return; }
      var c = $('card-' + idx); if (!c) return;
      var goalEl = c.querySelector('.goal'); var goal = goalEl ? goalEl.textContent : '';
      if (!goal) return;
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(c.querySelectorAll('.ans, .cardimg, .act-row'), function (n) { n.parentNode.removeChild(n); });
      var tr = $('trace-' + idx); if (tr) tr.innerHTML = '';
      setPhase(idx, ''); stopped = false;
      feed('info', 're-run \u2190 agent ' + (idx + 1));
      await serveOne('agent-' + (idx + 1), { idx: idx, goal: goal, tools: lastToolset || currentTools() });
    }

    function applyTheme(t) {
      var root = document.querySelector('.swarm'); if (!root) return;
      themePref = (t === 'dark') ? 'dark' : 'light';
      if (themePref === 'dark') root.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark'); else root.removeAttribute('data-theme');
      var tb = $('theme'); if (tb) { tb.innerHTML = themePref === 'dark' ? '\u2600' : '\u263D'; tb.setAttribute('aria-pressed', themePref === 'dark' ? 'true' : 'false'); }
    }
    function toggleTheme() { applyTheme(themePref === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark'); saveDraft(); }

    // autopilot: declarative rules that watch a run and intervene (weld.rules). Recreated each run so state resets.
    function makeAutopilot() {
      if (!(window.weld && window.weld.rules)) return null;
      var e = window.weld.rules.create({});
      e.metric('failFrac', function () { var tot = document.querySelectorAll('.card').length; var err = document.querySelectorAll('.dot.error').length; return tot ? err / tot : 0; });
      e.metric('elapsedSec', function () { return runT0 ? (Date.now() - runT0) / 1000 : 0; });
      e.add({ id: 'autostop', when: { metric: 'failFrac', op: '>=', value: 0.6 }, then: { type: 'stop' }, durationSec: 2, cooldownSec: 99999 });
      e.add({ id: 'timewarn', when: { metric: 'elapsedSec', op: '>=', value: 300 }, then: { type: 'timewarn' }, cooldownSec: 99999 });
      e.onAction(function (action) {
        if (action && action.type === 'stop') { if ($('stop') && !$('stop').disabled) { feed('error', 'autopilot: majority of agents failed \u2014 stopping run'); try { toast('warn', 'autopilot stopped the run'); } catch (e2) {} stopAll(); } }
        else if (action && action.type === 'timewarn') { feed('info', 'autopilot: run exceeding 5 min'); }
      });
      return e;
    }

    // unified step renderer, used by Local crews (direct) and Hub mode (streamed from
    // remote nodes). Shows a live "generating" indicator during the model call, the parsed
    // reasoning/tools, plus (with model I/O on) the raw prompt cue and raw completion.
    function renderStep(idx, s, vb) {
      if (!s) return;
      if (s.type === 'prompt') { setPhase(idx, 'thinking'); showThinking(idx); if (vb) traceLine(idx, 't-io', 'sent', 'prompt \u00b7 step ' + (s.step || '?')); return; }
      clearThinking(idx);
      if (s.type === 'raw') { if (vb) traceLine(idx, 't-io', 'model', String(s.reply || '').slice(0, 280)); }
      else if (s.type === 'thought') { setPhase(idx, 'reasoning'); traceLine(idx, 't-think', 'think', s.thought); }
      else if (s.type === 'action') { setPhase(idx, s.tool); traceLine(idx, 't-act', 'act', s.tool + '(' + JSON.stringify(s.args || {}) + ')'); }
      else if (s.type === 'observation') { setPhase(idx, 'observing'); traceLine(idx, 't-obs', 'obs', typeof s.observation === 'string' ? s.observation : JSON.stringify(s.observation).slice(0, 160)); }
      else if (s.type === 'final') { setPhase(idx, 'done'); traceLine(idx, 't-final', 'done', s.answer); }
      else if (s.type === 'error') { setPhase(idx, 'error'); traceLine(idx, 't-final', 'err', s.error); }
    }
    function cardOnStep(idx) { return function (s) { renderStep(idx, s, verbose()); }; }

    // compact a step for streaming over the swarm (trim large fields)
    function compactStep(s) {
      if (s.type === 'raw') return { type: 'raw', reply: String(s.reply || '').slice(0, 300) };
      if (s.type === 'thought') return { type: 'thought', thought: String(s.thought || '').slice(0, 300) };
      if (s.type === 'action') return { type: 'action', tool: s.tool, args: s.args };
      if (s.type === 'observation') return { type: 'observation', observation: typeof s.observation === 'string' ? s.observation.slice(0, 300) : s.observation };
      if (s.type === 'final') return { type: 'final', answer: String(s.answer || '').slice(0, 500) };
      if (s.type === 'error') return { type: 'error', error: String(s.error || '').slice(0, 300) };
      return { type: s.type, step: s.step };
    }

    // ---------- scripted reasoner (last-resort, offline, no AI plugin) ----------
    function scriptedReasoner(workerId, toolset) {
      var step = 0;
      return function (prompt) {
        step++;
        var g = (prompt.match(/GOAL:\s*(.*)/) || [])[1] || 'the task';
        var url = (g.match(/https?:\/\/\S+/) || [])[0];
        if (step === 1) return Promise.resolve(JSON.stringify({ thought: 'Breaking down: ' + g, tool: 'think', args: { note: 'analyzing ' + g } }));
        if (step === 2) {
          if (toolset.web && url) return Promise.resolve(JSON.stringify({ thought: 'I should fetch the source.', tool: 'web.fetch', args: { url: url } }));
          if (toolset.time) return Promise.resolve(JSON.stringify({ thought: 'Noting the time of analysis.', tool: 'time.now', args: {} }));
        }
        return Promise.resolve(JSON.stringify({ thought: 'Synthesizing an answer.', final: workerId + ': ' + g.replace(/^\W+/, '') }));
      };
    }
    // run Perchance native AI text: prefer the weld.stream wrapper, else the built-in ai-text-plugin
    // directly. Streams tokens via onToken. Returns the generated text (or '' on failure).
    function aiTextRun(o) {
      var w = streamWrap();
      // weld.stream delivers normalized chunks via onToken(deltaString); pass it straight through
      if (w) return w.run({ instruction: o.instruction, startWith: o.startWith, onToken: o.onToken }).then(function (r) { return (r && r.text != null) ? String(r.text) : ''; }, function () { return ''; });
      // built-in ai-text-plugin emits raw { textChunk, isFromStartWith } objects instead
      var onChunk = o.onToken ? function (c) { if (c && !c.isFromStartWith && c.textChunk) o.onToken(c.textChunk); } : undefined;
      var fn = builtinAI(); if (!fn) return Promise.resolve('');
      try {
        return Promise.resolve(fn({ instruction: o.instruction, startWith: o.startWith, hideStartWith: true, onChunk: onChunk }))
          .then(function (r) { return String((r && r.generatedText != null) ? r.generatedText : (r != null ? r : '')); }, function () { return ''; });
      } catch (e) { return Promise.resolve(''); }
    }
    // Perchance native reasoner: real generation, no key, with live token streaming
    function streamReasoner(onToken) {
      return function (prompt, system) { return aiTextRun({ instruction: system, startWith: prompt, onToken: onToken }); };
    }
    // text-to-image only generates while its iframe is mounted in a VISIBLE, onscreen element
    // (a display:none / 0x0 / detached wrapper silently never fires). So we mount into a small
    // live render bay pinned to a corner (a direct, visible body child), removed after.
    // image defaults, editable via the gear popup and persisted in the draft
    var imgCfg = { resolution: '768x768', style: '', guidance: '', suffix: '', seed: '', evolve: false };
    function applyImgPrompt(prompt) {
      var p = String(prompt || ''); var w = imageWrap();
      if (imgCfg.style && w && typeof w.withStyle === 'function') p = w.withStyle(p, imgCfg.style);
      if (imgCfg.suffix) p = p + ', ' + imgCfg.suffix;
      return p;
    }
    function imageBay() {
      var bay = document.createElement('div'); bay.className = 't2i-bay';
      var lbl = document.createElement('div'); lbl.className = 'cap'; lbl.textContent = 'rendering\u2026'; bay.appendChild(lbl);
      document.body.appendChild(bay); return bay;
    }
    // build image params, clamping user-set guidance/seed to valid ranges via weld.genparams.
    // resolution stays the app's constrained dropdown value; default guidance is omitted (backend default).
    function imgParams(promptText) {
      var out = { prompt: promptText, resolution: imgCfg.resolution || '768x768' };
      if (imgCfg.guidance !== '' && imgCfg.guidance != null) out.guidanceScale = +imgCfg.guidance;
      if (imgCfg.seed !== '' && imgCfg.seed != null) out.seed = +imgCfg.seed;
      try {
        var G = window.weld && window.weld.genparams;
        if (G && G.validate) {
          var v = G.validate({ prompt: promptText, cfgScale: out.guidanceScale, seed: out.seed });
          if (v && v.params) {
            if (out.guidanceScale != null && v.params.cfgScale != null) out.guidanceScale = v.params.cfgScale;
            if (out.seed != null && v.params.seed != null) out.seed = v.params.seed;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {}
      return out;
    }
    async function generateImage(prompt) {
      var p = applyImgPrompt(prompt).slice(0, 600);
      var pp = imgParams(p);
      var res = pp.resolution || '768x768';
      var g = (pp.guidanceScale != null) ? +pp.guidanceScale : null;
      var seed = (pp.seed != null) ? +pp.seed : null;
      var bay = imageBay();
      try {
        var w = imageWrap();
        if (w) {
          var opts = { prompt: p, resolution: res, into: bay, style: 'width:100%;height:100%;border:0;display:block;' };
          if (g != null) opts.guidanceScale = g; if (seed != null) opts.seed = seed;
          return await w.generate(opts);
        }
        var fn = builtinT2I(); if (!fn) throw new Error('image generation unavailable');
        var data = await new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
          var o = { prompt: p, resolution: res, onFinish: function (d) { resolve(d); } };
          if (g != null) o.guidanceScale = g; if (seed != null) o.seed = seed;
          var html; try { html = String(fn(o)); } catch (e) { reject(e); return; }
          bay.innerHTML = html;   // mount the t2i iframe into the visible bay so it actually fires
          setTimeout(function () { reject(new Error('image generation timeout')); }, 120000);
        });
        return { dataUrl: (data && data.dataUrl) || (data && data.canvas && data.canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.9)) || null, canvas: data && data.canvas, inputs: data && data.inputs };
      } finally { try { bay.remove(); } catch (e) {} }
    }
    // downscale a result's canvas for cheap transport over the swarm (hub renders at card width)
    function shrinkDataUrl(res, max) {
      try {
        var cv = res && res.canvas; if (!cv || !cv.width) return (res && res.dataUrl) || null;
        var scale = Math.min(1, max / Math.max(cv.width, cv.height));
        if (scale >= 1) return res.dataUrl || cv.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.85);
        var c = document.createElement('canvas'); c.width = Math.round(cv.width * scale); c.height = Math.round(cv.height * scale);
        c.getContext('2d').drawImage(cv, 0, 0, c.width, c.height);
        return c.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.82);
      } catch (e) { return (res && res.dataUrl) || null; }
    }
    // pick the reasoner: your own model (companion) > Perchance native (weld.stream) > scripted echo
    function buildCrew(workerId, idx, toolset, onToken, onImg) {
      var reason = caps.ai ? undefined : (caps.stream ? streamReasoner(onToken) : scriptedReasoner(workerId, toolset));
      feed('info', workerId + ' reasoner: ' + reasonerChoice());
      var crew = CR.create({ workspace: 'swarm-' + workerId + '-' + idx, maxSteps: 4, reason: reason });
      // real image tool: generate with weld.image (text-to-image) into a visible bay
      if (caps.image && toolset.image) {        crew.registerTool({ name: 'image.generate', description: 'Generate an image from a detailed text prompt. If the task asks for a picture, illustration, render, portrait, logo, or any visual, you MUST call this tool with a vivid, self-contained prompt -- do NOT describe the image in text or explain how to make it.', args: { prompt: 'string' },
          run: async function (a) {
            try {
              var res = await generateImage(a.prompt);
              if (res && res.dataUrl) { if (onImg) onImg(res, a.prompt); return { ok: true, note: 'image generated for: ' + a.prompt }; }
              return { ok: false, reason: 'no image produced' };
            } catch (e) { return { ok: false, reason: String(e && e.message || e) }; }
          } });
      }
      // offline randomness tools (weld.dice): dice notation + weighted/random pick
      if (toolset.dice && window.weld && window.weld.dice) {
        var D = window.weld.dice;
        crew.registerTool({ name: 'dice.roll', description: 'Roll dice using standard notation (e.g. "2d6+3", "4d6kh3", "1d20"). Use for random numbers, checks, or generating values.', args: { notation: 'string' },
          run: function (a) { try { var r = D.roll(String(a.notation || '1d6')); return { ok: true, total: r.total, rolls: r.rolls, notation: r.notation }; } catch (e) { return { ok: false, reason: String(e && e.message || e) }; } } });
        crew.registerTool({ name: 'random.pick', description: 'Pick one item at random from a list. Use to choose between options.', args: { items: 'array' },
          run: function (a) { try { var arr = Array.isArray(a.items) ? a.items : String(a.items || '').split(',').map(function (s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean); if (!arr.length) return { ok: false, reason: 'no items' }; return { ok: true, choice: D.pick(arr) }; } catch (e) { return { ok: false, reason: String(e && e.message || e) }; } } });
      }
      if (toolset.persona && window.weld && window.weld.persona) {
        crew.registerTool({ name: 'persona.build', description: 'Build a vivid character dossier from trait sliders. Use for character creation. args: traits, an object mapping trait names (warmth, energy, conscientiousness, openness, ...) to 0..1.', args: { traits: 'object' },
          run: function (a) { try { var p = window.weld.persona.dossier(a && a.traits ? a.traits : (a || {})); return { ok: true, archetype: p.archetype, dossier: p.text }; } catch (e) { return { ok: false, reason: String((e && e.message) || e) }; } } });
      }
      if (toolset.gen && window.weld && window.weld.gen) {
        crew.registerTool({ name: 'gen.lists', description: 'List the names of the host generator\'s data lists (if any).', args: {},
          run: function () { try { var L = window.weld.gen.lists(); return { ok: true, lists: Array.isArray(L) ? L : (L ? Object.keys(L) : []) }; } catch (e) { return { ok: false, reason: String((e && e.message) || e) }; } } });
        crew.registerTool({ name: 'gen.search', description: 'Search the host generator\'s lists for items matching a query. args: query, a search string.', args: { query: 'string' },
          run: function (a) { try { var hits = window.weld.gen.search(String((a && a.query) || '')); return { ok: true, hits: Array.isArray(hits) ? hits.slice(0, 20) : [] }; } catch (e) { return { ok: false, reason: String((e && e.message) || e) }; } } });
      }
      return crew;
    }

    // ---------- keep-awake: stop Chrome freezing/discarding a backgrounded Node tab ----------
    // A frozen tab stops sending presence heartbeats (so the hub prunes it -> "only N workers")
    // and stops processing incoming tasks ("nothing happens after an order"). Silent audio marks
    // the tab as "playing media", which exempts it from freezing/discarding; a screen wake lock
    // (re-acquired on focus) helps when visible. Both are started from the serve user-gesture.
    var awake = { on:false, ctx:null, lock:null };
    function acquireLock() {
      try { if (navigator.wakeLock && document.visibilityState === 'visible') navigator.wakeLock.request('screen').then(function (l) { awake.lock = l; }, function () {}); } catch (e) {}
    }
    function onVis() {
      if (document.visibilityState === 'visible') { acquireLock(); if (awake.ctx && awake.ctx.state === 'suspended') { try { awake.ctx.resume(); } catch (e) {} } }
      paintAwake();
    }
    function startKeepAwake() {
      if (!awake.on) {
        try {
          var AC = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
          if (AC) {
            awake.ctx = new AC();
            var osc = awake.ctx.createOscillator(), g = awake.ctx.createGain();
            g.gain.value = 0.0001; osc.frequency.value = 30;     // inaudible but non-zero output
            osc.connect(g); g.connect(awake.ctx.destination); osc.start();
            if (awake.ctx.state === 'suspended') awake.ctx.resume();
          }
        } catch (e) {}
        acquireLock();
        document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', onVis);
        awake.on = true;
      }
      paintAwake();
    }
    function stopKeepAwake() {
      try { if (awake.lock) awake.lock.release(); } catch (e) {} awake.lock = null;
      try { if (awake.ctx) awake.ctx.close(); } catch (e) {} awake.ctx = null;
      document.removeEventListener('visibilitychange', onVis);
      awake.on = false; $('awake').style.display = 'none';
    }
    function paintAwake() {
      var a = $('awake'); if (!awake.on) { a.style.display = 'none'; return; }
      a.style.display = '';
      var audioOk = awake.ctx && awake.ctx.state === 'running';
      a.innerHTML = '<span style="color:var(--green)">&#9679; keep-awake ' + (audioOk ? 'ON' : 'starting') + '</span> &middot; '
        + (document.visibilityState === 'visible' ? 'tab visible' : 'tab hidden &mdash; staying alive via audio')
        + '. Keep this tab open; do not close it.';
    }

    // ---------- a worker's brain: run weld.crew on the task, stream into the card ----------
    // The native model is inconsistent at calling image.generate for image goals; it sometimes
    // gives up or writes a meta-guide about prompting instead. These helpers let us detect an
    // image goal and, if the agent flaked, generate the image directly so the run still delivers.
    function isImageGoal(g) { return /\b(images?|pictures?|pics?|photo(?:graph)?s?|draw(?:ing|ings|n|s)?|render(?:ed|ing|s)?|illustrat\w*|portraits?|paint(?:ing|ings|ed|s)?|wallpapers?|logos?|icons?|artworks?|art|sketch(?:es|ed)?|posters?|selfies?|headshots?)\b/i.test(String(g || '')); }
    function imagePromptFor(g) {
      return String(g || '')
        .replace(/^\s*aspect\s+\d+\s+of:\s*/i, '')                                   // strip auto-split prefix
        .replace(/^\s*(create|generate|make|draw|render|produce)\s+(an?\s+|some\s+)?(images?|pictures?|photos?|art(work)?|illustrations?|drawings?|portraits?)\s+(of\s+)?/i, '')
        .trim() || String(g || '');
    }
    // turn a short brief into a rich, self-contained image prompt (the "describe" phase)
    async function describeImage(brief) {
      var b = imagePromptFor(brief);
      if (!aiAvailable()) return b;
      // optional: evolve candidate prompts and pick the top one (weld.promptforge -> string[])
      if (imgCfg.evolve && window.weld && window.weld.promptforge) {
        try {
          var pf = window.weld.promptforge.create({ instruction: b, mode: 'balanced' });
          var cands = await pf.generate(4);
          if (Array.isArray(cands) && cands.length && String(cands[0]).trim()) return String(cands[0]).trim();
        } catch (e) {}
      }
      try {
        var sys = 'You write a single vivid, self-contained text-to-image prompt. Output ONLY the prompt text: one paragraph, no preamble, no quotes, no markdown, no JSON. Describe the subject, appearance, pose, composition, setting, and lighting concretely.';
        var txt = await genText('Write one detailed image prompt for: ' + b, sys);
        txt = String(txt || '').replace(/^[\s"']+|[\s"']+$/g, '');
        return txt || b;
      } catch (e) { return b; }
    }
    // one image per worker, end to end: describe -> generate -> report. Steps use the standard
    // step types so the card trace (and Hub streaming) render them with no special-casing.
    async function runImagePipeline(workerId, idx, brief, onStep, onImage) {
      onStep({ type: 'action', tool: 'image.describe', args: { brief: imagePromptFor(brief) } });
      var prompt = await describeImage(brief);
      if (stopped) return { worker: workerId, ok: false, reason: 'stopped', idx: idx };
      onStep({ type: 'observation', observation: { prompt: prompt } });
      onStep({ type: 'action', tool: 'image.generate', args: { prompt: prompt } });
      try {
        var res = await generateImage(prompt);
        if (stopped) return { worker: workerId, ok: false, reason: 'stopped', idx: idx };
        if (res && res.dataUrl) {
          onImage(res, prompt);
          onStep({ type: 'observation', observation: 'image ready' });
          onStep({ type: 'final', answer: 'Image generated.' });
          return { worker: workerId, ok: true, answer: 'Image generated.', prompt: prompt, dataUrl: res.dataUrl, idx: idx };
        }
        onStep({ type: 'error', error: 'no image produced' });
        return { worker: workerId, ok: false, reason: 'no image produced', prompt: prompt, idx: idx };
      } catch (e) {
        onStep({ type: 'error', error: String((e && e.message) || e) });
        return { worker: workerId, ok: false, reason: String((e && e.message) || e), prompt: prompt, idx: idx };
      }
    }
    // optional, time-boxed audit pass: review each answer against its subtask and revise (weld.director)
    function auditOn() { return !!($('audit') && $('audit').checked); }
    async function auditAnswer(goal, draft) {
      if (!draft || !aiAvailable() || !(window.weld && window.weld.director)) return draft;
      try {
        var dir = window.weld.director.create();
        dir.define('audit', function (ctx, input) {
          var sys = 'You are a strict reviewer. Given a SUBTASK and a DRAFT answer, return an improved final answer that fixes inaccuracies, removes filler/scaffolding, and directly addresses the subtask. Output ONLY the revised answer -- no preamble, no commentary, no headers.';
          var p = 'SUBTASK: ' + input.goal + '\n\nDRAFT:\n' + input.draft + '\n\nReturn the revised answer only.';
          return genText(p, sys);
        });
        var run = dir.run({ goal: goal, draft: draft });
        var ctx = await Promise.race([run.foreground, new Promise(function (res) { setTimeout(function () { res(null); }, 45000); })]);
        var revised = ctx && ctx.audit;
        return (revised && String(revised).trim()) ? cleanText(String(revised)) : draft;
      } catch (e) { return draft; }
    }
    async function serveOne(workerId, payload) {
      var idx = (payload && typeof payload.idx === 'number') ? payload.idx : 0;
      if (stopped) return { worker: workerId, ok: false, reason: 'stopped', idx: idx };   // don't start new agents after a stop
      var toolset = (payload && payload.tools) || { web:false, time:true };
      cardStatus(idx, 'running', workerId);
      feed('action', workerId + ' \u2190 ' + payload.goal);
      // image goal -> dedicated pipeline (describe -> generate -> report), one image per worker
      if (caps.image && toolset.image && isImageGoal(payload.goal)) {
        feed('info', workerId + ' image pipeline: describe \u2192 generate \u2192 report');
        var rp = await runImagePipeline(workerId, idx, payload.goal, cardOnStep(idx),
          function (res, prompt) { cardImage(idx, res.dataUrl, prompt); });
        cardStatus(idx, rp.ok ? 'done' : 'error', workerId);
        cardResult(idx, rp.ok, rp.ok ? rp.answer : ('ERROR: ' + (rp.reason || 'failed')));
        feed(rp.ok ? 'obs' : 'error', workerId + ' \u2192 ' + (rp.ok ? ('image \u00b7 ' + String(rp.prompt || '').slice(0, 60)) : (rp.reason || 'failed')));
        return { worker: workerId, answer: rp.answer || rp.reason, ok: rp.ok, idx: idx };
      }
      var crew = buildCrew(workerId, idx, toolset,
        function (ch) { liveToken(idx, ch); },                          // live token stream into the card
        function (res, prompt) { cardImage(idx, res.dataUrl, prompt); });// render generated image on the card
      running.push(crew);
      var out = await crew.run(payload.goal, { onStep: cardOnStep(idx) });
      var ok = !!out.ok;
      if (ok) out.answer = cleanText(out.answer);
      if (ok && auditOn()) { setPhase(idx, 'audit'); feed('info', workerId + ' audit pass\u2026'); out.answer = await auditAnswer(payload.goal, out.answer); }
      cardStatus(idx, ok ? 'done' : 'error', workerId);
      cardResult(idx, ok, ok ? out.answer : ('ERROR: ' + (out.reason || out.error || 'failed')));
      feed(ok ? 'obs' : 'error', workerId + ' \u2192 ' + (out.answer || out.reason || 'failed'));
      return { worker: workerId, answer: out.answer, ok: ok, idx: idx };
    }
    function makeServe(workerId) {
      return function (payload) { return serveOne(workerId, payload); };
    }

    // ---------- decomposition strategies ----------
    var DECOMP = [
      { id:'manual', label:'Manual -- type subtasks below' },
      { id:'split',  label:'Auto-split the objective' },
      { id:'ai',     label:'AI decompose (your model or Perchance)' }
    ];
    // unified text generation: your own model (companion) -> Perchance native (weld.stream) -> none
    function aiAvailable() { return caps.ai || caps.stream; }
    async function genText(prompt, system) {
      if (caps.ai) { try { var r = await sb.ai(prompt, { system: system }); if (r && r.ok && r.text) return r.text; } catch (e) {} }
      if (caps.stream) { var t = await aiTextRun({ instruction: system, startWith: prompt }); if (t) return t; }
      return '';
    }
    function autoSplit(goal, n) {
      var parts = goal.split(/[\n.;]+| and | then |,/).map(function (s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(function (s) { return s.length > 2; });
      if (parts.length >= 2) return parts.slice(0, n);
      var out = []; for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) out.push('Aspect ' + (i + 1) + ' of: ' + goal);
      return out;
    }
    // robustly turn any decomposition item into a non-empty task string, never "[object Object]".
    // models sometimes return [{task:"..."}] or [{brief:"..."}] instead of a bare string array.
    function coerceTask(x) {
      if (x == null) return '';
      if (typeof x === 'string') return x.trim();
      if (typeof x === 'number' || typeof x === 'boolean') return String(x);
      if (Array.isArray(x)) return x.map(coerceTask).filter(Boolean).join(' ');
      if (typeof x === 'object') {
        var keys = ['task', 'subtask', 'brief', 'prompt', 'title', 'text', 'name', 'description', 'goal', 'step', 'value', 'content', 'instruction'];
        for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) { var v = x[keys[i]]; if (typeof v === 'string' && v.trim()) return v.trim(); }
        for (var k in x) { if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(x, k) && typeof x[k] === 'string' && x[k].trim()) return x[k].trim(); }
        try { return JSON.stringify(x); } catch (e) { return ''; }
      }
      return String(x);
    }
    // pull a task list out of a model reply that may be a JSON array, a {subtasks:[...]}-style object,
    // or messy text. Returns a non-empty string[] or null. Tolerant of any characters inside the strings.
    function parseTaskList(txt, n) {
      var s = String(txt == null ? '' : txt), best = null;
      function consider(a) { if (Array.isArray(a) && (!best || a.length > best.length)) best = a; }
      // most tolerant: weld.structured strips ``` fences and repairs trailing commas / smart quotes
      try {
        var S = window.weld && window.weld.structured;
        if (S && S.parse) { var r = S.parse(s); var v = r && r.value;
          if (Array.isArray(v)) consider(v);
          else if (v && typeof v === 'object') { ['items', 'subtasks', 'tasks', 'images', 'briefs', 'steps'].forEach(function (k) { if (Array.isArray(v[k])) consider(v[k]); }); } }
      } catch (e0) {}
      // every non-greedy bracketed candidate (handles commentary around the array; keep the longest)
      var re = /\[[\s\S]*?\]/g, m;
      while ((m = re.exec(s))) { try { consider(JSON.parse(m[0])); } catch (e) {} }
      // the greedy span (covers arrays whose string values legitimately contain "]")
      var mg = s.match(/\[[\s\S]*\]/); if (mg) { try { consider(JSON.parse(mg[0])); } catch (e3) {} }
      // a JSON object that wraps a list under a common key
      if (!best) { var mo = s.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/); if (mo) { try { var o = JSON.parse(mo[0]); var w = o.subtasks || o.tasks || o.images || o.briefs || o.items || o.steps; if (Array.isArray(w)) consider(w); } catch (e2) {} } }
      if (Array.isArray(best) && best.length) { var out = best.slice(0, n).map(coerceTask).filter(Boolean); if (out.length) return out; }
      return null;
    }
    async function aiDecompose(goal, n) {
      if (!aiAvailable()) return autoSplit(goal, n);
      try {
        var sys, p;
        if (isImageGoal(goal)) {   // for image goals, ask for distinct image briefs (one per worker)
          sys = 'You plan a set of images. Output strictly a JSON array of ' + n + ' short, distinct image briefs (vary the pose, angle, scene, or mood) for the requested subject. Nothing else.';
          p = 'Give ' + n + ' distinct image briefs for: ' + goal;
        } else {
          sys = 'You decompose objectives into parallelizable subtasks. Output strictly a JSON array of short strings, nothing else.';
          p = 'Break this objective into exactly ' + n + ' concise, independent subtasks. Reply with ONLY a JSON array of strings.\n\nObjective: ' + goal;
        }
        var txt = await genText(p, sys);
        var list = parseTaskList(txt, n);
        if (list) return list;
      } catch (e) {}
      return autoSplit(goal, n);
    }
    async function decompose() {
      var goal = $('goal').value.trim(); if (!goal) return;
      var n = parseInt($('workers').value, 10) || 3;
      var strat = DECOMP[parseInt($('decomp').value, 10)].id;
      if (strat === 'manual') { if (!$('tasks').value.trim()) $('tasks').value = autoSplit(goal, n).join('\n'); }
      else if (strat === 'split') $('tasks').value = autoSplit(goal, n).join('\n');
      else if (strat === 'ai') { feed('info', 'decomposing with ' + (caps.ai ? 'your model' : 'Perchance AI') + '\u2026'); $('tasks').value = (await aiDecompose(goal, n)).join('\n'); }
      syncTaskN();
    }
    function readTasks() { return $('tasks').value.split('\n').map(function (s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(Boolean); }
    function syncTaskN() { $('task-n').textContent = readTasks().length; }

    function currentTools() { var t = {}; Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.tg'), function (b) { t[b.getAttribute('data-tool')] = b.classList.contains('on'); }); return t; }
    function imgToggle() { return Array.prototype.filter.call(document.querySelectorAll('.tg'), function (b) { return b.getAttribute('data-tool') === 'image'; })[0] || null; }
    // when the objective is clearly an image request, turn the image tool on so "make images of X" just works
    function autoEnableImage() {
      if (!isImageGoal($('goal').value)) return;
      var b = imgToggle();
      if (b && !b.classList.contains('on')) { b.classList.add('on'); feed('info', 'image goal detected \u2014 enabled the image tool'); saveDraft(); }
    }
    // ---------- image-defaults popup ----------
    function imgStyleOptions() {
      var sel = $('img-style'); if (!sel) return;
      var names = (window.weld && window.weld.image && typeof window.weld.image.styleNames === 'function') ? window.weld.image.styleNames() : [];
      names.forEach(function (nm) { var o = document.createElement('option'); o.value = nm; o.textContent = nm; sel.appendChild(o); });
    }
    function applyImgCfgUI() {
      if ($('img-res')) $('img-res').value = imgCfg.resolution || '768x768';
      if ($('img-style')) $('img-style').value = imgCfg.style || '';
      if ($('img-g')) { $('img-g').value = (imgCfg.guidance === '' || imgCfg.guidance == null) ? 0 : imgCfg.guidance; $('img-g-v').textContent = (+$('img-g').value) ? $('img-g').value : 'default'; }
      if ($('img-suffix')) $('img-suffix').value = imgCfg.suffix || '';
      if ($('img-seed')) $('img-seed').value = (imgCfg.seed == null) ? '' : String(imgCfg.seed);
      if ($('img-evolve')) $('img-evolve').checked = !!imgCfg.evolve;
    }
    function readImgCfgUI() {
      imgCfg.resolution = $('img-res').value || '768x768';
      imgCfg.style = $('img-style').value || '';
      var g = +$('img-g').value; imgCfg.guidance = g ? g : '';
      imgCfg.suffix = $('img-suffix').value.trim();
      imgCfg.seed = $('img-seed').value.trim();
      imgCfg.evolve = !!($('img-evolve') && $('img-evolve').checked);
    }
    function openImgModal() { applyImgCfgUI(); showModal('img-modal', true); }
    function closeImgModal() { showModal('img-modal', false); }

    // ---------- aggregate / synthesis ----------
    // synthesis with live progress: stream tokens (native path) and run a spinner + elapsed timer
    async function genTextStream(prompt, system, onToken) {
      if (caps.ai) { try { var r = await sb.ai(prompt, { system: system }); if (r && r.ok && r.text) { if (onToken) onToken(r.text); return r.text; } } catch (e) {} }
      if (caps.stream) { var t = await aiTextRun({ instruction: system, startWith: prompt, onToken: onToken }); if (t) return t; }
      return '';
    }
    // when the combined worker answers exceed the synthesis budget, summarize the longest ones first
    // (weld.summarize -> {ok, summary}). Keeps synthesis from stalling/overflowing on huge inputs.
    async function condenseForSynthesis(results) {
      var S = window.weld && window.weld.summarize;
      if (!S || !S.summarize) return results;
      var total = tokenCount(results.map(function (r) { return (r && r.answer) || ''; }).join('\n'));
      if (total <= SYNTH_BUDGET) return results;
      feed('info', 'condensing oversized agent answers before synthesis (weld.summarize)');
      var out = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < results.length; i++) {
        var r = results[i];
        if (r && r.ok && r.answer && tokenCount(r.answer) > 800) {
          try { var s = await S.summarize(String(r.answer), { maxWords: 140 }); if (s && s.ok && s.summary) { out.push({ ok: true, answer: s.summary, worker: r.worker, idx: r.idx }); continue; } } catch (e) {}
        }
        out.push(r);
      }
      return out;
    }
    async function aggregate(results, objective, silent, onStream) {
      if (aiAvailable()) { try { results = await condenseForSynthesis(results); } catch (e) {} }
      var obj = (objective != null) ? objective : $('goal').value.trim();
      var ok = results.filter(function (r) { return r && r.ok; });
      if (!silent) $('agg').style.display = '';
      var joined = results.map(function (r, i) { return (i + 1) + '. ' + (r && r.ok ? r.answer : ('(failed) ' + ((r && (r.reason || r.error)) || ''))); }).join('\n');
      if (!(aiAvailable() && ok.length)) {
        $('agg-syn').textContent = 'collected'; $('agg-tag').textContent = ok.length + '/' + results.length; $('agg-body').textContent = joined;
        return joined;
      }
      $('agg-tag').textContent = caps.ai ? 'your ai' : 'perchance';
      var who = caps.ai ? 'your model' : 'Perchance AI';
      var t0s = Date.now(), streamed = '';
      $('agg').classList.add('working'); $('agg-body').textContent = '';
      function paint(label) { $('agg-syn').innerHTML = '<span class="spin"></span> ' + label; }
      paint('synthesizing with ' + who + '\u2026 0s');
      var promptTokens = tokenCount(joined);
      if (promptTokens > SYNTH_BUDGET) feed('info', 'synthesis input ~' + promptTokens + ' tokens (over budget ' + SYNTH_BUDGET + ') \u2014 will condense');
      var timer = setInterval(function () { paint('synthesizing with ' + who + '\u2026 ' + Math.round((Date.now() - t0s) / 1000) + 's' + (streamed ? ' \u00b7 ' + streamed.length + ' chars' : '')); }, 400);
      try {
        var txt = await genTextStream(
          'Synthesize these worker results into one cohesive answer to the objective "' + obj + '":\n\n' + joined,
          'You merge several agent results into ONE cohesive answer to the objective. Output only the answer itself: no title, no preamble, no header like "Final ... Profile:", do not re-number or restate the inputs, and never restate these instructions. Begin directly with the answer.',
          function (chunk) { streamed += chunk; $('agg-body').textContent = streamed; if (onStream) { try { onStream(streamed); } catch (e) {} } }   // live: text grows as it generates
        );
        clearInterval(timer); $('agg').classList.remove('working');
        var final = cleanText(txt || streamed);
        if (final) { $('agg-syn').textContent = 'synthesized in ' + Math.round((Date.now() - t0s) / 1000) + 's'; $('agg-body').dataset.md = final; $('agg-body').classList.add('md'); $('agg-body').innerHTML = mdRender(final);
          try { var ab = $('agg-body'); var old = ab.parentNode.querySelector('.act-row'); if (old) old.parentNode.removeChild(old); ab.parentNode.appendChild(actionRow('synth', function () { return $('agg-body').dataset.md || $('agg-body').textContent || ''; })); } catch (e) {}
          return final; }
        $('agg-syn').textContent = 'collected (synthesis unavailable)'; $('agg-body').textContent = joined;
        return joined;
      } catch (e) {
        clearInterval(timer); $('agg').classList.remove('working');
        $('agg-syn').textContent = 'collected (synthesis unavailable)'; $('agg-body').textContent = joined;
        return joined;
      }
    }

    // ---------- run lifecycle ----------
    var active = [];      // swarms to tear down
    var running = [];     // crews we can stop()
    var stopped = false;
    var runGen = 0;   // bumped on each run start AND on stop, so a stale in-flight run no-ops its tail
    var meterPoll = null;
    function teardown() { active.forEach(function (c) { try { c.leave(); } catch (e) {} }); active = []; }
    function setReady() { $('go').disabled = false; $('stop').disabled = true; }
    function stopAll() {
      stopped = true; runGen++;                                   // invalidate any in-flight run
      autopilot = null;
      if (meterPoll) { clearInterval(meterPoll); meterPoll = null; }
      running.forEach(function (c) { try { c.stop(); } catch (e) {} });
      try { if (window.weld && window.weld.stream && window.weld.stream.stopAll) window.weld.stream.stopAll(); } catch (e) {} // abort in-flight AI: agents + synthesis
      setReady(); $('meter').textContent = 'stopped'; feed('info', 'stopped by user'); toast('warn', 'run stopped');
    }
    function setMeter() {
      var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.card'); var done = document.querySelectorAll('.dot.done,.dot.error').length;
      $('meter').textContent = cards.length ? (done + ' / ' + cards.length + ' complete') : 'idle';
      if (autopilot) { try { autopilot.tick(0.3); } catch (e) {} }   // drive the rules engine from the run loop
    }

    // in-page shared bus for local mode (delivers to all peers but the sender)
    function sharedBus() {
      var subs = [];
      return function endpoint(id) {
        return { kind:'demo', send:function (m) { setTimeout(function () { subs.forEach(function (s) { if (s.id !== id) { try { s.fn(m); } catch (e) {} } }); }, 0); }, onMessage:function (fn) { subs.push({ id:id, fn:fn }); } };
      };
    }

    // ===== chat mode: each user turn runs a full swarm mission; the synthesis becomes the reply =====
    var chatSession = null;
    var chatBusy = false;
    var ACTIVE_PTR = '__active';
    var chatDB = (window.weld && window.weld.persist) ? window.weld.persist.open('swarm-chat') : null;
    var chatColl = chatDB ? chatDB.collection('sessions') : null;   // named conversations persisted via weld.persist; weld.session is the conversation model
    var chatSessionId = null;
    var chatSessionName = '';
    function genSessionId() { return 's_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6); }
    function ensureSession() {
      if (chatSession) return chatSession;
      chatSession = (window.weld && window.weld.session && window.weld.session.create) ? window.weld.session.create({}) : null;
      return chatSession;
    }
    function turnLine(t) { var who = t.role === 'user' ? 'User' : (t.role === 'assistant' ? 'Assistant' : t.role); return who + ': ' + String(t.content == null ? '' : t.content); }
    // Build conversation context. Under budget -> verbatim. Over budget -> keep the last few turns
    // verbatim and condense the older ones with weld.summarize (falling back to a char cap).
    async function buildContext(turns) {
      if (!turns || !turns.length) return '';
      var text = turns.map(turnLine).join('\n');
      if (tokenCount(text) <= SYNTH_BUDGET) return text;
      var keep = 4;
      if (turns.length > keep && window.weld && window.weld.summarize && window.weld.summarize.summarize) {
        var older = turns.slice(0, turns.length - keep), recent = turns.slice(turns.length - keep);
        try {
          var r = await window.weld.summarize.summarize(older.map(turnLine).join('\n'), { maxWords: 160 });
          if (r && r.ok && r.summary) return 'Summary of earlier conversation: ' + r.summary + '\n\n' + recent.map(turnLine).join('\n');
        } catch (e) {}
      }
      return text.slice(-SYNTH_BUDGET * 4);
    }
    function chatContext(s) {
      var tl = (s && s.timeline) ? s.timeline() : [];
      return buildContext(tl.slice(0, -1));   // exclude the just-added user turn; returns a Promise
    }
    function renderTranscript(thinking) {
      var log = $('chat-log'); if (!log) return;
      var tl = (chatSession && chatSession.timeline) ? chatSession.timeline() : [];
      if (!tl.length && !thinking) { log.innerHTML = '<div class="empty">No messages yet. Say something to start the conversation.</div>'; return; }
      log.innerHTML = '';
      tl.forEach(function (t) {
        var role = (t.role === 'user') ? 'user' : 'assistant';
        var wrap = el('div', 'chat-msg ' + role, null, log);
        el('div', 'chat-who', role === 'user' ? 'you' : 'swarm', wrap);
        var b = el('div', 'chat-bubble', null, wrap);
        if (role === 'user') { b.textContent = String(t.content || ''); return; }
        b.classList.add('md'); b.dataset.md = String(t.content || ''); b.innerHTML = mdRender(String(t.content || ''));
        if (t.meta && typeof t.meta.ok !== 'undefined') el('div', 'chat-meta', 'agents: ' + t.meta.ok + '/' + t.meta.agents, wrap);
        var tk = (chatSession && chatSession.takes) ? chatSession.takes(t.id) : { index: 0, count: 1 };
        var actions = el('div', 'chat-actions', null, wrap);
        if (tk.count > 1) {
          var prev = el('button', 'chat-act', '\u25c0', actions); prev.title = 'Previous variant'; prev.disabled = chatBusy || tk.index <= 0; prev.onclick = function () { swipeTurn(t.id, -1); };
          el('span', 'chat-take', (tk.index + 1) + '/' + tk.count, actions);
          var nxt = el('button', 'chat-act', '\u25b6', actions); nxt.title = 'Next variant'; nxt.disabled = chatBusy || tk.index >= tk.count - 1; nxt.onclick = function () { swipeTurn(t.id, 1); };
        }
        var regen = el('button', 'chat-act', '\u21bb regenerate', actions); regen.title = 'Run the mission again for this turn (adds a variant)'; regen.disabled = chatBusy; regen.onclick = function () { regenTurn(t.id); };
      });
      if (thinking) {
        var tw = el('div', 'chat-msg assistant', null, log);
        el('div', 'chat-who', 'swarm', tw);
        var lb = el('div', 'chat-bubble', null, tw); lb.id = 'chat-live';
        lb.innerHTML = '<span class="spin"></span> running mission\u2026';
      }
      log.scrollTop = log.scrollHeight;
    }
    // run the existing swarm engine for one chat turn and return the synthesized reply text
    async function runMissionForTurn(text, context, onStream) {
      var myGen = ++runGen; teardown(); running = []; stopped = false;
      var nWorkers = parseInt($('workers').value, 10) || 3;
      var conc = parseInt($('conc').value, 10) || 2;
      var tools = currentTools(); lastToolset = tools;
      var basis = context ? (context + '\n\nUser: ' + text) : text;
      var subtasks = null;
      try { subtasks = await aiDecompose(basis, nWorkers); } catch (e) { subtasks = null; }
      if (!subtasks || !subtasks.length) subtasks = [ text ];
      clearCards(); subtasks.forEach(function (g, i) { makeCard(i, g); });   // scratch cards (hidden in chat) so serveOne works unchanged
      var results = [];
      try {
        var driver = deployLocalAgents(nWorkers);
        await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 40); });
        if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return { text: '', meta: null };
        var tasks = subtasks.map(function (g, i) { return { goal:g, idx:i, tools:tools }; });
        results = await driver.dispatchMany(tasks, { concurrency:conc, timeoutMs:TASK_TIMEOUT });
      } finally { teardown(); }
      if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return { text: '', meta: null };
      var final = '';
      try { final = await aggregate(results, text, true, onStream); } catch (e) { final = ''; }   // silent: synthesize without the batch agg panel, but stream into the chat bubble
      var nOk = results.filter(function (r) { return r && r.ok; }).length;
      return { text: final || '(the agents returned nothing usable)', meta: { agents: results.length, ok: nOk } };
    }
    async function submitTurn() {
      if (chatBusy) return;
      var ta = $('chat-input'); var text = (ta ? ta.value : '').trim(); if (!text) return;
      var s = ensureSession(); if (!s) { toast('error', 'chat is unavailable (weld.session missing)'); return; }
      if (ta) ta.value = '';
      s.addUser(text);
      setChatBusy(true);
      renderTranscript(true);
      var live = $('chat-live'), streaming = false;
      function onStream(textSoFar) {
        if (!live) return;
        if (!streaming) { streaming = true; live.classList.add('md'); }
        live.innerHTML = mdRender(textSoFar);
        var lg = $('chat-log'); if (lg) lg.scrollTop = lg.scrollHeight;
      }
      var reply;
      try { var ctx = await chatContext(s); reply = await runMissionForTurn(text, ctx, onStream); }
      catch (e) { reply = { text: '(the mission failed: ' + ((e && e.message) || e) + ')', meta: null }; }
      try { await s.addAssistant(reply.text, reply.meta || null); } catch (e) { try { s.addAssistant(reply.text); } catch (e2) {} }
      setChatBusy(false);
      renderTranscript(); saveChatSession();
    }
    function safeP(p) { try { if (p && typeof p.catch === 'function') p.catch(function () {}); } catch (e) {} return p; }
    function setChatBusy(on, label) {
      chatBusy = !!on;
      if ($('chat-send')) $('chat-send').disabled = !!on;
      if ($('chat-meter')) $('chat-meter').textContent = label || (on ? 'working\u2026' : 'ready');
    }
    function chatFileName(ext) { return (chatSessionName || 'conversation').replace(/[^\w.-]+/g, '_').slice(0, 40) + '.' + ext; }
    var saveChatSession = debounce(function () {
      try {
        if (!chatColl || !chatSession || !chatSession.serialize) return;
        var tl = chatSession.timeline ? chatSession.timeline() : [];
        if (!tl.length) return;
        if (!chatSessionId) chatSessionId = genSessionId();
        if (!chatSessionName) { var fu = null; for (var i = 0; i < tl.length; i++) { if (tl[i].role === 'user') { fu = tl[i]; break; } } chatSessionName = fu ? String(fu.content).slice(0, 48) : 'New conversation'; }
        safeP(chatColl.put({ id: chatSessionId, name: chatSessionName, data: chatSession.serialize(), turns: tl.length, updatedAt: Date.now() }));
        safeP(chatColl.put({ id: ACTIVE_PTR, sessionId: chatSessionId }));
        refreshSessionDropdown();
      } catch (e) {}
    }, 500);
    // regenerate an assistant turn: re-run the mission for its user turn as a NEW sibling variant
    async function regenTurn(turnId) {
      if (chatBusy || !chatSession) return;
      var tl = chatSession.timeline();
      var idx = -1; for (var k = 0; k < tl.length; k++) { if (tl[k].id === turnId) { idx = k; break; } }
      if (idx < 1) return;
      var userTurn = null; for (var i = idx - 1; i >= 0; i--) { if (tl[i].role === 'user') { userTurn = tl[i]; break; } }
      if (!userTurn) return;
      var uidx = tl.indexOf(userTurn);
      var ctx = await buildContext(tl.slice(0, uidx));
      setChatBusy(true, 'regenerating\u2026');
      if (chatSession.branchFrom) chatSession.branchFrom(userTurn.id);   // fork from the user turn -> next assistant is a sibling
      renderTranscript(true);
      var reply;
      try { reply = await runMissionForTurn(userTurn.content, ctx); }
      catch (e) { reply = { text: '(regeneration failed: ' + ((e && e.message) || e) + ')', meta: null }; }
      try { await chatSession.addAssistant(reply.text, reply.meta || null); } catch (e) { try { chatSession.addAssistant(reply.text); } catch (e2) {} }
      setChatBusy(false);
      renderTranscript(); saveChatSession();
    }
    function swipeTurn(turnId, dir) {
      if (chatBusy || !chatSession || !chatSession.swipe) return;
      chatSession.swipe(turnId, dir); renderTranscript(); saveChatSession();
    }
    async function listChatSessions() {
      if (!chatColl) return [];
      try { var all = await chatColl.getAll(); return all.filter(function (s) { return s.id !== ACTIVE_PTR; }).sort(function (a, b) { return (b.updatedAt || 0) - (a.updatedAt || 0); }); } catch (e) { return []; }
    }
    async function refreshSessionDropdown() {
      var sel = $('chat-sessions'); if (!sel) return;
      var all = await listChatSessions();
      sel.innerHTML = '';
      el('option', null, all.length ? 'switch conversation\u2026' : 'no saved conversations', sel).value = '';
      all.forEach(function (s) {
        var when = s.updatedAt ? new Date(s.updatedAt).toLocaleDateString() : '';
        var o = el('option', null, (s.name || 'untitled') + (when ? ('  \u00b7 ' + when) : ''), sel);
        o.value = s.id;
        if (s.id === chatSessionId) o.selected = true;
      });
    }
    function freshSession() { chatSession = (window.weld && window.weld.session && window.weld.session.create) ? window.weld.session.create({}) : null; return chatSession; }
    function newChatSession() {
      if (chatBusy) return;
      freshSession(); chatSessionId = null; chatSessionName = '';
      if (chatColl) safeP(chatColl.delete(ACTIVE_PTR));
      renderTranscript(); refreshSessionDropdown();
      if ($('chat-input')) $('chat-input').focus();
    }
    async function loadChatSession(id) {
      if (chatBusy || !chatColl || !id) return;
      try {
        var rec = await chatColl.get(id); if (!rec) return;
        freshSession(); if (chatSession && chatSession.load && rec.data) chatSession.load(rec.data);
        chatSessionId = rec.id; chatSessionName = rec.name || '';
        try { safeP(chatColl.put({ id: ACTIVE_PTR, sessionId: chatSessionId })); } catch (e) {}
        renderTranscript(); refreshSessionDropdown();
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    async function renameChatSession() {
      if (!chatSessionId || !chatColl) { toast('info', 'nothing to rename yet'); return; }
      var name;
      try { name = (window.weld.toast && window.weld.toast.prompt) ? await window.weld.toast.prompt({ title: 'Rename conversation', defaultValue: chatSessionName }) : window.prompt('Conversation name', chatSessionName); } catch (e) { name = null; }
      if (name == null) return;
      chatSessionName = String(name).slice(0, 60) || chatSessionName;
      try { var rec = await chatColl.get(chatSessionId); if (rec) { rec.name = chatSessionName; rec.updatedAt = Date.now(); await chatColl.put(rec); } } catch (e) {}
      refreshSessionDropdown();
    }
    async function deleteChatSession() {
      if (!chatSessionId || !chatColl) { newChatSession(); return; }
      var ok;
      try { ok = (window.weld.toast && window.weld.toast.confirm) ? await window.weld.toast.confirm({ title: 'Delete this conversation?', message: 'This cannot be undone.', danger: true, okLabel: 'Delete' }) : window.confirm('Delete this conversation?'); } catch (e) { ok = false; }
      if (!ok) return;
      try { await chatColl.delete(chatSessionId); } catch (e) {}
      newChatSession();
    }
    function downloadBlob(name, text, type) {
      try {
        var blob = new Blob([ text ], { type: type || 'text/plain' });
        var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob); var a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = url; a.download = name; document.body.appendChild(a); a.click(); document.body.removeChild(a);
        setTimeout(function () { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); }, 1000);
      } catch (e) { toast('error', 'export failed'); }
    }
    function chatExportMd() {
      var tl = (chatSession && chatSession.timeline) ? chatSession.timeline() : [];
      if (!tl.length) { toast('info', 'nothing to export'); return; }
      var lines = [ '# ' + (chatSessionName || 'Page conversation'), '' ];
      tl.forEach(function (t) {
        if (t.role === 'user') lines.push('**You:** ' + String(t.content || ''));
        else if (t.role === 'assistant') lines.push('**Swarm:** ' + String(t.content || ''));
        else return;
        lines.push('');
      });
      downloadBlob(chatFileName('md'), lines.join('\n'), 'text/markdown');
    }
    function chatExportJson() {
      if (!chatSession || !chatSession.serialize) { toast('info', 'nothing to export'); return; }
      var payload = { type: 'swarm-chat', name: chatSessionName || 'conversation', exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(), session: chatSession.serialize() };
      downloadBlob(chatFileName('json'), JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2), 'application/json');
    }
    async function restoreChatSession() {
      try {
        var lastId = null;
        if (chatColl) {
          try { var ptr = await chatColl.get(ACTIVE_PTR); lastId = ptr && ptr.sessionId; } catch (e) {}
          if (!lastId) { var all = await listChatSessions(); lastId = all.length ? all[0].id : null; }   // fall back to the most recent
          if (lastId) {
            var rec = await chatColl.get(lastId);
            if (rec && rec.data) { freshSession(); if (chatSession && chatSession.load) chatSession.load(rec.data); chatSessionId = rec.id; chatSessionName = rec.name || ''; renderTranscript(); }
          }
        }
        await refreshSessionDropdown();
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    try {
      window.__chat = {
        list: function () { return listChatSessions(); },
        activeId: function () { return chatSessionId; },
        dropMemory: function () { chatSession = null; chatSessionId = null; chatSessionName = ''; renderTranscript(); },   // simulate losing in-memory state (page reload)
        restore: function () { return restoreChatSession(); }
      };
    } catch (e) {}

    // build N worker agents + a driver over the in-page bus; shared by the batch run and chat turns
    function deployLocalAgents(nWorkers) {
      var bus = sharedBus();
      for (var i = 1; i <= nWorkers; i++) { var id = 'agent-' + i; var w = SW.create({ role:'worker', id:id, transport:bus(id), heartbeat:false }); w.serve(makeServe(id)); active.push(w); }
      var driver = SW.create({ role:'user', id:'driver', transport:bus('driver'), heartbeat:false }); active.push(driver);
      return driver;
    }
    async function runLocal() {
      var myGen = ++runGen;
      teardown(); running = []; stopped = false;
      await decompose();
      var subtasks = readTasks(); if (!subtasks.length) { feed('error', 'no subtasks -- set an objective'); return; }
      var nWorkers = parseInt($('workers').value, 10) || 3;
      var conc = parseInt($('conc').value, 10) || 2;
      var tools = currentTools(); lastToolset = tools;
      beginRun();
      clearCards(); subtasks.forEach(function (g, i) { makeCard(i, g); }); setMeter();
      runT0 = Date.now(); autopilot = makeAutopilot();
      meterPoll = null;
      try {
        var driver = deployLocalAgents(nWorkers);
        await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 40); });
        if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return;
        refreshPresence(driver);
        feed('start', 'deploying ' + subtasks.length + ' subtasks to ' + nWorkers + ' agents (parallel ' + conc + ')');
        var tasks = subtasks.map(function (g, i) { return { goal:g, idx:i, tools:tools }; });
        meterPoll = setInterval(setMeter, 300);
        var results = await driver.dispatchMany(tasks, { concurrency:conc, timeoutMs:TASK_TIMEOUT });
        if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return;
        clearInterval(meterPoll); meterPoll = null; setMeter();
        feed('final', 'collected ' + results.length + ' results');
        await aggregate(results);
        if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return;
        var nOk = results.filter(function (r) { return r && r.ok; }).length;
        if (nOk === results.length && nOk > 0) { toast('success', 'mission complete \u2014 ' + nOk + '/' + results.length + ' agents'); celebrate(); }
        else toast('info', 'mission done \u2014 ' + nOk + '/' + results.length + ' agents succeeded');
        refreshPresence(driver);
        saveRun($('goal').value.trim(), subtasks, results);
      } finally {
        if (meterPoll) { clearInterval(meterPoll); meterPoll = null; }
        if (myGen === runGen) setReady();
      }
    }

    // ---------- cross-tab roles (over the live bus / weld.sync) ----------
    var roleSwarm = null, pollTimer = null;
    async function startServing() {
      teardown(); running = []; stopped = false;
      startKeepAwake();
      roleSwarm = SW.create({ role:'worker', peerTTL:20000, heartbeatMs:2000 }); active.push(roleSwarm);
      roleSwarm.serve(makeServeRemote('node@' + roleSwarm.id.slice(-4)));
      $('role-tag').textContent = 'worker'; feed('start', 'serving as ' + roleSwarm.id + ' over ' + roleSwarm.transport);
      pollPresence(roleSwarm);
    }
    // remote serve: streams each crew step back to the requesting hub (so the hub shows a
    // live trace), and returns the final result. Also logs locally on this node's own feed.
    // batch a node's live generation tokens and stream them to the hub (so the User tab shows
    // text appearing in real time) without flooding the transport: flush every ~120ms or 160 chars.
    function hubTokens(hub, idx) {
      var buf = '', timer = null;
      function flush() { if (buf && hub) { try { roleSwarm.send(hub, 'token', { idx: idx, chunk: buf }); } catch (e) {} } buf = ''; if (timer) { clearTimeout(timer); timer = null; } }
      return { push: function (ch) { buf += ch; if (buf.length >= 160) flush(); else if (!timer) timer = setTimeout(flush, 120); }, done: flush };
    }
    function makeServeRemote(workerId) {
      return async function (payload, msg) {
        var hub = msg && msg.from;
        var toks = hubTokens(hub, payload.idx);
        feed('action', workerId + ' \u2190 ' + payload.goal);
        function shipImage(res, prompt) {                                          // ship the finished image to the hub
          feed('obs', workerId + ' generated image: ' + (prompt || ''));
          if (hub) { try { roleSwarm.send(hub, 'image', { idx:payload.idx, worker:workerId, dataUrl:shrinkDataUrl(res, 512), prompt:prompt }); } catch (e) {} }
        }
        function shipStep(s) {
          if (hub) { try { roleSwarm.send(hub, 'step', { idx:payload.idx, worker:workerId, step:compactStep(s) }); } catch (e) {} }
          if (s.type === 'final') feed('obs', workerId + ' \u2192 ' + s.answer);
        }
        var tools = payload.tools || { time:true };
        // image goal -> dedicated pipeline; steps + finished image stream to the hub
        if (caps.image && tools.image && isImageGoal(payload.goal)) {
          feed('info', workerId + ' image pipeline: describe \u2192 generate \u2192 report');
          var rp = await runImagePipeline(workerId, payload.idx, payload.goal, shipStep, shipImage);
          toks.done();
          return { worker:workerId, answer:rp.answer || rp.reason, ok:rp.ok, idx:payload.idx };
        }
        var crew = buildCrew(workerId, payload.idx, tools,
          function (ch) { toks.push(ch); },                                        // stream live tokens to the hub
          shipImage);
        running.push(crew);
        var out = await crew.run(payload.goal, { onStep: shipStep });
        var ans = out.ok ? cleanText(out.answer) : out.answer;
        if (out.ok && auditOn()) { feed('info', workerId + ' audit pass\u2026'); ans = await auditAnswer(payload.goal, ans); }
        toks.done();
        return { worker:workerId, answer: ans, ok:!!out.ok, idx:payload.idx };
      };
    }
    async function runUser() {
      var myGen = ++runGen;
      stopped = false; running = [];
      if (!roleSwarm) { roleSwarm = SW.create({ role:'user', peerTTL:20000, heartbeatMs:2000 }); active.push(roleSwarm); pollPresence(roleSwarm); await new Promise(function (r) { setTimeout(r, 300); }); }
      // route live steps + finished images streamed from remote nodes into the matching card (bind once)
      if (!roleSwarm.__stepBound) {
        roleSwarm.on('step', function (m) { var p = m && m.payload; if (!p || typeof p.idx !== 'number') return; if (p.worker) cardStatus(p.idx, 'running', p.worker); renderStep(p.idx, p.step, verbose()); });
        roleSwarm.on('token', function (m) { var p = m && m.payload; if (p && typeof p.idx === 'number' && p.chunk) liveToken(p.idx, p.chunk); });
        roleSwarm.on('image', function (m) { var p = m && m.payload; if (p && typeof p.idx === 'number' && p.dataUrl) cardImage(p.idx, p.dataUrl, p.prompt); });
        roleSwarm.__stepBound = true;
      }
      $('role-tag').textContent = 'user';
      await decompose();
      var subtasks = readTasks(); if (!subtasks.length) { feed('error', 'no subtasks'); return; }
      if (!roleSwarm.workers().length) { feed('error', 'no worker tabs found -- open this app in another tab, switch it to NODE, and Start serving'); return; }
      var conc = parseInt($('conc').value, 10) || 2; var tools = currentTools();
      beginRun();
      clearCards(); subtasks.forEach(function (g, i) { makeCard(i, g); cardStatus(i, 'running', 'remote'); });
      feed('start', 'dispatching ' + subtasks.length + ' subtasks to ' + roleSwarm.workers().length + ' node(s)');
      try {
        var tasks = subtasks.map(function (g, i) { return { goal:g, idx:i, tools:tools }; });
        var results = await roleSwarm.dispatchMany(tasks, { concurrency:conc, timeoutMs:TASK_TIMEOUT });
        if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return;
        results.forEach(function (r, i) { var ok = r && r.ok; cardStatus(i, ok ? 'done' : 'error', (r && r.worker) || 'remote'); cardResult(i, ok, ok ? r.answer : ('ERROR: ' + ((r && (r.reason || r.error)) || 'failed'))); });
        setMeter(); feed('final', 'collected ' + results.length + ' results');
        await aggregate(results);
        if (stopped || myGen !== runGen) return;
        var nOk = results.filter(function (r) { return r && r.ok; }).length;
        if (nOk === results.length && nOk > 0) { toast('success', 'mission complete \u2014 ' + nOk + '/' + results.length + ' agents'); celebrate(); }
        else toast('info', 'mission done \u2014 ' + nOk + '/' + results.length + ' agents succeeded');
        saveRun($('goal').value.trim(), subtasks, results);
      } finally {
        if (myGen === runGen) setReady();
      }
    }

    // ---------- presence ----------
    function refreshPresence(swarm) {
      var ps = swarm.peers(); $('peer-n').textContent = ps.length;
      if (!ps.length) { $('presence').innerHTML = '<div class="hint">No peers yet.</div>'; return; }
      $('presence').innerHTML = '';
      ps.forEach(function (p) {
        var d = document.createElement('div'); d.className = 'peer ' + p.role;
        var r = document.createElement('span'); r.className = 'role'; r.textContent = p.role;
        var id = document.createElement('span'); id.className = 'pid'; id.textContent = p.peerId;
        d.appendChild(r); d.appendChild(id); $('presence').appendChild(d);
      });
    }
    function pollPresence(swarm) { if (pollTimer) clearInterval(pollTimer); pollTimer = setInterval(function () { refreshPresence(swarm); }, 1000); }

    // ---------- run history (via skybridge storage: companion -> kv -> persist -> memory) ----------
    async function saveRun(goal, subtasks, results) {
      if (!sb || !sb.storage) return;
      var key = 'swarm:run:' + Date.now();
      try {
        await sb.storage.set(key, { goal:goal, subtasks:subtasks, results:results, at:Date.now() });
        await loadHistory();
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    async function loadHistory() {
      if (!sb || !sb.storage) return;
      try {
        var keys = await sb.storage.list('swarm:run:'); keys = (keys || []).sort().reverse().slice(0, 12);
        var sel = $('hist'); sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">recent runs (' + keys.length + ')\u2026</option>';
        keys.forEach(function (k) {
          var ts = parseInt(k.replace('swarm:run:', ''), 10);
          var o = document.createElement('option'); o.value = k;
          o.textContent = new Date(ts).toLocaleTimeString() + ' \u00b7 ' + (k);
          sel.appendChild(o);
        });
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    async function restoreRun(key) {
      if (!key || !sb || !sb.storage) return;
      try {
        var rec = await sb.storage.get(key); if (!rec) return;
        $('goal').value = rec.goal || ''; $('tasks').value = (rec.subtasks || []).join('\n'); syncTaskN();
        clearCards(); (rec.subtasks || []).forEach(function (g, i) { makeCard(i, g); var r = (rec.results || [])[i]; var ok = r && r.ok; cardStatus(i, ok ? 'done' : 'error', (r && r.worker) || '\u2014'); if (r) cardResult(i, ok, ok ? r.answer : ('ERROR: ' + ((r.reason || r.error) || ''))); }); setMeter();
        await aggregate(rec.results || []); feed('info', 'restored run ' + key);
      } catch (e) {}
    }

    // ---------- modes ----------
    var MODES = [ { id:'local', label:'Local' }, { id:'chat', label:'Chat' }, { id:'user', label:'Hub / User' }, { id:'worker', label:'Node / Worker' } ];
    var mode = 'local';
    function applyMode(m) {
      mode = m;
      var isWorker = (m === 'worker'), isChat = (m === 'chat');
      $('cfg-pool').style.display = (isWorker) ? 'none' : 'flex';
      $('cfg-tasks').style.display = (isWorker || isChat) ? 'none' : '';
      $('cfg-goal').style.display = (isWorker || isChat) ? 'none' : '';
      $('cfg-decomp').style.display = (isWorker) ? 'none' : '';
      $('cfg-tools').style.display = (isWorker) ? 'none' : '';
      $('go').style.display = (isWorker || isChat) ? 'none' : '';
      $('stop').style.display = (isWorker || isChat) ? 'none' : '';
      $('serve').style.display = (isWorker) ? '' : 'none';
      // worker-stage vs chat panel
      if ($('stage-hd')) $('stage-hd').style.display = isChat ? 'none' : '';
      $('cards').style.display = isChat ? 'none' : '';
      if (isChat && $('agg')) $('agg').style.display = 'none';
      if ($('chat-panel')) $('chat-panel').style.display = isChat ? '' : 'none';
      $('role-tag').textContent = isChat ? 'chat' : (m === 'local' ? 'local' : (m === 'user' ? 'user' : 'worker'));
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('#modes button'), function (b) { var on = b.getAttribute('data-m') === m; b.classList.toggle('active', on); b.setAttribute('aria-selected', on ? 'true' : 'false'); });
      teardown(); roleSwarm = null; if (pollTimer) { clearInterval(pollTimer); pollTimer = null; }
      stopKeepAwake();
      $('peer-n').textContent = '0'; $('presence').innerHTML = '<div class="hint">No peers yet.</div>';
      $('hint').textContent = isChat
        ? 'Chat mode: each message runs a full swarm mission and the synthesis becomes the reply. Worker count, tools, and decomposition above shape every turn.'
        : (m === 'local'
          ? 'All agents run in this tab over an in-page bus. Fully self-contained.'
          : (m === 'user' ? 'This tab dispatches to NODE tabs over ' + (caps.bus ? 'the companion bus (any generator)' : 'weld.sync (same-origin tabs)') + '. Open another tab as NODE and Start serving. Timed-out nodes are auto-reassigned.'
                          : 'This tab answers tasks from a HUB tab. Press Start serving (this also keeps the tab awake so Chrome will not freeze it in the background), then deploy from the hub.'));
      if (!isChat) emptyCards();
    }

    // ---------- wiring ----------
    function fillSelect(sel, arr) { arr.forEach(function (x, i) { var o = document.createElement('option'); o.value = String(i); o.textContent = x.label; sel.appendChild(o); }); sel.value = '0'; }
    var TOOLS = [ { id:'web', label:'web.fetch', on:false }, { id:'image', label:'image', on:false }, { id:'dice', label:'dice', on:true }, { id:'time', label:'time', on:true }, { id:'memory', label:'memory', on:true }, { id:'persona', label:'persona', on:false }, { id:'gen', label:'gen', on:false } ];

    function init() {
      if (!SW || !CR) { feed('error', 'weld.swarm or weld.crew not loaded -- check the generator imports + that the host script calls root.weldSwarm()'); }
      // mode tabs
      $('modes').setAttribute('role', 'tablist'); $('modes').setAttribute('aria-label', 'Run mode');
      MODES.forEach(function (m) { var b = document.createElement('button'); b.textContent = m.label; b.setAttribute('data-m', m.id); b.setAttribute('role', 'tab'); b.onclick = function () { applyMode(m.id); }; $('modes').appendChild(b); });
      // ---- accessibility: label the controls a screen reader would otherwise read as bare text ----
      var ARIA = { 'go':'Deploy swarm', 'stop':'Stop run', 'import':'Import setup from file', 'export-setup':'Export setup', 'share-link':'Copy a shareable link', 'diag':'Copy diagnostics', 'data':'How your data is handled', 'feed-clear':'Clear activity log', 'img-cfg-btn':'Image defaults', 'agg-copy':'Copy synthesis', 'agg-export':'Export synthesis as Markdown', 'agg-export-json':'Export run as JSON', 'theme':'Toggle dark mode', 'verbose':'Toggle raw model input/output' };
      Object.keys(ARIA).forEach(function (id) { var el = $(id); if (el) el.setAttribute('aria-label', ARIA[id]); });
      var im = $('img-modal'); if (im) { im.setAttribute('role', 'dialog'); im.setAttribute('aria-modal', 'true'); im.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Image defaults'); }
      // ---- keyboard shortcuts: Cmd/Ctrl+Enter = deploy or stop; Esc = close modal or stop ----
      document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape') { if (im && im.style.display === 'flex') { closeImgModal(); } else if ($('priv-modal') && $('priv-modal').style.display === 'flex') { closeDataModal(); } else if ($('stop') && !$('stop').disabled) { stopAll(); } return; }
        if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'Enter') { e.preventDefault(); if ($('go') && !$('go').disabled) $('go').click(); else if ($('stop') && !$('stop').disabled) $('stop').click(); }
      });
      $('theme').onclick = toggleTheme;
      // decomposition + tools
      fillSelect($('decomp'), DECOMP);
      TOOLS.forEach(function (t) { var b = document.createElement('span'); b.className = 'tg' + (t.on ? ' on' : ''); b.setAttribute('data-tool', t.id); b.textContent = t.label; b.onclick = function () { b.classList.toggle('on'); }; $('tools').appendChild(b); });
      // sliders + inputs (debounced persistence so typing doesn't slam the db)
      $('workers').oninput = function () { $('workers-v').textContent = $('workers').value; saveDraft(); };
      $('conc').oninput = function () { $('conc-v').textContent = $('conc').value; saveDraft(); };
      $('tasks').oninput = function () { syncTaskN(); saveDraft(); };
      $('goal').oninput = saveDraft;
      $('decomp').onchange = function () { if (DECOMP[parseInt($('decomp').value, 10)].id !== 'manual') decompose(); saveDraft(); };
      // actions
      $('go').onclick = function () { autoEnableImage(); t0 = Date.now(); $('feed').innerHTML = ''; if (mode === 'local') runLocal(); else runUser(); };
      $('serve').onclick = function () { t0 = Date.now(); $('feed').innerHTML = ''; startServing(); };
      $('stop').onclick = stopAll;
      $('feed-clear').onclick = function () { $('feed').innerHTML = ''; };
      $('diag').onclick = copyDiagnostics;
      $('share-link').onclick = shareLink;
      if ($('chat-send')) $('chat-send').onclick = submitTurn;
      if ($('chat-input')) $('chat-input').addEventListener('keydown', function (e) { if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); submitTurn(); } });
      if ($('chat-sessions')) $('chat-sessions').onchange = function () { if (this.value) loadChatSession(this.value); };
      if ($('chat-new')) $('chat-new').onclick = newChatSession;
      if ($('chat-rename')) $('chat-rename').onclick = renameChatSession;
      if ($('chat-del')) $('chat-del').onclick = deleteChatSession;
      if ($('chat-export-md')) $('chat-export-md').onclick = chatExportMd;
      if ($('chat-export-json')) $('chat-export-json').onclick = chatExportJson;
      try { window.__shareCodec = { encode: encodeShare, decode: decodeShare, unwrap: unwrapEnvelope }; } catch (e) {}   // harness hook
      try { window.__auditAnswer = auditAnswer; } catch (e) {}   // harness hook
      registerPrivacy();
      $('data').onclick = openDataModal;
      $('priv-modal-x').onclick = closeDataModal; $('priv-ok').onclick = closeDataModal;
      $('priv-modal').onclick = function (e) { if (e.target === $('priv-modal')) closeDataModal(); };
      $('verbose').onclick = function () { $('verbose').classList.toggle('on'); };
      $('hist').onchange = function () { restoreRun($('hist').value); };
      $('agg-copy').onclick = function () { try { navigator.clipboard.writeText($('agg-body').textContent); $('agg-copy').textContent = 'copied'; setTimeout(function () { $('agg-copy').textContent = 'copy'; }, 1200); } catch (e) {} };
      $('agg-export').onclick = exportMd;
      $('agg-export-json').onclick = exportJson;
      $('export-setup').onclick = exportJson;   // settings + inputs snapshot (works before a run too)
      $('import').onclick = function () { $('importfile').value = ''; $('importfile').click(); };
      $('importfile').onchange = function (e) { importFile(e.target.files && e.target.files[0]); };
      // image-defaults popup
      imgStyleOptions();
      $('img-cfg-btn').onclick = openImgModal;
      $('img-modal-x').onclick = closeImgModal;
      $('img-modal').onclick = function (e) { if (e.target === $('img-modal')) closeImgModal(); };
      $('img-g').oninput = function () { $('img-g-v').textContent = (+$('img-g').value) ? $('img-g').value : 'default'; };
      $('img-save').onclick = function () { readImgCfgUI(); saveDraft(); closeImgModal(); feed('info', 'image defaults saved'); };
      applyMode('local');
      try { if (window.weld && window.weld.tokens && window.weld.tokens.preload) window.weld.tokens.preload().catch(function () {}); } catch (e) {}   // warm the tokenizer; estimate fallback if it can't load
      refreshQuota(true);   // storage-usage line for diag + one-time near-full warning
      if (sb && typeof sb.onConnect === 'function') sb.onConnect(function () { probe(); applyMode(mode); });
      (async function () {
        await probe();
        var had = await restoreDraft();   // restore saved objective/subtasks, or seed an example
        if (!had && !$('goal').value) $('goal').value = 'Plan a three-stop street-food tour of a fictional harbor city, one stop per agent.';
        await maybeImportFromHash();       // a #swarm=... link overrides the draft with the shared setup
        await restoreChatSession();        // bring back the last chat conversation if any
        await loadHistory();
      })();
    }
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init); else init();
  })();
</script>
